Golfin

Welcome to the Golfin team space!

Mission

GOLFIN aims to establish a new economic sphere by fusing the real (golf) and digital (games) world, complementing the

challenges of both, and creating synergy. GOLFIN's mission is also to contribute to people's health by increasing the number of

golfers and increasing opportunities to experience nature and exercise.

Golfin Project Walkthrough

Golfin Project Walkthrough

By Zachary Kilmer                                                                                                               Last Edited

5/29/2024

Golfin Project

Project Basics:

Engine: Unity

Version: 2022.3.29f1

Language: C#

Project Goals:

Alpha Build:

A playable game for the users. Which includes smooth controls, smooth ball movement, able to

putt in hole easily and simple camera movements. Refer to Game Mechanics document for more

info. (Alpha Release Plan Document)

Final Build:

The finished game should include various modes such as Story, PVP Tournaments, and

Challenges. Gameplay will be intermixed with featured customizable options for the player

including, Player Character, NFT and non-NFT items such as Clubs, Balls, and more. Reference

to Game Design Document for more info.

Onboarding Process:

Step 1: Setting Up Your Workstation

Setting up your workstation includes signing into the assigned station and performing setup if

necessary. Installing/Changing the workstations language. Downloading your preferred browser

and signing into your @wonderwall-g.com email account. Once into your email you need to

accept the invitation to the team's Jira project. If you do not see an invite stop and ask your

supervisor.

Step 2: Review Jira Documentation

15



Once on Jira go to the top left menu and open Confluence. Found in the Onboarding section of

the Jira Confluence will be this document and other onboarding documents. Review these

documents and familiarize yourself with both the project and Jira. Once complete, review the 

Game Design Document as well as the Project Guidelines Documentation. After reviewing these

documents please review anything related to your role that is present on the Jira Confluence or

dashboard.

Step 3: Tasks and Work

Once documentation has been reviewed please return to the original Jira board and look at the

current sprints tasks. See if there has been any work assigned to you and ask any questions you

may have regarding the tasks. If no work has been assigned to you, speak with your supervisor

about your role and inform them that you are ready to start your duties.

Document Access:

16



Jira Walkthrough

Jira Walkthrough

By Carson Griffin

Step by Step Guide to Jira

What is Jira?

Jira is a widely used project management and issue tracking software developed by Atlassian. 

Designed to help teams organize and keep track of their work, manage individual tasks, track

bugs and issues, and collaborate better on projects.  Jira is extremely flexible with customizable

workflows, agile project management, reporting and analytics, and integration with different

online tools.  It’s commonly used in software development such as websites, IT operations,

project management, and game development.  

Planning Segment (Found on the left of the screen)

Roadmap:

1. Timeline View: 

a. The roadmap is presented in a timeline format, typically divided into quarters or specific

timeframes. It provides a visual representation of how features and tasks are planned over

time.

2. Epics and Initiatives:

a.  Epics represent larger bodies of work or projects, while initiatives encompass multiple

epics or themes. The roadmap allows you to organize and track progress on these epics

and initiatives.

3. Drag-and-Drop Functionality:

a. Jira's roadmap allows you to easily rearrange and prioritize items by dragging and dropping

them on the timeline. This flexibility enables teams to adjust plans based on changing

priorities or resource availability.

17



4. Status Tracking:

a. The roadmap indicates the current status of each item, whether it's in progress, completed,

or yet to be started. This helps teams monitor the progress of their initiatives and provides

stakeholders with visibility into the overall project status.

5. Collaboration and Sharing:

a.  Jira's roadmap can be shared with team members, stakeholders, and clients, fostering

collaboration and alignment. It ensures that everyone involved in the project has a clear

understanding of the planned roadmap and can provide input or feedback.

Overall: 

Jira's roadmap feature is a powerful tool for project planning, providing teams with a visual

representation of their project's direction and helping them prioritize and communicate their

plans effectively.

Backlogs:

Overview:  

Jira's backlog section is a key component of the software's project management functionality.

It is a centralized space where teams can capture, organize, and prioritize their work items or

tasks. The backlog represents a repository of all the work that needs to be completed, serving

as a dynamic to-do list for the team.

1. User Stories and Tasks: 

a. The backlog consists of user stories, which describe the functionality or requirements from

a user's perspective, and tasks, which are the specific actions needed to complete those

user stories. These items are created and added to the backlog by the team or product

owner.

2. Prioritization:

a. The backlog allows teams to prioritize their work items based on factors such as business

value, urgency, dependencies, or customer needs. The most important and high-priority

items are typically placed at the top of the backlog.

3. Estimation and Sizing: 

a. Work items in the backlog can be estimated or sized to provide an understanding of their

effort or complexity. This helps with capacity planning and determining how much work can

be taken up in a given time period.

18



4. Backlog Grooming:

a. Regular backlog grooming sessions are conducted to review, refine, and update the items in

the backlog. This includes breaking down larger user stories into smaller, actionable tasks,

clarifying requirements, and ensuring that the backlog is up to date and relevant.

5. Sprint Planning:

a. From the backlog, teams select a set of work items to be completed in a sprint during the

sprint planning phase. The backlog serves as a source from which the team pulls items into

the sprint based on their priority and capacity.

6. Collaboration and Visibility:

a.  Jira's backlog section allows team members, stakeholders, and product owners to

collaborate, discuss, and provide input on the work items. It provides transparency and

visibility into the planned work, allowing everyone involved to understand the team's

progress and priorities.

Overall:

Jira's backlog section is a central hub for managing and organizing the team's work items,

ensuring that the most important tasks are prioritized and ready for execution. It facilitates

effective planning, collaboration, and progress tracking throughout the project lifecycle.

Board:

Overview:

Jira's board section is a powerful feature that helps teams visualize and track their work items

in an agile or Kanban-style project management approach. It provides a visual representation

of the team's workflow and allows for efficient task management and collaboration.

1. Board Types: 

a. Jira offers different types of boards, including Scrum boards and Kanban boards. Scrum

boards are used for managing work in sprints, while Kanban boards provide a continuous

flow of work items.

2. Columns and Swimlanes: 

a. Boards are typically organized into columns representing different stages of the workflow,

such as "To Do," "In Progress," and "Done." Swimlanes can be used to further categorize or

group work items based on specific criteria, such as assignees, priorities, or issue types.

3. Drag-and-Drop Functionality:

a. One of the key features of Jira's board section is the ability to easily move work items

between columns using drag-and-drop functionality. This allows for quick status updates

19



and progress tracking.

4. Work in Progress (WIP) Limits:

a. Teams can set limits on the number of work items allowed in each column to manage their

workflow and prevent bottlenecks. WIP limits help teams maintain a steady pace of work

and encourage collaboration.

5. Quick Filters and Search:

a. Boards provide quick filter options to narrow down the view based on specific criteria, such

as assignees, labels, or issue types. Additionally, search functionality allows users to find

specific work items within the board.

6. Collaboration:

a. Jira's board section promotes collaboration by allowing team members to leave comments,

attach files, and mention other team members on work items. This fosters effective

communication and keeps everyone on the same page.

7. Customization Options:

a. Jira's boards can be customized to fit the team's specific needs. Users can add custom

columns, configure board settings, apply filters, and create board-specific workflows to

align with their unique processes.

Overall:

Jira's board section provides a visual and interactive platform for teams to manage their work

items, track progress, and collaborate effectively. It offers flexibility and customization options

to adapt to different project management approaches and workflows.

Development and Code Category

Dev and Code

Overview:

Jira's Development and Code section, also known as the Development panel or Development

Tools Integration (DTI), is a feature that integrates with various development and code

management tools to enhance collaboration between development teams and project

management.

20



1. Code Repository Integration: 

a.  Jira can be integrated with popular code hosting platforms like GitHub, Bitbucket, or

GitLab. This integration allows developers to link their code repositories directly to Jira

issues, enabling seamless tracking of code changes and providing visibility into

development progress.

2. Development Information in Issues:

a. With the integration in place, Jira issues can display relevant development information such

as commits, branches, pull requests, and code reviews associated with a particular issue.

This helps stakeholders and team members understand the code changes related to a

specific task or bug.

3. Seamless Workflows: 

a. The Development panel allows developers to transition issues directly from Jira to their

preferred development tools without leaving the Jira interface. This ensures smooth

collaboration between development and project management teams, as they can work in

their respective environments while staying connected.

4. Code Reviews:

a. The Development and Code section often includes features for code reviews and

collaboration. It may support integrations with code review tools like Crucible or provide

inline commenting and discussion capabilities to facilitate effective code collaboration

among team members.

5. Traceability and Visibility:

a. Integrating development tools with Jira provides traceability between code changes and

project requirements or issues. It enables stakeholders to understand the status and

progress of development tasks, review code changes, and gain visibility into the

development process.

6. Automation and Notifications: 

a. Jira's Development and Code section can be configured to trigger automated actions or

notifications based on certain code events or changes. For example, notifications can be

sent when a pull request is created, reviewed, or merged, keeping team members informed

about code updates and progress.

Overall: 

Jira's Development and Code section bridges the gap between project management and

software development by integrating code repositories and development tools. It enhances

collaboration, provides traceability, and streamlines workflows, allowing teams to effectively

manage their code and development processes within the broader context of their projects.

21



Proeject Pages

Project Pages information:

Overview: 

Jira's project pages are dedicated spaces within the software where teams can manage and

organize their projects. They serve as centralized hubs for collaboration, tracking progress,

and accessing project-related information. Each project in Jira has its own project page,

which can be customized to fit the specific needs of the team and project.

1. Project Overview: 

a. The project page provides an overview of the project, including project name, key details,

and a summary of its progress. It serves as a central point of reference for team members

and stakeholders to understand the project's scope, objectives, and current status.

2. Issue Tracking and Management:

a. Jira's project pages allow teams to create, track, and manage issues or tasks related to the

project. Issues can be categorized, prioritized, assigned to team members, and updated

with relevant information, such as status, due dates, and attachments. The project page

provides visibility into the overall issue status and progress.

3. Project Boards:

a.  Project pages often include project boards, such as Scrum or Kanban boards, which

visualize the project's workflow and help teams track the progress of their work items.

Boards provide a visual representation of tasks, their statuses, and can be customized to fit

the team's preferred workflow.

4. Project Documentation:

a. Teams can leverage the project page to store project documentation, guidelines, and other

resources in a centralized manner. This allows team members to access important project-

related information, collaborate on documentation, and maintain a knowledge base for

future reference.

5. Reporting and Analytics:

a. Jira's project pages offer reporting and analytics features that provide insights into project

metrics, such as issue progress, team velocity, and performance trends. This helps teams

track their progress, identify bottlenecks, and make data-driven decisions to improve

project outcomes.

22



6. Collaboration and Communication: 

a.  Project pages facilitate collaboration among team members and stakeholders. They often

include features for commenting, mentioning team members, and sharing updates or

discussions related to specific issues or tasks. This promotes effective communication and

keeps everyone aligned.

7. Customization and Integration:

a. Jira's project pages can be customized to meet the unique requirements of the team and

project. Users can configure project settings, customize fields and workflows, and integrate

with other tools or plugins to extend functionality and enhance project management

processes.

Overview:

Jira's project pages provide a comprehensive platform for teams to manage their projects,

track progress, collaborate effectively, and access project-related information. They offer

flexibility, customization options, and integration capabilities to cater to different project

management methodologies and workflows.

Creating Backlogs

Step-by-Step Walkthrough

Overview:

Creating a backlog in Jira involves a series of steps that allow you to define, prioritize, and

organize the work items for your project. Here's a guide on how to make a backlog in Jira:

1. Access Jira:

a. Log in to your Jira account and navigate to the desired project for which you want to create

a backlog.

2. Enable Backlog: 

a. Ensure that the Agile board is enabled for your project. If not, go to the project settings and

enable Agile board or create a new one.

3. Access the Backlog: 

23



a. Once the Agile board is enabled, go to the board view by selecting the "Boards" option

from the main Jira navigation menu and choosing the appropriate board for your project.

4. Navigate to the Backlog View:

a. In the board view, you'll see different tabs, such as "Backlog," "Active Sprints," and

"Reports." Click on the "Backlog" tab to access the backlog view.

5. Creating Issues: 

a.  In the backlog view, you can start creating issues or work items by selecting the "Create"

button or using the shortcut key "C." Fill in the required details such as summary,

description, and assignees. You can also add labels, attachments, and set the issue type,

priority, and other relevant fields.

6. Add Issues to the Backlog:

a. As you create issues, they will appear in the backlog. Drag and drop the issues to reorder

them based on their priority. Higher priority issues should typically be placed at the top of

the backlog.

7. Organize Backlog with Epics and Versions (Optional):

a. If your project requires further organization, you can use epics and versions. Epics help

group related issues together, while versions represent specific milestones or releases.

You can create epics and 

8. Define Issue Details: 

a. Click on an issue in the backlog to open its details. Here, you can add more information,

set due dates, estimate effort, link related issues, and add any other necessary details.

9. Prioritize Backlog Items:

a. To prioritize the backlog items, you can use Jira's default priority field or create custom

fields specific to your project's needs. Assign priority values to each issue based on its

importance and urgency.

10. Refine Backog:

a. Regularly review and refine your backlog. As you gain more insights or receive feedback,

you may need to add, remove, or reprioritize issues to ensure the backlog accurately

reflects the project's requirements.

24



Creating Stories

Story Making:

1. Click on "Create" or "C" in Backlogs:

a. In the backlog view, click on the "Create" button or use the shortcut key "C" to initiate the

creation of a new issue.

2. Select issue Type:

a. In the issue creation dialog, you'll see a list of available issue types. Select the appropriate

type for user stories, which is typically "Story" or "User Story." If you don't see these

options, consult your Jira administrator to ensure that the appropriate issue types are

configured for your project

3. Provide Details: 

a. Fill in the necessary details for the user story. At a minimum, include the story summary and

description. The summary should provide a concise title for the user story, while the

description should provide more detailed information about the user story's purpose,

requirements, and acceptance criteria.

4. Assign the Story:

a. Assign the user story to the appropriate team member who will be responsible for its

completion. You can select the assignee from the "Assignee" field in the issue creation

dialog.

5. Add Labels, Components, and Epics (optional):

a.  Depending on your project's requirements, you can add labels, components, and epics to

further categorize and organize the user stories. Labels and components can help with

filtering and searching, while epics can be used to group related user stories together.

6. Set the Story Points (Optional):

a. If your team uses story points for estimating the effort required to complete user stories,

you can set the story points for each story. The "Story Points" field is typically a custom

field that needs to be configured for your project.

7. Save the User Story:

a. Once you have provided all the necessary details, click the "Create" button to save the user

story. The user story will now be added to the backlog and can be prioritized, assigned to

sprints, and worked on by the team.

8. Refine and Update User Stories; 

a.  User stories often undergo refinement and updates as the project progresses. You can edit

the user stories to add more details, update the status, modify acceptance criteria, or make

25



any other necessary changes. Simply open the user story and click the "Edit" button to

make updates.

Creating a Task/ Child Issue

Creatng a task:

1. Open the User Story:

a.  Locate the user story for which you want to create tasks. You can find the user story in the

backlog, active sprint, or any other board view where it is visible. Click on the user story to

open its details.

2. Navigate to the “Issue Detail” View: 

a.  In the user story's detail view, you'll see various tabs such as "Details," "Comments,"

"Activity," and more. Ensure you are in the "Details" tab, which is usually the default view.

3. Creat a Task: 

a. To create a task, scroll down to the "Issue Detail" view and find the "Issue Links" section.

Click on the "Create" button located next to the "Linked Issues" field.

4. Select Task as the Issue Type:

a. In the "Create Issue" dialog that appears, select the appropriate issue type for tasks, which

is typically "Task" or "Sub-task." Choose the relevant option from the issue type dropdown.

i. Note that is may be called “Child Issue” for some people

5. Provide Task Details: 

a. Fill in the necessary details for the task. Give the task a summary, provide a detailed

description, and set the assignee. You can also add labels, components, and set other

relevant fields as needed.

6. Link Task to User Story:

a. In the "Issue Links" section of the task creation dialog, make sure to link the task to the

user story. Select the appropriate link type, which is typically "Relates to" or "is parent of,"

and search for the user story to link it.

7. Save the Task: 

a. Once you have provided all the necessary details, click the "Create" button to save the task.

The task will now be linked to the user story.

8. Repeat for Additional Tasks:

26



a. If there are multiple tasks associated with the user story, repeat steps 4-8 to create each

task. You can create as many tasks as needed to break down the work required to

complete the user story.

9. Update Task Status:

a. Once the tasks are created, you can update their status, assignees, and other details as the

work progresses. Open each task individually and make the necessary updates.

Overall:

By creating tasks under user stories, you can break down the work into smaller, manageable

units and track the progress of each task. This approach allows for better visibility and

collaboration within the team, facilitating the completion of user stories in an organized

manner.

27



Plastic SCM Walkthrough

By: Zoë Campos

What is Plastic SCM? 

Plastic SCM was acquired by Unity DevOps as a tool specifically for game development.

Providing users with access to Version Control, Build Automation, and more. For the purposes of

this project, Version Control is the main focus of this software.

Why Use Version Control?

Long gone are the days of unfixable build errors. When working with a team, efficient workflows

are essential. Version control allows clear communication on changes made by each user for the

project. After creating tasks in Jira, users should create a branch for each task, as it is good

practice. Then, users are able to develop/make changes to these tasks without affecting the

integrity of the project. This allows developers to be able to test other branches as well. The

trunk of the repository is main. Each branch that is created will eventually be merged back to

main. Peer revisions are essential, thus each branch allows testing from any user within the

team. Once completed, the branch can be merged back to the main branch.

As a programmer, most likely you will only be making pull requests from the Gameplay Branch at

first to get comfortable with the pulling process. Once this process is mastered, the work

completed within the engine will be pushed onto a branch related to the completed task. Refer

to the Figma Workflow Chart for more in depth information on the development process. 

Application Setup / How to Access the Workspace

First, download the most current version of Plastic SCM Cloud Edition for Windows. Connect

your Unity account (link documentation to how to create Unity account) with Plastic SCM. Once

the setup is complete, open the software. An invitation is required to access the workspace,

which will be provided by the supervisor. Once connected, open the software and a repo titled

“Golfin”, will appear on the homepage. Then select the blue button titled “Download repository”.

28



Be sure to download the repository onto a folder within File Explorer that is easily accessible, as

your work will be stored in this folder. 

Add Ignore Private Files

In order to avoid compiler errors when adding the project to Unity, you must have a ignore.conf

file. This can be found within the Golfin folder. Copy and paste the ignore.conf outside the Golfin

folder. 

How To Pull Current Version of Project

Now it is time to add the project from the disk to Unity Hub. Select Add Project, and select the

Golfin Project. Yay! You now are connected to the cloud, and can access the current version of

whichever branch you are working off of. Communicate with your supervisor which branch you

will be working on. The last thing you want is to cause merge conflicts for the team, as they are

working hard!

Troubleshooting

Most likely, there will be troubleshooting required as there are inevitable bumps when first

connecting your Unity Hub to the Plastic SCM cloud. There are a few options to troubleshoot

any compiler errors when opening the project in Unity:

1. Download the most current version of Git. Sometimes, the project requires your device to

have a git.exe file to work properly. 

2. Visit the Plastic SCM Manual. This manual is written by the engineers behind this software,

and they have the most current information on how to navigate through any potential bumps.

Navigate to the section you are having trouble with, and dive in from there.  

3. If you are able to make it inside the Unity project, but there are multiple errors, be sure the

right packages are installed. Head to Window > Project Manager > Packages (In Project).

Here, ensure the proper packages are installed in your version. 

4. In the event that you download Git and are receiving an error (as seen below) that Git is not

found/recognized, here are some steps to follow:  

29



In Git Bash type git --version  to confirm Git is recognized. If it is downloaded

correctly, the output should look like this: 

Head over to System Properties on Window settings. Type Env into the Window search bar,

and select the top result. Under the Advanced tab, click on Environment Variables and

ensure Git is set as a variable within the list. Click on Path under the system variables, and

add the directories for both the Git bin folder and Git cmd folder. Be sure to add \git.exe at

the end of these variables. Be sure to apply these changes, and restart your computer

before opening Unity again. 

If there are still problems, remove the packages completely from the Package Manager. Be

sure to write down the name of the package. In my case, the VContainer package and the

Unitask package was having trouble being recognized. Begin by removing both the

corrupted packages. Copy the link where the package was downloaded from. From there,

restart your computer and close all Unity and Plastic tabs. After restarting, re-add the link of

30



the packager by going to Window > Package Manager > Click the Plus Button > Add

Package from git URL, and paste the URL. This solved my compilation errors, and allowed

both correct packages to be added into the project.

Remember, there are bound to be bumps in the road; be sure to ask questions and communicate

with your supervisor for support. This is a team project, meaning there are always people to

support you through any hardships!

AI Usage Guideline

The EU has enacted an AI regulation law, which will take effect in 2026. According to the AI

Act, any content created by AI must be clearly labeled as "AI-generated" before being released

externally. Violations of this requirement will result in severe penalties. The use of generative AI

within companies is permitted, however, it should be used as a reference or with additional

editing and revisions.

New article

https://www.europarl.europa.eu/news/en/press-room/20240308IPR19015/artificial-intelligence-

act-meps-adopt-landmark-law

https://www3.nhk.or.jp/news/html/20240521/k10014456551000.html

Jira recommended practices

Listing recommended practices for Jira tickets

 Links to files

Case 1: Leaving a link in a comment:

When posting a comment for someone to review:

1. Add a title to the link

2. Then add the link

3. A screenshot (low res) can be added to help locate the file/understanding the context better

Example:

Case 2: Closing the Jira ticket “Done”:

When the ticket is closed, nobody wants to revisit it later and waste time looking at all the

threads to find the relevant links.

Therefore, ask yourself the question: If I need to come back later, is there a link that would help

me?

If the answer is YES:

Photoshop Sprite export automatization

Note: Need updating as scripts are now catering for both the game and Marketplace

I created an automatic script for Photoshop.

It can export a sprite automatically in 4 different sizes

The final sprites will have different name extensions reflecting the sprite size

Here: 1600x1600, 1200x1200, 1080x1080 and 512x512 px

Note: The process is slightly different between PC and Mac

Tickets File “S_Marketplace_Gacha_Ticket_Gold.psd” (Can be any other items) :

S_Marketplace_Gacha_Ticket_Gold.psd

Script PC:

exportPngPc.jsx

Script Mac:

exportPngMac.jsx

Need:

+ Use an original item file 1600x1600 (Club, CHaracter, item, ball, ticket, etc)

+ The item exported name must be the “root” final name: eg:

S_Marketplace_Gacha_Ticket_Gold (Ask management and dev for final name)

The script will add automatically the extensions “_1600”, “_1200”, “_1080” and “_512”

eg: The final export files will become: S_Marketplace_Gacha_Ticket_Gold_1200

+ For PC: Create a folder named “export” in root c drive

+ For Mac: Create a folder named “export” in the download folder

+ For Mac: you need to make a path name change in the script file

Open “exportPngMac.jsx” in a plain text editor software

At the bottom look for:

saveToPNG("_1600","/Users/Username/Downloads/export/"); // Username is the computer

username doh!!!

42



resizeToPixels(1200, 1200); // Resizing to 1200x1200

saveToPNG("_1200","/Users/Username/Downloads/export/"); // Exporting 1200

resizeToPixels(1080, 1080); // Resizing to 1080x1080

saveToPNG("_1080","/Users/Username/Downloads/export/"); // Exporting 1080 

resizeToPixels(512, 512); // Resizing to 512x512

saveToPNG("_512","/Users/Username/Downloads/export/"); // Exporting 512 

Replace all “Username” by your computer username

Save the file “exportPngMac.jsx”

Close it

+ Open Photoshop

+ Open desired item sprite (1600x1600px)

+ Run the script “exportPng.jsx” from File/Scripts/Browse 

(Note the script could be embed in Photoshop and called with an action/keypad shortcut)

+ For PC the output files will be in the “C:\export” folder

+ For Mac the output files will be in the “Downloads/export” folder

Intro

risako@wonderwall-g.com

Thanks

Remote Work

The following rules for remote work will be standardized going forward:

【Conditions】

Remote work will be permitted up to two times per month.

Excluded days include the first workday of the month, the last workday of the month, and the

days around long weekends (3 consecutive days or more).

Remote work for two consecutive business days is not allowed.

57



【Remote Work Procedure】

The schedule for remote work must be added to Google Calendar by the day before the

planned remote work day.

The start time for the workday must be added to the calendar to ensure it is visible to team

members.

The remote work status must be reported in the daily report the day before the planned

remote work day.

On the remote work day, attendance must be recorded in the timesheet at both the start and

end of the workday.

【Important Notes】

＊Failure to comply with remote work rules may result in immediate revocation of

remote work privileges without warning.

＊Remote work may not be permitted during events requiring team collaboration.

＊Remote work arrangements may be discontinued at any time at owner(komatsu-

san)'s discretion

＊Unless under exceptional circumstances, no arrangements outside these rules will

be permitted.

(Annual leave should be used. For members not yet eligible for annual leave, cases will

be reviewed based on individual circumstances)

今後、リモート勤務のルールを以下の通り統一します。

【条件】

１ヶ月のうち2回までリモート勤務を許可する
除外日は月初の勤務日、月末最終勤務日、3連休以上の休日の前後

2営業日連続のリモート勤務は認めない

【リモート勤務時のフロー】

リモート勤務予定日前日までにGoogleカレンダーに予定を入力する
カレンダーに勤務開始予定時間を必ず入力し、メンバーが把握できるようにする

58



リモート勤務予定日前日の日報にてリモート勤務の旨を報告をする
リモート勤務当日は勤務開始時点、終了時点で勤怠表に必ず入力する

【注意点】

＊リモート勤務のルールを守れない場合は警告なしで当該メンバーはリモート禁止するこ

とがある

＊イベントなど皆の協力が必要な場合はリモートを認めない場合がある

＊今後、オーナー判断でリモート勤務がなくなる可能性もある

＊やむを得ない場合を除き、このルール以外のことは認めない

　（基本的に有給休暇を使う。有給休暇がまだ付与されていないメンバーは理由により検

討する）

⇨　Subject to deductions

       ⇨　1 day of leave to do residential related matters

Track Starting and Finishing times in 15-minute increments

Compensatory work (eg: swap Saturday for Tuesday)

Missing information about process to request a compensatory day (Swap working days)

⇨"Compensatory work" is mainly used when you work on Saturday and take "substitute day

off" on a weekday. Therefore, in the future, in such cases, please manage them as follows. 

(Example) 

Saturday: Compensatory work (振替出勤)
Monday: Compensatory day off (代休)

Compensatory work

振替出勤について

62



Eligibility for year-end adjustment in 2024

What is it?

"The total amount of income tax withheld from your salary each month by your employer

differs from your total income tax liability for the year or your income tax deductions differ for

the year, at the end of each year your employer will adjust your salary for any excess or

shortage in the amount of tax withheld so that an exact calculation results. All employees

enrolled in the company are subject to this procedure."

The procedure includes: Filling out the required forms (multiple copies) and Attaching the

necessary certificates, etc. 

*Documents to be prepared differ depending on the person

Foreign employees who have been employed by Japanese company for the first time this year

should pay attention to the following points.

In the period of 2024.1.1~2024.12.31, required some certificates:

1. National Pension (国民年金保険)

→Amount of payment and Payment slip 

(If you don't have, pls go to public office and get proof of the amount of payment)

2. National Health Insurance (国民健康保険)

→Same as 1

3. Life Insurance (if you have)

→Deduction certificate (sent by insurance company)

4. Withholding Tax Statement

→Necessary if you have had a part-time job this year

December salary reflects year-end adjustment refund.

At the bottom of your pay slip, there is a column titled “年末調整 Year-end Adjustment".

The amount shown there is your refund.

2024年度 年末調整対象者の方

お疲れ様です。

63



12月の給与に年末調整の還付金が反映されています。
ご確認をお願いいたします。

Payroll date

The payday is scheduled for the 10th of each month, and I understood that if the 10th falls on a

weekend or holiday, the payment would be made on the next business day.

EG: 10th November is a Sunday so payday will be on Monday, the 11th November.

Moving forward, please note that when the 10th falls on a weekend or holiday, payday will be the

following business day. We appreciate your understanding.

給与日に関しては、私と従業員の方で誤認識が発生しておりました。

毎月10日の給料日ですが、休日が10日の場合は翌営業日だと認識しておりました。

ですので、今回の給料日は週明けの11日月曜日になります。

今後もお休みになる日は翌営業日となりますので、ご理解いただければ幸いです。

67



Addressable Outline Structure

AppStore, PlayStoreでリリースするアプリケーション本体は2GBがファイルサイズの上限と設定
されている。現在のプログラムはファイルサイズの合計が2GBを超えること、またアイテムの
更新が発生するため追加データをサーバーからダウンロードする仕組みを構築することが必要で
あり、その仕組みをここに定義する。

ファイル、データの管理方法

ファイルやデータは複数の管理方法が存在する。

管理するファイル、データ

アプリケーション プログラムファイル、初期状態で必要なファイル
本体

S3 Storage 追加データとして提供する必要のあるデータ（ファ
イルサイズが大きいもの、サーバーから更新したい
もの）を保持する

Database ユーザーデータ、マスターデータ

以下はS3 Storageのファイル管理方法と更新方法について定義する

ファイル一覧の管理

bundleファイルリストとそれらを保持するCloudFrontアドレスを一覧化したCatalogファイルを
生成する。
buneleファイルにはLocal上のファイルパスを保持している。

これらのファイルはUnityによって生成される。

アセットファイルの更新有無の判定方法

CloudFrontに配置されたCattalogファイルをhash化した値と、ローカルが保持したCatalogファ
イルをhash化した値の一致を確認する。一致している場合は更新がなく、不一致の場合はデータ
の差分が存在するため更新が必要である。

具体的な確認フロー

1. Catalogのhash値を記録したファイルを.hashという名称でCloudFrontに保存する

68



2. Unityのプラグインが.hashファイルをダウンロード
3. ローカルのHashとダウンロードした.hashの値を比較する

4. hash値が異なっている場合に、Catalog.jsonファイルをダウンロードする
5. Catalog.jsonファイルを元にプラグインが差分を判定し、追加データのダウンロード、または
ローカルデータの削除を行う

更新有無の判定と更新するタイミング

アプリケーションの起動時

APIリクエスト時
リクエスト時にバージョンが最新ではないエラーがレスポンスされたら、上で定義した
hashの最新判定、更新の処理を通し、再度APIにリクエストする

APIリクエスト時の更新判定方法

フロントエンドからAPIへのリクエスト時に、RequestHeaderにCatalogVersionパラメータを
追加し、その値にローカルのhash値をセットし、APIリクエストする
バックエンドはエンドポイントのDependsとしてRequestHeaderのCatalogVersionの値が最新
かどうかを判定する
最新判定はデータベースの値で行う。
カラムはhash_value, released_at, created_at, updated_at

released_atの日付が過去かつ最新の1件のレコードで判定する

利用するリソース

AWS S3 Storage

AWS Cloud Front

gamecdn.DOMAIN

(subdomain: gamecdn or gamecdn-prod, gamecdn-stage)

なお、S3 Storageのバケットは専用に新しい専用のものを用意する

SideNotes

Addressable Requirements

Addressables - Workflow

69



Unity Addressables Hosting: AWS S3 + CloudFront Setup Guide

Create & Configure S3 Bucket

1. Go to AWS Console → S3 → Create Bucket.

2. Bucket Name: Choose a unique name (e.g., golfin-game-prod ).

3. Region: Choose a region i.e US West (Oregon) us-west-2

4. Check “Block all public access” under Object Ownership > Permissions.

5. Enable ACLs if needed and confirm changes.

6. Click Create Bucket.

Create CloudFront Distribution

1. Go to AWS Console → CloudFront → Create Distribution.

2. Origin domain: Select S3 bucket

3. Origin Access: Use Origin Access Control (OAC) for private S3 buckets.

4. Viewer protocol policy: Redirect HTTP to HTTPS.

5. Web Application Firewall (WAF): Set AWS WAF protection enabled

6. Allowed HTTP methods: Set to GET, HEAD, OPTIONS

7. Cache Policy:

a. Use “Legacy cache settings” or create a custom policy for cache busting.

8. Click Create Distribution.

9. Configure Bucket Policy to allow only Cloudfront OAC

1 {
2 "Version": "2008-10-17",
3 "Id": "PolicyForCloudFrontPrivateContent",
4 "Statement": [
5 {
6 "Sid": "AllowCloudFrontServicePrincipal",
7 "Effect": "Allow",
8 "Principal": {
9 "Service": "cloudfront.amazonaws.com"
10 },
11 "Action": "s3:GetObject",
12 "Resource": "arn:aws:s3:::golfin-trial-bundles/*",
13 "Condition": {
14 "StringEquals": {
15 "AWS:SourceArn":

"arn:aws:cloudfront::027511157035:distribution/E3FSUU98D8A9DP"

74



Authentication

認証はAmazon Cognitoを利用して認証を行う。
認証ユーザーに対する認可は、Cognitoにより認証された情報をもとにAPIにてデータベースと
突合して判定する。

1. ログイン方法

次の3つのログイン方式に対応する

メールアドレスとパスワード
Googleアカウント
Apple ID (iOSの場合)

2.ユーザー認証

次のドキュメントを参照
DOC: Cognito Authentication Flow

Cognito Frontend & Auth Test

認証が成功するとIDトークン、アクセストークン、更新トークンが発行される

3.認証が必要なAPIリクエスト

認証が必要なエンドポイントへのリクエストは、HTTPリクエストヘッダーにCognitoが発行し
たアクセストークンをBearerトークンとして付与してリクエストする

1 Authorization: Bearer <access_token>

C# Example:

1 var url = "https://....";
2 var accessToken = "abc123...";
3 var client = new HttpClient();
4 var request = new HttpRequestMessage(HttpMethod.Get, url);
5 request.Headers.add("Content-Type", "application/json");
6 request.Headers.add("Authorization", $"Bearer {accessToken}");
7 var response = await client.SendAsync(request);

トークンの期限が切れた場合は、更新トークンを利用して新しいトークンに更新する必要があ
る。

75



Pagination

リスト返却が必要なデータは、技術的な制約等、特定の条件を除いて返却最大数を設定する。
返却最大数(ページ分割数)は想定されるデータ量に応じて、インタフェースごとに定義する。

ページネーションが必要な場合、次のパラメータを共通として定義する

Request Parameter

Parameters Mandat DataTyp Default

ory e

page_start bigint 1

page_limit int Interfaceごとに定義する

page_startは、返却するデータの何件目から取得するかを指定する。

page_limitは、取得するデータの件数を指定する。

Response Parameter

Parameters DataType Note

rows bigint 条件に一致したデータの総数を返す

start bigint 開始として指定されたデータの値を
返す

limit int 指定されたデータの件数を返す
(Interfaceごとに指定された値のし
きい値を超えた場合はしきい値の範
囲に変換した値)

Attention

仮に1000件のデータが存在する場合、page_startに1を指定すると先頭から取得。101を指定した
場合は、101件目からを取得する。存在するデータの最大数を超えた値が指定された場合、エラ
ーとせず、0件の空配列が返却される。

このエンドポイントへのGETリクエストでは、公開開始日をすぎているクラブアイテムの一覧
を返却する。マスターデータの返却であるため、ユーザーの所有ステータスは考慮しない。

Request Parameters

Parameter Mandatory DataType Nullable Default

page_start integer ○ 1

page_limit integer ○ 50

order_by string ○ id

is_asc boolean ○ true

page_start

request start data sorted record data

page_limit

min: 1, max: 200

order_by

sort column

acceptable column

id: master recourd id

78



created_at: master data created datetime

published_at: master data published datetime

is_asc

true: asc

false: desc

パラメータがセットされていない場合は、クラブマスタに登録されたデータのうち、アイテム
の公開開始日時を過ぎたクラブリストをidから順に先頭の50件をステータスなしに返却する。

Example

1 /v1/game_club
2 /v1/game_club?page_start=1&page_limit=50&order_by=id&is_act=true

Filter

データの抽出条件は次を満たすデータとする

公開日時を過ぎている(published_at >= current_time)

Response Schemas

正常にデータの取得ができた場合、HTTPステータスコード200番でデータを返却する。

CHARACTERS (登場人物)

OVERVIEW (概要)

Characters are one of the main gameplay features present in GOLFIN, as they are what allow

players to interact with and play the game. Characters will have stats, levels, lifetimes, and traits

that all affect gameplay. These characters are needed for players to play holes in GOLFIN. For

more information see reference documents below.

キャラクターは、GOLFINにおける主要なゲームプレイ要素の1つであり、プレイヤーがゲーム
とやり取りし、プレイするために必要です。キャラクターには、ゲームプレイに影響を与える

87



ステータス、レベル、ライフタイム、および特性があります。これらのキャラクターがあって
初めて、プレイヤーはGOLFINでホールをプレイすることができます。詳細については、以下の
参考資料を参照してください。

CHARACTER PARAMETERS (キャラクターパラメータ)
Characters possess four main parameters that affect gameplay, and can be altered by traits,

gear, and skill points:

Strength

Directly affects max shot distance

Club Control

Directly affects the sizes of the circular zones of safe flicks 

Stamina

Directly affects the maximum energy a character has to play holes

Stamina Regeneration

Directly affects the speed which the character gets stamina back

キャラクターには、ゲームプレイに影響を与える4つの主要なパラメータがあり、これらは特
性、ギア、およびスキルポイントによって変更することができます:

強さ

最大ショット距離に直接影響します
クラブコントロール

ショットゲージの速度に直接影響します。

元気

キャラクターがホールをプレイするために必要な最大エネルギーに直接影響します。
スタミナの回復

キャラクターがスタミナを回復する速度に直接影響します

There are multiple parameters that are not able to be directly affected by the player or may only

be affected indirectly through gear, traits, or gameplay.

CONDITION

88



Offers a bonus or penalty to all parameters depending on how recently a character has

played a hole

Ranges from 90-110

Increases with every game played during a given timeframe, and deteriorates over time if

not playing

REWARD POINT GAIN

Reward Point Gain is a parameter which will increase the amount earned at the end of any

game mode

AGE & LIFETIME

Age will range from 16-70 Years

Age will be entirely cosmetic and will not effect gameplay

Lifetime will be the system used to grow character

プレイヤーによって直接影響を受けることができない、またはギア、特性、またはゲームプレ
イを通じて間接的にのみ影響を受けるパラメーターが複数あります。

状態

キャラクターがどれだけ最近ホールをプレイしたかに応じて、すべてのパラメータにボーナ
スまたはペナルティを提供します
90～110の範囲

一定期間内にゲームがプレイされるたびに増加し、プレイしていない場合は時間の経過と
ともに減少します

報酬ポイントの獲得
報酬ポイント獲得は、ゲームモードの終了時に獲得する量を増加させるパラメータです

年齢と生涯

年齢は16歳から70歳までとなります
年齢は完全に表面上のものであり、ゲームプレイには影響しません。

ライフタイムはキャラクターを成長させるためのシステムとなります

LEVEL (レベル)
As players play through Story Mode and win games in Battle Mode, their characters will gain

experience points (EXP) and level up. Brand new characters will always start at Lvl. 1, and have

89



different max levels depending on rarity. These maximum levels are as follows:

Common: Lvl. 25

Uncommon: Lvl. 40

Rare: Lvl. 55

Mythic: Lvl. 70 (old name: Epic)

Legendary: Lvl. 85

Supreme: Lvl. 100

プレイヤーがストーリーモードを進め、バトルモードでゲームに勝利すると、キャラクターは経
験値（EXP）を獲得し、レベルアップします。新しいキャラクターは常にレベル1から始まり、
レアリティに応じて異なる最大レベルを持ちます。これらの最大レベルは次の通りです:

Common: レベル25

Uncommon: レベル40
Rare: レベル55
Mythic: レベル70

Legendary: レベル85
Supreme: レベル100

Every time a unit levels up, they will gain Skill Points that can be invested into stats in order to

increase them. Each Skill Point will give one point to a stat (seen as twenty-five extra points by

the player). Characters will gain one Skill Point per level, earning an extra point whenever they

enter a new rarity bracket of levels (for example, a Rare character will get one Skill Point from

Lvl. 1 - 25, two from Lvl. 26 - 40, and three from Lvl. 41 - 55.

ユニットがレベルアップするたびに、ステータスに投資して増加させるためのスキルポイント
を獲得します。各スキルポイントは1つのステータスに1ポイント（プレイヤーからは追加の25ポ
イントとして見えます）を与えます。キャラクターはレベルごとに1つのスキルポイントを獲得
し、新しいレアリティのレベル範囲に入るたびに追加のポイントを獲得します（例えば、レア
キャラクターはレベル1〜25で1スキルポイント、レベル26〜40で2スキルポイント、レベル41〜
55で3スキルポイントを得ます）。

90



LIFETIME (寿命)

Character lifetimes represent the duration within which the player is able to use the character,

when they will gain traits, and what the maximum stat capacities will be:

Lifetimes occur in three stages

Stage 1 is when characters will receive their first trait and have the highest maximum

strength

Stage 2 is when characters will receive their second trait and have the most balanced

maximum stats

Stage 3 is when characters will receive their third trait and have the highest maximum club

control

When a characters life time has ended they will be unusable until the player either sells them

on the market or buys more lifetime stages

Characters will retain the same level and stats they had even when unusable

キャラクターのライフタイムは、プレイヤーがキャラクターを使用できる期間を表し、特性を獲
得するタイミングや最大ステータスのキャパシティが決まります:

ライフタイムは3つのステージに分かれています

ステージ1: キャラクターが最初の特性を獲得し、最大の強さを持つ
ステージ2: キャラクターが2つ目の特性を獲得し、最もバランスの取れた最大ステータスを
持つ

ステージ3: キャラクターが3つ目の特性を獲得し、最大のクラブコントロールを持つ
キャラクターのライフタイムが終了すると、プレイヤーが市場で売却するか、ライフタイム
ステージを追加購入するまで、キャラクターは使用できなくなります
キャラクターは使用不能になっても同じレベルとステータスを保持します

TRAITS (特性)

Traits are special bonuses that characters will get as they go through their first lifetime. When a

character is initially rolled, they will randomly receive between three and six slots to fill with

traits. These traits come in different rarities which affect the characters stats:

特性は、キャラクターが最初の生涯を経るときに得られる特別なボーナスです。キャラクターが
最初にロールされると、特性を埋めるために 3 ～ 6 つのスロットがランダムに与えられます。

91



これらの特性にはさまざまなレアリティがあり、キャラクターの統計に影響を与えます。

Traits will be gained at the beginning of each lifetime stage

特性は各ライフタイムステージの開始時に獲得されます
Traits can have both positive and negative effects but will always be a net positive effect

特性にはポジティブな効果とネガティブな効果がありますが、常に総合的にプラスの効果を
もたらします
Traits come in rarities at the same rates as the gacha

特性のレアリティはガチャと同じ確率で設定されています
Players can buy trait rerolls

プレイヤーは特性のリロールを購入することができます

REFERENCE DOCUMENTS (参照文書)

Player Character Trait Overview

Player Character & Club Calculator Metric Data (Used for multiple systems)

Player Character Parameters

Player Character Leveling Mechanics

CLUBS & BALLS (クラブ & ボール)

OVERVIEW (概要)

Clubs are the second core gameplay mechanic present in GOLFIN, as players must be able to

use and master a wide variety of clubs to succeed in gameplay. Players are able to obtain new

clubs through the gacha and marketplace, and then select clubs to put into their golf bag.

During play, players can use whatever clubs they have in their golf bag to make the most out of

their situations. Similarly to characters, clubs also gain levels through gameplay, with max level

being determined by the rarity of the club.

クラブは、GOLFINのゲームプレイにおける2番目の主要なメカニックであり、プレイヤーは
様々なクラブを使いこなして成功する必要があります。プレイヤーはガチャやマーケットプレ
イスを通じて新しいクラブを入手し、それをゴルフバッグに入れるクラブを選択します。プレ
イ中は、ゴルフバッグに入っているクラブを自由に使い、状況に応じて最適なショットを狙いま
す。キャラクターと同様に、クラブもゲームプレイを通じてレベルアップし、クラブのレアリ
ティによって最大レベルが決まります。

92



Balls are also an important part of the gameplay cycle, as they allow players to more easily

adapt to the courses they are playing on. Balls act as consumable items that can be used at the

start of a hole in order to give players certain advantages, such as wind resistance or increased

shot distance.

ボールもゲームプレイサイクルにおいて重要な役割を果たします。ボールは、プレイヤーがプ
レイするコースに適応しやすくするための消耗品として機能します。ホールの開始時に使用する
ことで、風の抵抗を減らしたり、ショット距離を増やしたりといった特定の有利な効果をプレイ
ヤーに与えます。

CLUB TYPES (クラブの種類)

In GOLFIN, there are five different types of clubs that players can use, each with their own

specialties:

Driver

Drivers are used from the tee and have high power and accuracy stats

Wood

Woods are used from the fairway and have split power and accuracy stats

Iron

Irons are used for smaller approach shots and have high accuracy and spin

Wedge

Wedges are used from the rough to get the player back onto the course and have a high

recovery and spin stat

Putter

Putters are used on the green and have high power and accuracy stats

GOLFINには、プレイヤーが使用できる5種類のクラブがあり、それぞれに特有の特徴がありま
す:

ドライバー

ドライバーはティーから使用され、高いパワーと精度のステータスを持っています

ウッド

ウッドはフェアウェイから使用され、パワーと精度のステータスが分割されています

93



アイアン

アイアンは短いアプローチショットに使用され、高い精度とスピンを持っています

ウェッジ

ウェッジはラフからコースに戻るために使用され、高いリカバリーとスピンのステータス
を持っています

パター

パターはグリーン上で使用され、高いパワーと精度のステータスを持っています

CLUB PARAMETERS (クラブのパラメーター)
Clubs possess six main parameters that affect gameplay:

Power

Affects maximum shot distance

Accuracy

Affects the error deviation of non-perfect shots

Spin

Affects the maximum amount of angle players can hit the ball with to add to the Natural Loft

of the club

Recovery

Affects how easy it is to make shots from rough terrain

Natural Loft

Affects the clubface angle, this angle imparts a small amount of upward force no matter

where the ball is hit

Durability

The number of times a club can be used before it must be repaired

クラブには、ゲームプレイに影響を与える6つの主要なパラメーターがあります:

1. パワー

最大ショット距離に影響します
2. 精度

ショットゲージの異なるヒットゾーンのサイズに影響します

3. スピン

クラブの自然なロフトに加えるために、ボールを打つ角度の最大量に影響します

94



4. リカバリー

ラフなどの困難な地形からショットを打つ際の難易度に影響します

5. 自然なロフト

クラブフェースの角度に影響し、ボールがどこに当たってもわずかな上向きの力を加えま
す

6. 耐久性

クラブが修理を必要とするまでに使用できる回数に影響します

BALL PARAMETERS (ボールのパラメーター)
Balls possess three parameters, each of which having a different effect on gameplay:

Power

Affects max shot distance

Rebound

Affects how bouncy the ball is after touching the ground

Wind Resistance

Affects how much of an effect wind has on the ball while in the air

Roll

Affects how far the ball rolls after landing

Spin

Affects the spin point selection zone of the ball

パワー

最大ショット距離に影響します
リバウンド
地面に触れた後のボールの反発力に影響します

風抵抗
空中で風がボールに与える影響の大きさに影響します

ロール
ボールが着地した後の転がり距離に影響します

Unlike club and character parameters, ball parameters can range from +5 to -5, and are

completely static. Players default to using a Standard White Ball with zero in all parameters, but

95



certain special balls can be obtained and used to increase certain parameters.

クラブやキャラクターのパラメーターとは異なり、ボールのパラメーターは +5 から -5 の範囲
で、完全に静的です。プレイヤーはデフォルトですべてのパラメータがゼロの標準白ボールを使
用しますが、特定の特別なボールを入手して、特定のパラメータを増加させるために使用できま
す。

REFERENCE DOCUMENTS (参考文書)

GEAR & ITEMS (装備とアイテム)

OVERVIEW (概要)

The main purpose of gear in GOLFIN is to enhance the players stats beyond what their skill

points are able to. Player’s gear will come in multiple rarities which will increase their

effectiveness in enhancing the characters stats.

Items are another important part of the gamble experience, as they allow players to gain extra

bonuses outside of gear and equippables. Items are usually single use items that perform

special actions such as repairing gear or granting extra experience.

GOLFIN におけるギアの主な目的は、プレイヤーのスキル ポイントを超えてプレイヤーの統計
を強化することです。プレイヤーの装備には複数のレアリティがあり、キャラクターのステー
タスを強化する効果が高まります。

アイテムは、プレイヤーがギアや装備品以外の追加ボーナスを獲得できるようにするため、ギャ
ンブル体験のもう 1 つの重要な部分です。アイテムは通常、装備の修理や追加の経験値の付与な
どの特別なアクションを実行する使い捨てアイテムです。

96



GEAR (装備)

Overall, there are five different types of gear that players can equip, each of which giving

different bonuses in various areas:

Headgear

Greatly increases a character’s stamina regeneration, slightly increases their club control

Shirt

Greatly increases a character’s strength, slightly increases their stamina

Pants

Greatly increases a character’s stamina, slightly increases their stamina regeneration

Gloves

Greatly increases a character’s club control, slightly increases their strength

Shoes

Decreases the penalties from rough terrain

全体として、プレイヤーが装備できる5種類のギアがあり、それぞれがさまざまな分野で異なる
ボーナスを提供します：

ヘッドギア

キャラクターのスタミナ回復を大幅に増加させ、クラブコントロールを少し増加させま
す。

シャツ

キャラクターの強さを大幅に増加させ、スタミナを少し増加させます。
パンツ
キャラクターのスタミナを大幅に増加させ、スタミナ回復を少し増加させます。

グローブ
キャラクターのクラブコントロールを大幅に増加させ、強さを少し増加させます。

シューズ
ラフなどの悪条件によるペナルティを軽減します。

97



Each character can equip up to one of each type of gear at a time. For every hole completed,

the durability of any equipped gear will decrease by one. Players can also equip gear, broken or

not, in vanity slots that change their character’s appearance, but not their stats.

各キャラクターは一度に各タイプのギアを 1 つまで装備できます。ホールを完了するごとに、装
備されているギアの耐久性が 1 つ減少します。プレイヤーは、壊れているかどうかに関係なく、
キャラクターの外観を変更するバニティ スロットに装備を装備することもできますが、ステー
タスは変更できません。

ITEMS (アイテム)
There are a variety of consumable items present in GOLFIN that players are able to use to give

certain buffs. These items can be obtained from Story Mode gameplay, as well as the

marketplace:

Repair Kit

Restores the durability of a club or piece of gear, but lowers its maximum durability

Premium Repair Kit

Restores the durability of a club or piece of gear, without changing the maximum

Specialty Balls

Special balls that have have altered parameters

Lifetime Extension

Extends the lifetime of a character. Can be for all three stages of a lifetime, or one specific

stage

Experience Booster

Boosts the amount of experience points gained through gameplay

GOLFINには、プレイヤーが特定のバフを得るために使用できるさまざまな消耗品アイテムが存
在します。これらのアイテムは、ストーリーモードのゲームプレイやマーケットプレイスで入
手できます：

修理キット
クラブまたはギアの耐久性を回復させますが、最大耐久性は低下します。

プレミアム修理キット
クラブまたはギアの耐久性を回復させ、最大耐久性は変わりません。

98



特殊ボール
パラメータが変更された特殊なボールです。

ライフタイム延長
キャラクターのライフタイムを延長します。ライフタイムの全3段階を延長するか、特定の
段階を延長することができます。

経験値ブースター
ゲームプレイを通じて得られる経験値の量を増加させます。

USER INTERFACE (ユーザーインターフェース)
The User Interface for gameplay is meant to leave the upper half of the screen empty and allow

for a sense of alignment with the player's finger placement and the interactions with the golf

ball. The UI also allows for a familiarity between both normal shots and putting while being

functionally different from one another.

ゲームプレイ用のユーザーインターフェースは、画面の上半分を空け、プレイヤーの指の配置と
ゴルフボールとの相互作用が調和するように設計されています。UIは通常のショットとパッテ
ィングの間に親しみを持たせつつも、機能的には異なるデザインになっています。

REFERENCE DOCUMENTS (参考文書)

Hitting, Driving, & Putting UI Design Brief

CAMERA SYSTEM (カメラシステム)

The camera system will be a standardized way of setting up the camera and generating

reactions based on the actions taken in game. Players will be presented with the same camera

position each time they take a shot and then the camera will react in specified ways depending

101



on how well the player hits the ball. Other cameras such as the map view will be the exact same

no matter the situation.

カメラ システムは、カメラをセットアップし、ゲーム内で行われたアクションに基づいて反応
を生成する標準化された方法になります。プレーヤーにはショットを打つたびに同じカメラ位置
が表示され、プレーヤーがボールをどれだけうまく打つかに応じてカメラは指定された方法で反
応します。マップビューなどの他のカメラは、状況に関係なくまったく同じです。

REFERENCE DOCUMENTS (参考文書)

Camera Mechanics

GAMEPLAY MODES (ゲームプレイモード)

STORY MODE (話モード)
The story mode format follows a linear path that the player will follow as they complete themed

courses for each section and earn stars as they complete challenges set forth for each level

individually. Players will be required to collect enough stars before they are allowed to continue

on to the next course.

ストーリー モードの形式は、プレーヤーが各セクションのテーマ コースを完了し、レベルごと
に個別に設定された課題を完了することでスターを獲得するときにたどる直線的なパスに従いま
す。プレイヤーは次のコースに進む前に、十分なスターを集める必要があります。

REFERENCE DOCUMENTS (参考文書)

Story Mode Design Document

BATTLE MODE (戦いモード)

The Battle Mode will allow players to connect with other players online and play 1v1 matches

against each other to increase their ranking and earn Reward Points. These ranking points will

determine the strength of opponents they match with, as well as determining the league they

are able to compete in during the end of week tournaments.

102



バトルモードでは、プレイヤーが他のプレイヤーとオンラインで接続し、1対1の対戦を行ってラ
ンキングを上げたり報酬ポイントを獲得したりします。これらのランキングポイントは、マッ
チングされる対戦相手の強さを決定し、週末のトーナメントで競えるリーグを決定します。

REFERENCE DOCUMENTS (参考文書)

Ranking Points

TOURNAMENTS (競争)

Tournaments are held every weekend with large cash prize tournaments being held on the last

weekend of each month. These tournaments will be held in a single elimination format taking

place over multiple days.

トーナメントは毎週末に開催され、毎月最後の週末には高額の賞金トーナメントが開催されま
す。これらのトーナメントは、複数日に渡って行われるシングルエリミネーション形式で開催さ
れます。

REFERENCE DOCUMENTS (参考文書)

Tournament Mode Technical Document

Ranking Points

MONETIZATION (収益化)

The listed forms of monetization possible in GOLFIN are collected from all aspects of the design

thus far and can be found in their respective sections.

GOLFINの可能な収益化形態は、これまでのデザインのあらゆる側面から収集され、それぞれの
セクションで見つけることができます。

CHARACTERS (キャラクター)
Buying Characters

103



Pulling for the character in a gacha or an event

Buying the character directly from the marketplace

Experience Boosts

Players who want to speed up their progress can spend money on experience boosts that

will allow them to earn more experience

Lifetime Stages

Players who have characters that they enjoy will be able to purchase extra Lifetime in one

of the three stages to continue playing that character

Trait Rerolling

Players that want to build their character in a specific way can spend money on random

trait rerolls to try and improve their character

キャラクターの購入
ガチャやイベントでキャラクターを引くこと
マーケットプレイスから直接キャラクターを購入すること

経験値ブースト
プレイヤーが進行を加速させたい場合、経験値ブーストにお金を使ってより多くの経験値を
獲得することができます

ライフタイムステージ
お気に入りのキャラクターを持つプレイヤーは、そのキャラクターを継続的にプレイする
ために、3つのステージのうちの1つで追加のライフタイムを購入することができます

特性の再振り

特定の方法でキャラクターを構築したいプレイヤーは、キャラクターの特性をランダムに
再振りするためにお金を使うことができます

プレイヤーはプレミアム修理キットを購入してクラブを修理し、最大耐久度を下げること
なく修理することができます

きます

す

しません。

Clubs & Balls Formulas

CALCULATIONS (計算)
OVERVIEW (概要)
MAXIMUM HEIGHT FORMULA (最大高さの式)
CARRY DISTANCE FORMULA (飛距離計算式)
WIND FORCE EFFECT FORMULA (風力効果の公式)
BALL TRAIL FORMULA (ボール・トレイルの計算式)

CALCULATIONS (計算)

OVERVIEW (概要)

In GOLFIN, there are two main calculations used in regards to the distance that balls travel after

getting hit: the calculation for Maximum Ball Height, and the one for Carry Distance. These

calculations are based on the average, real-world formulas for finding these variables. They also

assume there is no wind present, which would affect the trajectory of the ball.

ゴルフでは、ボールが打たれた後に移動する距離に関する2つの主要な計算があります：最大ボ
ール高さの計算とキャリー距離の計算です。これらの計算は、これらの変数を見つけるための平
均的な実世界の式に基づいています。また、ボールの軌道に影響を与える風がないことを前提と
しています。

For intractable versions of all equations listed below, refer to the Player Character & Club

Calculator Metric Data.

108



以下にリストされているすべての式の操作可能なバージョンについては、Player Character &
Club Calcula を参照してください。

MAXIMUM HEIGHT FORMULA (最大高さの式)

The formula for calculating the maximum height a ball will reach while midair is as follows:

H = (Vo * sin(𝜃))2 / (2 * g)

Where:

H is the ball’s maximum height (in meters)

Vo is the initial velocity of the ball (in meters per second)

Equal to 1.5 times the club’s Swing Speed

Swing Speed is equal to a club’s Power multiplied by Shot Power

𝜃 is the launch angle of the ball (in degrees)

Determined by where the player hits the ball

g is the ball’s acceleration due to gravity (9.81 m/s2)

ボールが空中にある間に到達する最大高さを計算する式は次のとおりです：

H = (Vo * sin(𝜃))2 / (2 * g)

ここで：

H はボールの最大高さです（メートル単位）
Vo はボールの初速度です（秒速メートル単位）

クラブのスイングスピードの1.5倍に等しいです
スイングスピードは、クラブのパワーにショットパワーを乗じたものです

𝜃 はボールの打ち出し角度です（度単位）
プレイヤーがボールを打つ位置によって決定されます

g は重力によるボールの加速度です（9.81 m/s2）

109



CARRY DISTANCE FORMULA (飛距離計算式)

Carry Distance is the distance in which a ball travels after it gets hit until it hits the ground for the

first time. The formula to calculate it is as follows:

CD = BS * cos(LA) * 1.75

Where:

CD is the Carry Distance of the ball (in yards)

To convert meters to yards, multiply the value in yards by 0.9144

BS is the speed at which the ball is traveling (in miles per hour)

You can convert initial velocity to ball speed by multiplying it by 2.2369

LA is the Launch Angle of the ball

キャリー距離とは、ボールが打たれてから初めて地面に着地するまでの距離です。それを計算す
るための式は次のとおりです：

CD = BS * cos(LA) * 1.75

ここで：

CD はボールのキャリー距離です（ヤード単位）
メートルをヤードに変換するには、ヤードでの値を0.9144倍します

BS はボールの移動速度です（マイル毎時単位）
初速度をボールの速度に変換するには、それを2.2369倍します

LA はボールの打ち出し角度です

WIND FORCE EFFECT FORMULA (風力効果の公式)

Wind Force Effect is the force applied to the ball from the wind. The force will be applied in the

direction of the wind to the ball directly. The formula is as follows:

AF = WF * BR

Where:

AF is the Applied Force on the ball

WF is the Wind Force from the scene that is applicable to the ball

BR is the Ball Resistance to the wind (Range of 0-2)

110



風力効果は、風がボールに直接与える力です。この力は、風の方向にボールに適用されます。計
算式は以下の通りです：

AF = WF * BR

ここで：

AFはボールに適用される力です。
WFはシーンからボールに適用される風力です。

BRは風に対するボールの抵抗係数です（範囲は0から2）。

BALL TRAIL FORMULA (ボール・トレイルの計算式)

The ball trail is the colored effect (generally a line) that follows behind the ball. These trails will

follow the ball and their length will be determined by the speed the ball is moving. The trail effect

lifetime in seconds will be as follows:

Where:

If BS >= 25

TL = 3 * (BS / 100)

Else

TL =  1 * (BS / 100)

BS is the speed at which the ball is traveling (in miles per hour)

You can convert initial velocity to ball speed by multiplying it by 2.2369

TL is the trails lifetime in seconds

ボールトレイルは、ボールの後ろに続く色付きのエフェクト（一般的にはライン）のことです。
このトレイルはボールの後を追い、その長さはボールの移動速度によって決まります。トレイ
ルエフェクトの持続時間は以下の通りです。

ここで：

If BS >= 25

TL = 3 * (BS / 100)

Else

111



TL =  1 * (BS / 100)

BS はボールの移動速度です（マイル毎時単位）
初速度をボールの速度に変換するには、それを2.2369倍します

TLは、トレイルの持続時間（秒）を表します。

Club Design Master Document

CHANGELOG

DATE VERSION CONTENT  USER

Dec 1, 2024 Ported to @Cesar

Confluence Guarinoni

OVERVIEW (概要)

Clubs are one of the most important aspects of GOLFIN, as they are used throughout normal

gameplay to hit balls and complete courses. Players are able to put a variety of clubs into their

golf bag in order to create a playstyle that fits their characters and the courses they are playing.

This document covers clubs and their types, the parameters of clubs and their rarities. Brands

and how they affect clubs. The upgrades players can use  on their clubs as well as the usage

restrictions of certain clubs and the penalties of different terrain types.

クラブは、GOLFINの最も重要な要素の一つです。通常のゲームプレイ中にボールを打ち、コー
スをクリアするために使用されます。プレイヤーは、キャラクターやプレイしているコースに
合ったプレイスタイルを作成するために、さまざまなクラブをゴルフバッグに入れることがで
きます。この文書では、クラブとその種類、クラブのパラメータと希少性について説明します。
また、クラブに影響を与えるブランドや、クラブのアップグレード方法、特定のクラブの使用制
限、そして異なる地形タイプのペナルティについてもカバーします。

113



CLUB TYPES (クラブの種類)

Clubs are organized into five different types, each with different traits and specialties for players

to take advantage of:

DRIVER

Possesses high Power and Durability, and above average stats in other areas

Can only be used when making a tee shot (the first of a hole)

Base Hit Distance: 200 meters

Possesses higher than average power

Excels at hitting the ball medium to long distances

Wood 3 Information:

Base Hit Distance: 180 meters

Wood 5 Information:

Base Hit Distance: 170 meters

Wood 7 Information:

Base Hit Distance: 160 meters

IRON

Possesses all-around decent stats, with good Spin and Recovery

Excels at hitting the ball short to medium distances, and out of the Rough

Base Hit Distance: 185 meters

Iron 4 Information:

Base Hit Distance: 175 meters

Possesses high Recovery, with lower than average stats in other areas

Excels at hitting the ball out of Bunkers and the Rough

Pitching Wedge Information:

Base Hit Distance: 90 meters

Sand WedgeInformation:

Base Hit Distance: 75 meters

PUTTER

Possesses high Accuracy and Durability

The only club that can be used on the Green

115

専門分野があります:

全体的にまずまずの統計を持ち、スピンとリカバリーが良好です

CLUB PARAMETERS (クラブパラメーター)
Like characters, clubs possess their own set of parameters that affect various aspects of

gameplay. Each club has an innate set of base stats, though these can be adjusted in a variety

of ways. Furthermore, these parameters are completely separate from those found on players.

Power

Affects the maximum distance your ball can travel before it hits the ground

Is used in the calculations for carry distance and maximum ball height

Accuracy

Affects the speed of the shot gauge

Higher accuracy means the shot gauge will move more slowly

Spin

Increases the amount of spin you can apply to the ball

Increases the area on the surface of the ball that players are able to aim at

Recovery

Affects how easy it is to make shots out of rough terrain

Mitigates terrain penalties by a percent determined by recovery

Natural Loft

The permanent angle the club has

More loft means a wider angle head on the club

Durability

The number of times a club can be used before it needs to be repaired

Clubs can be repaired with Repair Kits, consumable items that lower a club’s maximum

durability, and then restores it to that new max

Premium Repair Kits can be used to repair clubs without lowering maximum durability

118



キャラクターと同様に、クラブにもゲームプレイの様々な要素に影響を与える独自のパラメータ
ーがあります。各クラブには固有の基本ステータスがあり、これらはさまざまな方法で調整可能
です。さらに、これらのパラメーターはプレイヤーのものとは完全に別です。

パワー

ボールが地面に着く前の最大飛距離に影響します
キャリー距離と最大ボール高さの計算に使用されます

精度

ショットゲージの速度に影響します
精度が高いほどショットゲージの動きが遅くなります

スピン

ボールにかけるスピンの量を増やします
プレイヤーが狙えるボールの表面の範囲を広げます

リカバリー

悪い地形からのショットがどれだけ容易になるかに影響します
リカバリーによって決定される割合で地形ペナルティを軽減します

ナチュラルロフト

クラブの固定された角度です

ロフトが多いほど、クラブのヘッドの角度が広くなります

耐久性

修理が必要になる前にクラブを使用できる回数です

クラブは消耗アイテムである修理キットを使って修理でき、クラブの最大耐久性を減らし
てからその新しい最大値まで回復します

プレミアム修理キットを使うと、最大耐久性を減らすことなくクラブを修理できます

OBTAINING CLUBS (クラブの入手方法)

When players first start the game, they will be given six clubs. Out of these clubs, two of them

will be Uncommon rarity, while four of them will be Common rarity. The Driver, Wedge, and

Putter are predetermined, while Woods and Irons will randomly roll Natural Loft between the

following values each with about 0° - 3° of variation, reflecting the different types of clubs in

real life:

Wood

119



3 Wood - 15-18°

5 Wood - 18-21°

7 Wood - 21-24°

Iron #1

3 Iron - 19-22°

4 Iron - 21-24°

5 Iron - 23-26°

Iron #2

6 Iron - 26-29°

7 Iron - 30-33°

8 Iron - 35-38°

9 Iron - 40-43°

プレイヤーがゲームを初めて開始する際、6本のクラブが与えられます。これらのクラブのう
ち、2本はアンコモンのレアリティであり、残りの4本はコモンのレアリティです。ドライバ
ー、ウェッジ、パターは事前に決定されていますが、ウッドとアイアンはリアルのクラブの種
類を反映して、次の値の間で約1°〜2°のばらつきでナチュラルロフトがランダムに設定されま
す：

ウッド

3ウッド - 15-18°

5ウッド - 18-21°

7ウッド - 21-24°

アイアン #1

3アイアン - 19-22°

4アイアン - 21-24°

5アイアン - 23-26°

アイアン #2

6アイアン - 26-29°

7アイアン - 30-33°

8アイアン - 35-38°

9アイアン - 40-43°

120



Besides the initial clubs the player receivers, there are two other ways for players to gain new

clubs:

The Gacha: For a price, players will be able to roll the game’s gacha, allowing them to obtain

clubs, as well as other items and gear. If a player receives a club from the gacha, it will be added

to their inventory, where they can put it in one of their character’s golf bags to use. Alongside

special banners for events and collaborations, there will also be a set of permanent banners for

players to roll on. This will include a basic banner with all available clubs, as well as banners

specific to certain club types. These will be more expensive than the basic banner, but will

feature increased odds for higher rarity clubs, as well as only having one type of club available

on the banner.

The Marketplace: Much like with characters, players are also able to put clubs up on the

marketplace as well. While they will often be more expensive than the gacha, this will allow

players an opportunity to purchase specific clubs they need, rather than relying on random

chance.

プレイヤーが初期のクラブを受け取る以外に、新しいクラブを手に入れる方法が2つあります:

ガチャ: プレイヤーは料金を支払うことで、ゲームのガチャを回してクラブや他のアイテム、装
備を手に入れることができます。プレイヤーがガチャでクラブを手に入れると、それはインベ
ントリに追加され、キャラクターのゴルフバッグに入れて使用できます。イベントやコラボレ
ーションの特別なバナーと並んで、プレイヤーが回せる常設のバナーセットも用意されていま
す。これには、利用可能なすべてのクラブを含む基本バナーや特定のクラブタイプに特化したバ
ナーが含まれます。これらは基本バナーよりも高価ですが、高レアリティのクラブの確率が高
く、バナーに表示されるクラブの種類が一つだけという特徴があります。

マーケットプレイス: キャラクターと同様に、プレイヤーはクラブをマーケットプレイスに出品
することもできます。ガチャよりも高価になることが多いですが、ランダムな運に頼るのでは
なく、必要な特定のクラブを購入する機会が得られます。

CLUB RARITIES (クラブのレアリティ)
Clubs exist in six rarities, each determining the club’s base stats and maximum level:

Common

The lowest rarity and the most commonly obtained clubs by players. Common clubs have stats

that are randomly determined within specified ranges depending on the club type, and a

maximum level of Lvl. 25.

121



Uncommon

The second lowest rarity. Uncommon clubs have stats that are randomly determined within

specified ranges depending on the club type, and a maximum level of Lvl. 45.

Rare

The third lowest rarity. Rare clubs have stats that are randomly determined within specified

ranges depending on the club type, and a maximum level of Lvl. 55.

Epic

The third highest rarity. Epic clubs have stats that are randomly determined within specified

ranges depending on the club type, and a maximum level of Lvl. 70.

Legendary

The second highest rarity. Legendary clubs have stats that are randomly determined within

specified ranges depending on the club type, and a maximum level of Lvl. 85.

Supreme

The highest rarity. Supreme clubs will have stats that are randomly determined within specified

ranges depending on the club type, and a maximum level of Lvl. 100.

See Character Mechanic Metric Data’s Club Metrics Sheet for more information.

クラブは6つのレアリティがあり、それぞれがクラブの基本ステータスと最大レベルを決定しま
す:

コモン

最も低いレアリティで、プレイヤーが最も頻繁に入手するクラブです。コモンクラブのステー
タスは、クラブの種類に応じて指定された範囲内でランダムに決定され、最大レベルは25で
す。

アンコモン

2番目に低いレアリティです。アンコモンクラブのステータスは、クラブの種類に応じて指定さ
れた範囲内でランダムに決定され、最大レベルは45です。

レア

3番目に低いレアリティです。レアクラブのステータスは、クラブの種類に応じて指定された範
囲内でランダムに決定され、最大レベルは55です。

エピック

3番目に高いレアリティです。エピッククラブのステータスは、クラブの種類に応じて指定され
た範囲内でランダムに決定され、最大レベルは70です。

122



レジェンダリー

2番目に高いレアリティです。レジェンダリークラブのステータスは、クラブの種類に応じて指
定された範囲内でランダムに決定され、最大レベルは85です。

スプリーム

最高のレアリティです。スプリームクラブのステータスは、クラブの種類に応じて指定された
範囲内でランダムに決定され、最大レベルは100です。

Character Mechanic Metric Data のクラブメトリックスシートをご覧ください。

CLUB TRAITS AND BRANDS (クラブブランド)
Clubs will gain traits as they level. Every 20 levels a player’s club will receive a trait that is

randomly rolled. Clubs will be able to have five traits total when they reach max level. These

traits will only affect the specific club they are on. The traits on clubs will be percentage

bonuses much like character traits, these bonuses can be passive or situational.

クラブはレベルが上がるにつれて特性を獲得します。 20 レベルごとに、プレイヤーのクラブは
ランダムにロールされる特性を受け取ります。クラブは最大レベルに達すると、合計 5 つの特
性を持つことができます。これらの特性は、所属している特定のクラブにのみ影響します。クラ
ブの特性はキャラクターの特性と同様にパーセンテージボーナスとなり、これらのボーナスは受
動的または状況に応じたものになります。

Every club and piece of gear will also possess a Brand, signifying the company that made it.

These can be made up in-house, but can also be taken from real-life manufacturers that we

collaborate with.  Brands will give a specific bonus that can be either passive or situational. In

order for a brand's bonus to be active the player must have three or more pieces of gear

equipped at once. For each piece of gear that a player has an active bonus for, the bonus will

raise by 1% for a total increase TBD. (~13% can do a final full gear bonus to make it a nice 15%)

Players will be able to have multiple brand bonuses active at once as long as they have three or

more pieces of gear equipped of the same brand.

すべてのクラブとギアにもブランドがあり、それを製造した会社を示します。これらは社内で
作成することもできますが、提携している実際のメーカーから入手することもできます。  ブラ
ンドは、受動的または状況に応じた特定のボーナスを提供します。ブランドのボーナスを有効に

123



するには、プレーヤーは一度に 3 つ以上のギアを装備する必要があります。プレイヤーがアク
ティブなボーナスを持っているギアごとに、ボーナスは 1% ずつ増加し、合計増加額は未定で
す。 (最大 13% は、最終的なフル装備ボーナスを実行して、15% に増やすことができます) プレ
イヤーは、同じブランドの装備を 3 つ以上装備している限り、複数のブランド ボーナスを同時
に有効にすることができます。

Furthermore, each Brand in the game will possess a unique Brand Characteristic, which is a

passive or conditional boost to the club’s performance or parameters. All clubs with the same

Brand will possess the same Characteristic. Characteristics for brands made in-house will

always possess a trade off (e.g. +1% Power, -1% Accuracy when in the Fairway), while real-life

brands from collaborations will always only provide benefits, in order to make their gear feel

more unique and powerful.

さらに、ゲーム内の各ブランドには固有のブランド特性があり、クラブの性能やパラメータに対
するパッシブまたは条件付きのブーストがあります。同じブランドのクラブはすべて同じ特性
を持ちます。自社製のブランド特性は常にトレードオフを伴います（例：フェアウェイではパワ
ーが+1%、正確さが-1%）が、コラボレーションによる実際のブランドは常に利益のみを提供
し、そのギアをより独自で強力に感じさせます。

CLUB USAGE RESTRICTIONS (クラブの使用制限)

There are currently two club usage restrictions in GOLFIN. The first usage restriction is on the

driver. Drivers may only be used from the tee (the first stroke). The second club usage

restriction is on the putter. Putters may only be used on the green.

現在、GOLFINには2つのクラブ使用制限があります。最初の使用制限はドライバーに関するも
のです。ドライバーはティーからのショット（最初の一打）のみで使用可能です。2つ目のクラ
ブ使用制限はパターに関するものです。パターはグリーン上でのみ使用可能です。

CLUB TERRAIN INTERACTIONS (クラブと地形の相互作用)

Different pieces of terrain have different penalties or bonuses from one another. While the green

and the tee have no penalties or bonuses the other terrain types do. The penalties and the

bonuses are as follows:

124



Fairway: Hitting from the fairway gives a 5% bonus to the players max shot distance

Semi-Rough (First Cut): Hitting from the semi-rough gives a 20% debuff to the max shot

distance

Rough: Hitting from the rough gives a 40% debuff to the max shot distance

Bunker: Hitting from the bunker gives a 60% debuff to the max shot distance

異なる地形はお互いに異なるペナルティやボーナスを持っています。グリーンとティーにはペ
ナルティやボーナスがありませんが、他の地形タイプにはあります。ペナルティとボーナスは
以下の通りです：

フェアウェイ：フェアウェイからの打球は、プレーヤーの最大飛距離に5%のボーナスを与えま
す。

セミラフ（初カット）：セミラフからの打球は、最大飛距離に20%のデバフを与えます。

ラフ：ラフからの打球は、最大飛距離に40%のデバフを与えます。

バンカー：バンカーからの打球は、最大飛距離に60%のデバフを与えます。

SUMMARY (概要)

Clubs will come in specific types that specialize in different areas

Certain types of clubs have different variations that further increase specialization

Clubs can be obtained through the game’s gacha system or from the marketplace

Players will also receive a set of semi-random clubs at the beginning of the game

Club Parameters are the stat types that clubs will have

We added a new parameter, Natural Loft, that determines the innate angle of the club’s

head

Club Rarities will determine the total value of specific parameters on clubs

Basic rarity has been added for the players initial set of clubs and gear

Club brands will add specific traits to clubs, and extra bonuses to clubs in the same bag that

share brands

Brands also possess special Characteristics that provide bonuses and are innate on any

club from a given Brand

Special club components can be added to clubs to increase their base stats

125



Only one component of each type can be applied to a club at one time, and certain clubs

cannot be upgraded

Club restrictions exist for both the driver and the putter

Drivers are only useable from the Tee

Putters are only usable from the Green

Clubs will receive buffs and debuffs depending on the terrain

Tee & Green: No changes

Fairway: 5% total distance buff

Semi-Rough: 20% total distance debuff

Rough: 40% total distance debuff

Bunker: 60% total distance debuff

クラブには、異なる分野に特化した特定のタイプがあります
特定の種類のクラブには、さらなる専門性を高めるためのさまざまなバリエーションがあ
ります

クラブはゲームのガチャシステムまたはマーケットプレイスで取得できます
プレイヤーはゲーム開始時にセミランダムなクラブのセットも受け取ります

クラブパラメータは、クラブが持つステータスの種類です
新しいパラメータ「ナチュラルロフト」を追加しました。これはクラブヘッドの固有の角
度を決定します

クラブのレアリティは、クラブの特定のパラメータの総価値を決定します。
基本的なレアリティは、プレイヤーの初期セットのクラブとギアに追加されました

クラブブランドはクラブに特定の特性を追加し、同じブランドのクラブをバッグに入れるこ
とで追加のボーナスが得られます
ブランドには特別な特徴があり、特定のブランドのクラブに固有のボーナスを提供します

クラブの制限は、ドライバーとパターの両方に存在します
ドライバーはティーからのみ使用可能です

パターはグリーンからのみ使用可能です
クラブは地形に応じてバフとデバフを受けます
ティー＆グリーン：変更なし

フェアウェイ：総距離5%バフ
セミラフ：総距離20%デバフ

ラフ：総距離40%デバフ

Missions Design Document

Brief 

Mission Goals

Mission List

Replaying Missions

Mission Types

Tutorial

Club

Distance

Precision

Hazards

Elements

Mission Rewards 

Brief 

The Missions mode of GOLFIN acts as one of the game’s primary gameplay modes (Only mode

available on Release). In this mode, players will take part in solo gameplay in order to complete 

goals and earn rewards to help them develop their characters and equipment. 

Missions are completed in a linear fashion, and more will be added as time progresses in order

to allow for a constant stream of content to keep players engaged.

Mission Goals

Up to 3 Goals can be combined with a Hole, Start Location and Wind Conditions to create

Missions. 

All goals are  validated AFTER the player finishes a course. This means the player has to sink the

ball with all goals fulfilled for the mission to be considered Completed.

Mission List

A Mission List, listing of all missions, is available an can be accessed from the Navigation Bar.

Missions are completed in a linear fashion, so to unlock the next mission, the previous one has

to have been completed before.

They are listed in order of difficulty, which new difficulty tabs unlocking in linear fashion as well. 

140



By default, the next available mission is always shown in the Main Screen and can be selected it

by simply tapping Play. 

Replaying Missions

Missions can be replayed as many times as the player wants from the Mission List . However, its

rewards diminish after the first time they beat .

Mission Types

Tutorial

Designed to teach the player a game mechanic. Example:

Description: Sink the ball with the putter in 2 shots or less

Start Position: Green

Club

These missions focus on using a specific club to fulfill the objective. Example:

Club Challenge

Objective: Hit the target area with a specific club.

Golf Club: 3-iron.

Target Area: A small green area surrounded by water hazards.

Distance

These missions are focused on driving the ball or hitting long distances, sometimes with added

challenges like wind or obstacles.  Example:vvvvvv

Long Drive

Objective: Drive the ball the furthest distance within a specific target zone.

Golf Club: Driver.

Target Area: A long fairway with a narrow landing zone near a water hazard.

Windy Conditions

Objective: Adjust for windy conditions while maintaining accuracy over a long distance.

Golf Club: 5-iron.

Target Area: A medium-sized green with varying wind speeds.

Precision

These missions require careful planning, managing multiple shots to reach a target or overcome

obstacles.  Examples:

141



Par 3 Precision

Objective: Get as close to the pin as possible within a set number of shots.

Golf Club: 7-iron.

Target Area: A large circular green with the flagstick in the middle, surrounded by bunkers.

The Fairway Gauntlet

Objective: Hit multiple fairway targets without missing.

Golf Club: 4-iron.

Target Area: Multiple targets spaced evenly across a fairway, with rough and hazards in

between.

Hazards

These missions involve risky situations like water hazards, narrow landing areas, or precision

shots where failure is likely if not executed properly. Examples:

Objective: Hit the target area with a specific club, navigating risks.

Golf Club: 3-iron.

Target Area: A small green surrounded by water hazards.

Objective: Get the ball out of a sand trap and into the hole in a specific number of shots.

Golf Club: Sand wedge.

Target Area: A slightly elevated green surrounded by hazards.

Objective: Get as close to the pin as possible within a set number of shots.

Golf Club: 7-iron.

Target Area: A large green with flagstick in the middle, surrounded by bunkers.

Elements

These missions require precise control of the ball, often with added factors like wind, elevation,

or different yardages.

Objective: Adjust for windy conditions while maintaining accuracy.

Golf Club: 5-iron.

Target Area: Medium-sized green with varying wind speeds.

Mission Rewards 

The game can offer up to 3 rewards per mission. Rewards change if the mission is re-played

after being cleared. We will not have all reward types for Release but we should be ready to add

different rewards post-lunch.

Reward Points 

142



Repair Kit

Premium Repair Kit
