Usage:

IAPOrderItemResponse.product_category  - Product item in IAP purchase response

ProductDetailsEntrySchema.product_category  - Product display information

OrderHistoryEntrySchema.product_category  - Purchase history entry

GrantedItemSchema.product_category  - Granted item information

555



Security and Idempotency

1. Duplicate Purchase Prevention

Prevent duplicate purchases using transaction ID.

Database constraint: UNIQUE(provider, transaction_id)  on payment_receipt  table

Returns 409 Conflict  error if transaction ID has already been processed

2. Receipt Verification

Apple App Store

Uses Apple verifyReceipt API

Auto-detects Sandbox/Production environment

Sends Base64-encoded receipt data

Endpoint: Set via APPLE_VERIFY_RECEIPT_ENDPOINT  environment variable

Google Play

1. Signature Verification

Verify signature using RSA PKCS#1 v1.5 + SHA1

Uses public key obtained from Google Play Console

2. Developer API Verification

Uses Workload Identity Federation (AWS)

Calls purchases.products.get  endpoint

Confirms purchaseState = 0  (Purchased)

3. Idempotency Guarantee

Prevents duplicate Payment creation with idempotency_key = user_id + transaction_id

Entire transaction executes atomically

Automatic rollback on errors

4. Transaction Management

All database operations execute within a single transaction.

Processing sequence:

1. Product verification

2. Duplicate check

3. Order creation

4. Payment creation

5. Receipt creation

6. Receipt verification ← Rollback if fails here

7. Entitlement granting

8. Status update

9. Log recording

10. Commit

556



Error Codes

HTTP Status Description Action

200 OK Success -

400 Bad Request Invalid request or Check request
receipt verification parameters
failed

401 Unauthorized Authentication error Check JWT token

404 Not Found Product does not exist Check
product_package_mast
er_id

409 Conflict Duplicate purchase Already processed
(normal)

500 Internal Server Server error Contact support
Error

Rate Limiting

Rate limiting is not currently implemented. Implementation is planned for the future.

Multi-language Support

Overview

The IAP API supports internationalization (i18n) for product-related content through the Accept-Language
header.

Supported Languages

Language Code Language Region

en-US English United States (default)

ja-JP Japanese Japan

How It Works

Request Header:

1 Accept-Language: ja-JP
2

Localized Fields:

The following fields are automatically localized based on the Accept-Language  header:

Endpoint Localized Fields Description

557



/api/v1/game/p name , info Product package name

roduct/listin and description

g

/api/v1/game/o name Product name in

rder/history purchase history

Translation Mechanism:

1. Translation Lookup:

Translations are stored in the localization_translation  table

Linked to the localization_language  table via language_code

Associated with product_package_master  records via record_id

2. Fallback Behavior:

If a translation is not available for the requested language, the system falls back to the default value from the 

product_package_master  table

This ensures that content is always returned, even if translations are incomplete

3. Supported Fields:

name : Product package name

description : Product package description (returned as info  in responses)

Example Request:

1 GET /api/v1/game/product/listing HTTP/1.1
2 Host: api.golfin.game
3 Authorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>
4 Accept-Language: ja-JP
5

Example Response (Japanese):

1 {
2 "products": [
3 {
4 "product_package_master_id": 123,
5 "name": "ゴールデンチケット10枚パック",
6 "info": "ゴールデンチケットを10枚即座に入手",
7 "image_url":

"https://cdn.golfin.game/products/golden_ticket_10.png",
8 "product_category": 1,
9 "purchase_limit": -1,
10 "sale_end_period": null,
11 "quantity_per_package": 10
12 }
13 ]
14 }
15

Best Practices

1. Always Include Accept-Language Header:

Include the Accept-Language  header in all requests to ensure users receive content in their preferred

language

558



Unity clients should automatically set this header based on the device's language settings

2. Handle Missing Translations:

The API will always return content, even if translations are missing

Display default (English) content gracefully if necessary

3. Language Code Format:

Use the full locale format: language-REGION  (e.g., ja-JP , not just ja )

The API may accept short codes (e.g., ja ) but full locale codes are recommended for consistency

Technical Details

Database Schema:

1 -- Localization tables
2 CREATE TABLE localization_language (
3 id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
4 language_code VARCHAR(10) UNIQUE NOT NULL,  -- e.g., 'en', 'ja',

'ko'
5 language_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
6 );
7

8 CREATE TABLE localization_translation (
9 id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
10 language_code VARCHAR(10) REFERENCES

localization_language(language_code),
11 table_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,           -- e.g.,

'product_package_master'
12 record_id INTEGER NOT NULL,                  -- Foreign key to the

target table
13 field_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,            -- e.g., 'name',

'description'
14 translated_text TEXT NOT NULL
15 );
16

Translation Function:

The backend uses the load_product_translations_by_code()  helper function to retrieve

translations:

1 def load_product_translations_by_code(
2 db: Session, 
3 language_code: str, 
4 product_ids: list[int]
5 ) -> Dict[int, Dict[str, str]]:
6 """
7 Returns: {product_id: {field_name: translated_text}}
8 Example: {123: {"name": "ゴールデンチケット10枚パック", "description":

"ゴールデンチケットを10枚即座に入手"}}
9 """

2. 購入前価格検証

GET /api/v1/game/order/price_validation

ユーザーがアプリ内で購入ボタンをタップする前に、商品パッケージが現在販売可能かどうかを検証します。

設計思想：

価格変更は別の product_package_master_id を使用して管理されます

App Storeの価格変更は反映に遅延が発生する可能性があります

バックエンドが販売期間を確実に制御し、意図しない価格での販売を防止します

データ構造が販売期間管理を product_package_master_id に紐付けています

このエンドポイントは、指定されたパッケージが現在販売可能期間内かどうかのみを検証します

金額は検証しません（異なるパッケージIDは異なる商品として扱われます）

リクエスト

ヘッダー：

1 Authorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>
2

クエリパラメータ：

パラメータ 型 必須 説明

product_pa integer ✓ 検証する商品パ

ckage_mast ッケージマスタ
ーID

er_id

例：

1 GET /api/v1/game/order/price_validation?product_package_master_id=123
2

レスポンス

成功： 200 OK

1 {
2 "is_valid": true,
3 "product_package_master_id": 123,
4 "name": "ゴールデンチケット10枚パック",
5 "sale_end_period": "2025-12-31T23:59:59Z"
6 }
7

レスポンスフィールド：

フィールド 型 説明

is_valid boolean 商品が現在販売可能か
どうか

562



product_packag integer 商品パッケージマスタ

e_master_id ーID

name string 商品名

sale_end_perio string | null 販売終了日時（ISO

d 8601形式）、終了日が
ない場合はnull

検証チェック項目

このエンドポイントは以下を検証します：

1. 商品パッケージの存在

指定された product_package_master_id が存在するか

is_active = true であるか

2. 販売可能期間チェック

GAMEチャネルで販売可能か（ is_sellable = true ）

現在時刻が有効期間内か（ effective_start_at <= now <= effective_end_at ）

価格エントリが存在するか
3. 検証しない項目

ユーザー支払金額（ paid_price_amount ）の妥当性

購入制限（ purchase_limit ）

在庫状況

ユースケース

1 1. ユーザーがストア内で商品を閲覧
2 2. ユーザーが購入ボタンをタップ
3 3. [このエンドポイントを呼び出し] ← 現在販売可能かチェック
4 4. is_valid = trueの場合のみ、ストアのIAP購入フローを開始
5 5. ストア購入完了後、/api/v1/game/order/iapを呼び出し
6

エラーケース

is_valid = falseの場合：

1 {
2 "is_valid": false,
3 "product_package_master_id": 123,
4 "name": "ゴールデンチケット10枚パック",
5 "sale_end_period": null
6 }
7

このレスポンスの理由：

商品パッケージが存在しない

商品が非アクティブ（ is_active = false ）

販売期間外

GAMEチャネルで販売不可
価格エントリが存在しない

563



対応方法：

ユーザーに「この商品は現在利用できません」というメッセージを表示

商品一覧を更新して最新の利用可能な商品を表示

エラーレスポンス

処理フロー

1. 商品パッケージの存在確認

567



2. トランザクションIDの重複チェック
3. アクティブな価格情報の取得（GAMEチャネル）

4. 注文ヘッダー作成（ステータス：PENDING）
5. 注文明細作成

6. 決済レコード作成
7. レシート作成
8. レシート検証

Apple：verifyReceipt APIを呼び出し
Google：署名検証 + Developer APIを呼び出し

9. エンタイトルメント付与（フェーズ1：TICKETのみ）
10. 注文/決済ステータス更新（COMPLETED / CAPTURED）
11. トランザクションログ記録

12. コミット

エラーが発生した場合は自動的にロールバックされます。

データモデル

値 説明

値 説明

APPLE Apple In-App Purchase

GOOGLE Google Play Billing

値 説明

CANCELED キャンセル

値 説明

BAG 6 バッグ

使用箇所：

IAPOrderItemResponse.product_category  - IAP購入レスポンスの商品アイテム

ProductDetailsEntrySchema.product_category  - 商品表示情報

OrderHistoryEntrySchema.product_category  - 購入履歴エントリ

GrantedItemSchema.product_category  - 付与されたアイテム情報

セキュリティと冪等性

1. 重複購入の防止

トランザクションIDを使用して重複購入を防止します。

データベース制約： payment_receipt テーブルに UNIQUE(provider, transaction_id)

トランザクションIDが既に処理済みの場合は 409 Conflict エラーを返します

2. レシート検証

Apple App Store

Apple verifyReceipt APIを使用
Sandbox/Production環境を自動検出

Base64エンコードされたレシートデータを送信

エンドポイント： APPLE_VERIFY_RECEIPT_ENDPOINT 環境変数で設定

Google Play

1. 署名検証

RSA PKCS#1 v1.5 + SHA1を使用して署名を検証

571



Google Play Consoleから取得した公開鍵を使用
2. Developer API検証

Workload Identity Federation（AWS）を使用

purchases.products.get エンドポイントを呼び出し

purchaseState = 0 （購入済み）を確認

3. 冪等性の保証

idempotency_key = user_id + transaction_id で重複Payment作成を防止

トランザクション全体がアトミックに実行されます
エラー時は自動的にロールバック

4. トランザクション管理

すべてのデータベース操作は単一トランザクション内で実行されます。

処理シーケンス：

1. 商品検証
2. 重複チェック
3. 注文作成

4. 決済作成
5. レシート作成

6. レシート検証 ← ここで失敗した場合はロールバック
7. エンタイトルメント付与
8. ステータス更新

9. ログ記録
10. コミット

エラーコード

HTTPステータス 説明 対応

200 OK 成功 -

400 Bad Request 無効なリクエストまた リクエストパラメータ
はレシート検証失敗 を確認

401 Unauthorized 認証エラー JWTトークンを確認

404 Not Found 商品が存在しない product_package_mast
er_idを確認

409 Conflict 重複購入 既に処理済み（正常）

500 Internal Server サーバーエラー サポートに連絡
Error

レート制限

現在、レート制限は実装されていません。将来的に実装予定です。

多言語サポート

概要

IAP APIは、 Accept-Language ヘッダーを通じて商品関連コンテンツの国際化（i18n）をサポートしています。

サポート言語

言語コード 言語 地域

en-US 英語 アメリカ合衆国（デフ
ォルト）

ja-JP 日本語 日本

動作方法

リクエストヘッダー：

1 Accept-Language: ja-JP
2

ローカライズされるフィールド：

以下のフィールドは Accept-Language ヘッダーに基づいて自動的にローカライズされます：

エンドポイント ローカライズされるフ 説明
ィールド

/api/v1/game/p name , info 商品パッケージ名と説

roduct/listin 明

g

/api/v1/game/o name 購入履歴内の商品名

rder/history

翻訳メカニズム：

1. 翻訳の検索：

翻訳は localization_translation テーブルに保存されています

language_code を介して localization_language テーブルにリンクされています

record_id を介して product_package_master レコードに関連付けられています

2. フォールバック動作：

リクエストされた言語の翻訳が利用できない場合、システムは product_package_master テーブルのデ
フォルト値にフォールバックします
これにより、翻訳が不完全な場合でもコンテンツが常に返されることを保証します

573



3. サポートされるフィールド：

name ：商品パッケージ名

description ：商品パッケージ説明（レスポンスでは info として返されます）

リクエスト例：

1 GET /api/v1/game/product/listing HTTP/1.1
2 Host: api.golfin.game
3 Authorization: Bearer <JWT_TOKEN>
4 Accept-Language: ja-JP
5

レスポンス例（日本語）：

1 {
2 "products": [
3 {
4 "product_package_master_id": 123,
5 "name": "100ジェムパック",
6 "info": "100個のジェムを即座に入手",
7 "image_url": "https://cdn.golfin.game/products/gems_100.png",
8 "product_category": 1,
9 "purchase_limit": -1,
10 "sale_end_period": null,
11 "quantity_per_package": 100
12 }
13 ]
14 }
15

ベストプラクティス

1. 常にAccept-Languageヘッダーを含める：

ユーザーが希望する言語でコンテンツを受け取れるよう、すべてのリクエストに Accept-Language ヘッダ
ーを含めてください

Unityクライアントは、デバイスの言語設定に基づいてこのヘッダーを自動的に設定する必要があります
2. 翻訳欠落の処理：

APIは翻訳が欠落している場合でも常にコンテンツを返します

必要に応じてデフォルト（英語）コンテンツを適切に表示してください
3. 言語コードの形式：

完全なロケール形式を使用してください： language-REGION （例： ja-JP 、単なる ja ではなく）

APIは短いコード（例： ja ）も受け入れる可能性がありますが、一貫性のために完全なロケールコードを推奨し
ます

技術詳細

データベーススキーマ：

1 -- ローカリゼーションテーブル
2 CREATE TABLE localization_language (
3 id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
4 language_code VARCHAR(10) UNIQUE NOT NULL,  -- 例：'en', 'ja',

'ko'
5 language_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
6 );
7

8 CREATE TABLE localization_translation (
9 id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
10 language_code VARCHAR(10) REFERENCES

localization_language(language_code),

574



11 table_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,           --
例：'product_package_master'

12 record_id INTEGER NOT NULL,                  -- ターゲットテーブルへ
の外部キー

13 field_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,            -- 例：'name',
'description'

14 translated_text TEXT NOT NULL
15 );
16

翻訳関数：

バックエンドは load_product_translations_by_code() ヘルパー関数を使用して翻訳を取得します：

1 def load_product_translations_by_code(
2 db: Session, 
3 language_code: str, 
4 product_ids: list[int]
5 ) -> Dict[int, Dict[str, str]]:
6 """
7 戻り値：{product_id: {field_name: translated_text}}
8 例：{123: {"name": "100ジェムパック", "description": "100個のジェムを
即座に入手"}}

9 """

In-App Purchase (IAP) Sequence Diagram v1

Overview

Sequence diagram for Golfin's In-App Purchase (IAP) implementation. Shows the complete IAP purchase flow from

Unity client.

Main Flow: IAP Purchase Processing

Pre-purchase Price Validation Flow

1 sequenceDiagram
2 participant Unity as Unity Client
3 participant API as FastAPI Backend
4 participant PriceVal as PriceValidationService
5 participant DB as Database
6

7 Note over Unity,DB: Validation on purchase button tap (GET
/api/v1/game/order/price_validation)

8

9 Unity->>Unity: User taps purchase button
10

11 Unity->>+API: GET /api/v1/game/order/price_validation?
product_package_master_id=123

12

13 API->>+PriceVal: validate_price_by_package_id()
14

15 PriceVal->>DB: Search ProductPackageMaster
16 Note right of PriceVal: is_active = true
17 DB-->>PriceVal: product_package
18

19 alt Product not found or inactive
20 PriceVal-->>API: is_valid = false
21 API-->>Unity: 200 OK (is_valid: false)
22 Unity->>Unity: Display "Not available" error
23 else Product exists
24 PriceVal->>DB: Search ProductPrice
25 Note right of PriceVal: GAME channel,<br/>is_sellable = true,

<br/>within effective period
26 DB-->>PriceVal: price_entries
27

28 alt No sellable price found
29 PriceVal-->>API: is_valid = false
30 API-->>Unity: 200 OK (is_valid: false)
31 Unity->>Unity: Display "Not available" error
32 else Sellable
33 PriceVal-->>-API: is_valid = true, sale_end_period
34 API-->>-Unity: 200 OK (is_valid: true)
35 Unity->>Unity: Start store's IAP purchase flow
36 end
37 end

State Transition Diagram

580



1 stateDiagram-v2
2 [*] --> PENDING: Order created
3 PENDING --> COMPLETED: Receipt verification success
4 PENDING --> FAILED: Receipt verification failed
5 COMPLETED --> [*]
6 FAILED --> [*]
7

8 note right of PENDING
9 - Order created
10 - Payment created
11 - Receipt saved
12 end note
13

14 note right of COMPLETED
15 - Receipt verification success
16 - Items granted
17 - Payment Captured
18 end note
19

20 note right of FAILED
21 - Receipt verification failed
22 - Transaction rolled back
23 end note
24

Key Points

1. Pre-purchase Price Validation

Call /api/v1/game/order/price_validation  when user taps purchase button

Check if product package is currently available for sale

Does NOT validate amount (price changes use different product_package_master_id by design)

Only start store's IAP purchase flow if is_valid = true

Prevents purchases outside of sale period due to timing lag

2. Idempotency Guarantee

Prevent duplicate purchases with transaction_id

Prevent duplicate Payment creation with idempotency_key  (user_id + transaction_id)

Database constraint: UNIQUE(provider, transaction_id)  on payment_receipt

3. Transaction Management

All operations within a single DB transaction

Automatic ROLLBACK on errors

Proper rollback on receipt verification failure

4. Receipt Verification

Apple: verifyReceipt API (Base64-encoded receipt)

Google:

Signature verification (RSA PKCS#1 v1.5 + SHA1)

Developer API (via Workload Identity Federation)

5. Entitlement Granting

Phase 1: TICKET category only

Uses ProductMaster's reference_table/reference_master_id to resolve GameTicket

581



Creates UserInventory and UserTicket records

6. Price Resolution

Dynamic pricing system (ProductPrice/ProductPriceEntry)

Only sellable prices in GAME channel

Uses prices within effective period (effective_start_at <= now <= effective_end_at)

7. Unity Compatibility

Response format designed to match existing Unity-side classes

gacha_result  field name (contains IAPOrderEntitlements)

8. Product Category Mapping

The product_category  field is mapped with the following numbers:

Category Number Description

TICKET 1 Ticket

CLUB 2 Club

BALL 3 Ball

CHARACTER 4 Character

ITEM 5 Item

BAG 6 Bag

2D Assets Guidelines

Texture Height and width

Dimensions should be in the

power of 2

that is, 2, 4, 8, 16,

32, 64, 128, 256,

512, 1024, 2048

pixels (px), and

so on

Textures do not

have to be

square; the width

can be different

from height

Target Device iPhone 13 1170x2532 9:19.5

Resolution

Screen UI

Resolution

Import style guide

Naming should follow PascalCase 

Format :S_ScreenName_AssetName

Assets should group into  sprite sheets

Format : TP_AssetName

Assets should group into Sprite atlas

Format : Atlas_AssetName

584



3D Textures : T_AssetName_TypeName

Example : T_Skin_Albedo

3D Materials : M_AssetName

Example : M_Skin

3D Meshes : MESH_AssetName

Example : MESH_Body

3D Animations : ANIM_AssetName

Example : ANIM_Male, ANIM_JapaneseMale, ANIM_Female

Use 9-patch images whenever possible

Always add a mockup/ref image with the UI assets.

Disclamer

Even if we strive to standardize our processes, art and its creation is a collaborative effort

so we have to allow for flexibility and “back and forths” if we want to achieve the best

results. 

Constructive criticism and feedback should always be welcomed as long as they are

respectfully given, which does not mean that every opinion needs to be acted upon.

Game Update Flow
Miro Flowchart

Case 1 (When new build is required)

1. Merge working branches to Develop

2. Update the build version and ID 

3. Set the Game Environment to Dev

4. Download “addressables_content_state.bin” from the last version in S3 bucket

5. Build Addressables and upload to the Dev S3

6. Create Android and iOS builds

7. Upload to the store as Test release

8. Invalidate the CloudFront Cache

9. Smoke Test

10. Merge Develop branch to Release Branch

11. Increment the build version by keeping the build Id same

a. In Android, build version is located in the player settings

b. In iOS, build version is located in the x-code

12. Set the Game Environment to Production

13. Use same “addressables_content_state.bin” as Dev builds

14. Build Addressables and upload to the Dev S3

15. Create Android and iOS builds

16. Invalidate the CloudFront Cache

17. Upload to Test Flight and test the Addressable download and Authentication

18. Upload the builds to the store for review

19. Create a branch in Plastic with release version

Case 2 (When no build is required)

1. Merge working branches to Develop

2. Set the Game Environment to Dev

3. Download “addressables_content_state.bin” from the last version in S3 bucket

599



4. Build Addressables and upload to the Dev S3

5. Invalidate the CloudFront Cache

6. Smoke Test

7. Merge Develop branch to Release Branch

8. Merge Release Branch to the branch with latest release version

9. Set the Game Environment to Production

10. Use same “addressables_content_state.bin” as Dev builds

11. Build Addressables and upload to the Dev S3

12. Invalidate the CloudFront Cache

600



Guideline for Communication Channels (wip)

Guideline: Communication Channels

By Rob Ross 2024/05/08

Aim

Communication is essential for any successful project. 

This first draft of the Communication Channel guideline will try to help manage multiple

communication channels effectively and efficiently. How can you ensure that your team and

stakeholders are on the same page, avoid information overload, and choose the right tools for

the right purpose

Index

I. Introduction

II. Wonderwall Communication channels

I. Introduction

Reference material:

https://www.linkedin.com/advice/1/what-some-best-practices-using-multiple-communication

What are some best practices for using multiple communication channels in a project?

Communication is essential for any successful project, but it can also be challenging to manage

multiple communication channels effectively and efficiently. How can you ensure that your team

and stakeholders are on the same page, avoid information overload, and choose the right tools

for the right purpose? In this article, we will share some best practices for using multiple

communication channels in a project, based on the principles of communication channel

effectiveness and efficiency.

Define your communication plan

A communication plan is a document that outlines the goals, objectives, strategies, methods,

frequency, and responsibilities of communication in a project. It helps you to align your

601



communication with your project scope, schedule, budget, quality, and risks. A communication

plan also helps you to identify and prioritize your communication channels, based on their

effectiveness and efficiency.

Choose your communication channels wisely

Communication channels are the means or modes of transmitting information in a project, such

as email, phone, video conference, chat, social media, or face-to-face. Each channel has its own

advantages and disadvantages, depending on the context, audience, and message. For

instance, email is a good channel for formal, written, and asynchronous communication, but it

can be slow, impersonal, and prone to misinterpretation. Video conferences are a good channel

for visual, verbal, and synchronous communication, yet it can be costly, complex, and

distracting. To choose your communication channels wisely, you need to take into account the

purpose and goal of your communication, the complexity and urgency of your message, the size

and diversity of your audience, the availability and accessibility of your channel, and the

feedback and interaction you expect or require.

Balance your communication channels

Using multiple communication channels in a project can increase your communication

effectiveness and efficiency, but it can also create some challenges, such as information

overload, inconsistency, and fragmentation. To balance your communication channels, you need

to use the right channel for the right message, the appropriate channel frequency, consistent

channel content, and integrated channel management. Match your channel to your purpose,

complexity, urgency, audience, availability, and feedback. Communicate as often as needed, but

not more than necessary, and avoid duplication or redundancy. Adapt the same information to

the channel format, style, and tone. Use a central platform or tool to organize, store, and access

your communication channels, and keep them updated and synchronized.

Evaluate your communication channels

Using multiple communication channels in a project is not a one-time decision, but an ongoing

process that requires constant evaluation and improvement. To ensure the effectiveness and

efficiency of your communication channels, you need to define communication metrics, collect

data, analyze the data, and make improvements based on the feedback and results you receive.

Identify indicators and criteria that reflect your communication goals, objectives, and strategies,

such as reach, engagement, satisfaction, quality, or impact. Gather information and evidence

that show your communication performance, such as surveys, analytics, reports, or testimonials.

Interpret and compare your communication data, and identify the strengths, weaknesses,

602



opportunities, and threats of your communication channels. Finally, implement the changes and

actions that enhance your communication effectiveness and efficiency, and address the issues

and challenges you face.

II. Wonderwall Communication channels

The following is based on the latest understanding of the channels selected

When a production starts:

+ Define the channels for the team members to communicate

+ Define the purpose for each channels

1) Figma

+ Project UI UX design

+ Project UI UX comments

2) Google chat

+ External Team Communication

When addressing a specific person in a channel, @name_person

Add a title to the purpose of the post (eg: Re: feedback for this ...)

Add reaction Thumb Up to acknowledge it was read

Reply in the post’s thread to keep it in one place/tidy  

3) Emails

+ …

4) Calls

+ create desktop video recording to make video presentation

(or in different offices), some challenges have arisen regarding communication via digital

channels. Follow these rules on time limits for responses to stay on top of everyone’s needs.

message stating so.

message stating so.

Guideline for projects postmortem/review/retrospective

Guideline: Postmortem Meeting

By Rob Ross 2024/04/16

Aim

A project postmortem/review/retrospective meeting is a meeting held after a project's

completion (or in some cases mid project)

The main goal is to reflect on how the project went and identify what can be changed moving

forward to create a more streamlined process. 

Index

I. Introduction

II. Running postmortem files templates

III. Rhythm Dummy Game Post Mortem (sample)

I. Introduction

(Based on the resource: 6 steps for a successful project postmortem meeting. 

https://asana.com/resources/project-post-mortem-tips)

Postmortem meetings are meetings you hold once a project is over. This meeting is a chance for

your project team to identify the things that went well throughout the project and the things that

could have gone differently. It can help the team to improve processes for future projects.

Applying your learnings from past projects can also help prevent mistakes and mitigate risk. etc

Note: Postmortem meetings can go by a few different names. Project debrief, Retrospective,

Project recap, Wrap-up meeting, Lessons learned meeting

Steps:

1. Meet within a few days of project completion

2. Send a pre-meeting questionnaire

Sample pre-meeting questions:

What are three things that went well during this project?

What are three things that did not go well during this project?

609



Do you have any suggestions on how we can improve for the next project?

3. Share a postmortem meeting agenda:

Introduction (2.5 minutes)

Team shoutouts (5 minutes)

What went well (5 minutes)

What could have gone better (5 minutes)

Suggestions for next project (5 minutes)

Wrap up (2.5 minutes)

4. Assign a dedicated note taker and moderator

5. Host the meeting

6. Send a meeting recap to attendees

7. Backup

II. Running postmortem files templates samples

1) Email to all team members for the meeting:

Dear Team

This email is about: Post Mortem for the Rhythm Dummy Game project

Date: Thursday 3 August

Time: Same as usual weekly team meetings

Location: Wherever you are!!!!

Meeting link (same as you google meet): meet.google.com/rbq-tdgw-yss

Meeting agenda (30mn):

Introduction (2.5 minutes)

Team shoutouts (5 minutes)

What went well (5 minutes)

What could have gone better (5 minutes)

Suggestions for next project (5 minutes)

Wrap up (2.5 minutes)

Please just answer those 3 questions:

What are three things that went well during this project?

What are three things that did not go well during this project?

Do you have any suggestions on how we can improve for the next project?

610



And that is it!!!

Speak to you soon and on Thursday anyway

Thanks you

Jon Dow

Note: Now, if you want to learn more about post mortem, look online!!!

The following is my summary of an online article. It is short, so if you are interested by the topic

but just need a rough idea, that should do:

6 steps for a successful project postmortem meeting (See I. Introduction)

2) Excel entry form

Entry form for Mid-Project Retrospective

Original file link HERE

Thanks

Rob Ross

ChatGPT review of the above:

Your post mortem project review seems well-structured and thoughtful.

It's great that you're reflecting on both the pros and cons of the project to identify areas for

improvement.

Here's a breakdown of your points:

Pros:

Good Teamwork: Strong teamwork is crucial for project success, and it's great that you

acknowledge this as a strength.

Meeting Deliverables: Successfully meeting project deliverables is a significant

accomplishment, especially for a first-time project with no loose ends.

Communication Channels: Effective communication is key in any project, and having clear

communication channels is a positive aspect.

Creativity: Creativity can lead to innovative solutions and outcomes in projects.

Team Management: Properly managing tasks and time is essential for project efficiency.

Educational Vision: Maintaining a clear educational vision throughout the project is important

for aligning with project goals and objectives.

Cons:

Time Zone Differences: Time zone disparities can indeed create challenges in addressing

issues promptly.

Inclusion Outside Core Team: Expanding inclusion beyond the core team can bring in fresh

perspectives and ideas.

Missed Game Difficulty: Recognizing and addressing issues like game difficulty early in the

project can help prevent major problems later on.

Information Overload: Managing the flow of information is crucial, as too much information or

unclear information can lead to confusion and inefficiency.

Communication Channels: It seems like there may be some redundancy or confusion in your

communication channels that need to be addressed.

613



Lack of Experience: Lack of experience can be a hurdle in project management, but it's also

an opportunity for growth and learning.

Conclusions:

Team Weaknesses: Recognizing the team's weaknesses, such as not knowing the target

audience well enough, is an important step in improving future projects. Bringing in external

perspectives can be valuable.

Information Overload: Implementing strategies to manage information overload and setting

clear guidelines for information sharing are essential.

Communication Channels: Defining and standardizing communication channels and their

rules from the beginning can enhance project communication and coordination.

Overall, your review demonstrates a commitment to learning from your project experiences and

making improvements for future endeavors. Implementing the suggested changes and lessons

learned should help your team become even more successful in future projects.

Jira Task Management Guideline

Golfin project will follow Agile project management system. Where execution of tasks will be

very flexible. Sprint will be of 1 week duration. Every week Monday 7pm will be start of the new

sprint. 

Rules to follow

1. Create Tickets only of type “Task”

2. Anyone can create the tickets and assign it to themselves or to anyone it addresses to.

3. Assign appropriate priority to the tickets.

4. By default Created tickets should be placed in the backlog section.

5. At the start of each new sprint, tickets will be to moved to the new sprint and set the status to

either “To Planning” or “To Do”.

6. Before starting to work on a ticket fill the “Due Date” field.

7. For any dependency of your ticket, use the comment section of the ticket. Always use

Mentions when you write a comment.

8. After completion of the ticket, assign the ticket to the reviewer to review the ticket and vice

versa.

9. Screenshot attached below represents the workflow of the tickets. 

Workflow Diagram of Development cycle

621



Note

*Subject to Change based on needs of organization.

*Any suggestions are welcome for discussion.

622



GOLFIN GAME JIRA Bug Report Guidelines

Creating a Bug Report

This is a brief explanation on how to properly report a bug in Jira using.

1. Open the Project Backlog.

2. At the top of the screen, you will see a + CREATE  button (color’s might differ in your Jira if you are

not using Dark Mode).

3. The Create an Ticket screen will pop-up.

4. Select Bug as Work Type, this will display the proper fields for you to fill in.

623



5. Fill as many of the fields as possible.

a. Summary (Mandatory)

Brief description of the bug.

b. Priority

Priority should be handled by the Project Manager or Director, only change it if you are

100% sure it fits the below criteria :

i. Highest: The game crashes or all progress is blocked.

ii. High: A feature doesn’t work.

iii. Medium: Affects functionality but have workarounds.

iv. Low: Visual issues that do not affect the game’s functionality.

v. Lowest: Trivial errors, typos, small graphical inaccuracies.

c. Current Behavior

How the game is behaving right now. Include videos/images whenever possible. 

d. Expected Behavior

How the game is supposed to work. Add links to design documentation here whenever

possible.

e. Reproduction Steps

A step by step guide to reproduce the issue. Be succinct but clear.

f. Reproduction Rate

How often does the bug occur, in % of times tested.

g. Device

Device that was use to test and find this issue (e.x. iPhone 15 Pro Max, Pixel 6, etc.)

h. Environment

If you know, whether the build points to Dev or Production environment.

i. Affects version

The version of the game you came across the bug

j. Fix version

The version of the game we expect the fix to be published in

k. Assignee

Who will take care of the issue. Leave Unassigned if you don’t know.

l. Reporter

The person who found the issue, in case the people trying to solve it need to reach out for

more info.

m. Linked work items

If the issue is related to another issue already in JIRA, use this to point to that issue and

624



choose the relationship.  

n. Sprint

In what sprint we will tackle the work. This should be used by the PM or Director only.

o. Description

This field is being deprecated. It’s here only so older bugs show their descriptions and will

be removed in the near future.

Bug Workflow

Once a bug is created, it should follow this workflow 

Bug Report is created

If bug is a Crash, Reporter should reach out to PM or Director via Slack with the issue link

Bug is assigned by PM or Director (or Reporter only if 100% of Assignee)

Assignee receives the bug with priority in their Sprint backlog

Assignee picks up the issue once their are done with all other higher priority bugs int heir

Sprint Backlog

If the bug does not belong to current Assignee, reassign and leave a comment about the

reasons

If no bugs remain for this Sprint, Assignee can take bugs from future sprint or directly from

the backlog in order of priority

If bug is duplicated Assignee sets it to Done. The Resolve Issue Screenwill appear  

Assignee sets Status to In Progress 

If more information is needed, Assignee leaves a comment with request for more

information using @ to notify the person who should provide it  

If no further work can be done without more information, Assignee  should reassign the

issue to the person who should provide it  

After solving the issue Assignee 

Change Build Version to the proper version 

Status to QA

Reassigns the issue to the PM or Director for QA

PM or Director reassigns to the proper assignee to do QA

Assignee tries to reproduce issue

If issue persists

Add current version to Affects versions 

Set Status to Reopened

625



Reassign issue to developer who worked on the issue before

Whenever the issue can’t be reproduced, Assignee sets status to Done. The Resolve Issue

Screen will appear.

Resolve Issue Screen
To finally close an bug, you will always have to go through the Resolve Issue screen. There are

only a few fields here to take into account:

Resolution

Done

The bug has been resolved

Won’t Do

It has been decided that nothing should be done about this bug (for example, it is working

as designed)

Duplicate

The issue is a duplicate of another issue and the other issue will be used as primary source

of info

Cannot Reproduce

The developer never managed to reproduce the issue

Fix Version

Only PM or Director should change this field

Assignee

Leave as is

Log Work

Ignore

Dates

Ignore

Build Version

Leave as is

Comment

For anything other than Done, please leave a comment

626



Build Steps iOS

Follow the below instructions to create iOS build from Unity and deploy to a test device without

uploading to the app store.

 Instructions

1. Create a Xcode build from Unity to a folder named Golfin[version] e.g Golfin0.1.8

2. Open the Xcode and fill the game detail under the Identity section as shown in the below

image

3. In Signing & Capabilities, assign the Provisioning profile created by Apple developers

account. 

4. To create a provisioning profile, you need a Apple developer account. For which ask

Nishikawa to invite you to the company’s developer account.

5. Register your test device under the devices as shown below

627



6. To register Device you require UDID, you can find the UDID in Mac’s system report as shown

below. 

Note: your test device needs to be connected to the Mac and developer mode enabled in the

device.

7. Go to Profiles, create a new profile of Type “Development“ and Platform “iOS“. Assign App ID

and a signed certificated as shown below. Save the provisioning profile in following naming

format [AppName]ProvisioningProfile[ExpireDate] e.g GolfinProvisioningProfile31July2025

8. Download the created provisioning profile and assign it in the Singing & Capabilities in the

Xcode.

9. From the top menu bar of the Xcode, select Product and select Archive to start the build

process.

628



10. From the Archive window, click on Distribute App and select Debugging and at last Click on

the Distribute button.

11. After a while you will get a window with the Build summary, Click on Export and save it in the

folder named Golfin[version]IPA e.g Golfin0.1.8IPA

12. Use Apple Configurator to install the IPA in the testing device.

629



Golfin GPS Development Environment Setup/Build Instructions

Follow the below instructions to setup the development environment for Golfin GPS, and to

create an iOS build from XCode to install the app on a physical iOS device.

Setting up the Golfin GPS Development Environment

Prerequisites

1. Git installation

Check Terminal: git --version

2. Flutter installation

Check Terminal: flutter --version

3. Minimum Xcode and Xcode Commandline tools installed

Check Flutter Doctor to see if requirements are met: flutter doctor

Clone Git Repository:

1. Clone Golfin GPS app repository with this command in the terminal. Change user_name and

token with your username and token with sufficient permission.

1 git clone <https://<user_name>>:<token>@github.com/Wonderwall-Inc/golfin_gps_app.git

2. Navigate the root application folder: cd golfin_gps_app

3. git checkout dev  for the latest updates

Setting up AWS Amplify

1. To connect with Amplify, an accessKeyId  and secretAccessKey  will be needed

for validation. Go to the AWS IAM console and create an access key as prerequisite. We will

need this access key/secret access key for the next steps.

630



2. Pull the Amplify config with amplify pull  and choose AWS access keys as the

validation option

3. Provide the access key and secret access key. The region as us-west-2 and choose the

Golfin app. Set the configuration store file location to ./lib/core/config/

Run Application in an iOS Emulator

1. Execute flutter run  and select iPhone 15 Pro (mobile)  from the list of

devices

**Note: If iPhone 15 Pro (mobile)  is not an option, try opening the iOS module

in XCode ( golfin_gps_app/ios/Runner.xcworkspace ) and running it as an

emulated iPhone 15 device.

631



Building Golfin GPS

1. To build Golfin GPS and install it on a physical device, you first need to register the iOS

device. First, you need the UDID. You can find the UDID by connecting the iOS device to the

Mac via USB and enabling developer mode on the iOS device. Then, open the System Report

app on the Mac, and find the Serial Number (aka the UDID).

2. Open the the Runner.xcworkspace  file with Xcode and fill the game detail under the

Identity section as shown in the below image

632



3. Login to the Apple Developer portal (ask Nishikawa-san for access if you need it), and setup

the device in the Devices list/tab.

633



4. After that, you can add the device to the Golfin GPS provisioning profile in the Profiles tab.

Select the GPS profile, and then click the “Edit” button in the Review Provisioning

Profiles  screen.

634



5. In the edit screen, you can see a list of certificates and devices for the profile.

6. Select your Apple certificate and device from this list, then update the date in the profile

name to be 1 year from today. So, if today is 2024/10/01, the name would become 

GolfinGPSProvisioningProfile01October2025 . 

635



7. After that, click “Save”, and download the newly updated provisioning profile.

8. Open Xcode, and import the provisioning profile under the Signing and

Capabilities  tab

9. With Xcode opened, select Product at the top of your Mac tray, and select Archive to start the

build process. 

636



10. Once that is finished, you should see the Archives window pop up, along with a “Distribute

App” button. Click on “Distribute App”, and then select the “Debugging” option, and click

“Distribute”.

637



11. Once it is finished, click on “Export” and save it to your machine.

12. To install the app on the iOS device, we will need to install Apple Configurator
from the App Store. 

13. With Apple Configurator opened, make sure your device is connected via USB, click the

“Add” button at the top of the application, select Apps, and then “Choose from my Mac…” at

the bottom left of the window.

14. Navigate to where you exported the distribution, and select the IPA file.

15. Thats it! The GPS app should now be installed on the iOS device.

641



UI Creation Process

The following steps outline the approved pipeline for UI creation, ensuring streamlined

collaboration and clarity across teams:

1. Initial Requirements

Responsibility: Nishikawa-san, Kouzuki-san, Lena

Set initial requirements 

2. Initial Wireframe 

Responsibility: Robin, Lena and Cesar

Robin, Lena and Cesar are responsible for creating the initial wireframe and design

requirements for the screen or element.

3. Creation of Vision and gathering of references

Responsibility: Cesar

Cesar will gather references and provide direction for Olga.

2. Sketch Creation

Responsibility: Olga

Olga creates a preliminary sketch based on the wireframe and requirements provided.

3. First Sketch Approval

Responsibility: Lena, Cesar

Lena and Cesar review and approve the sketch, ensuring alignment with design intent and

director’s vision. Cesar send the sketch to Nishikawa-san.

2. Final Sketch Approval

Responsibility: Nishikawa-san

Nishikawa-san and the engineering team review and approve the sketch, ensuring technical

feasibility and alignment with design intent.

2. Final Design & Asset Handover

Responsibility: Robin

Robin finalizes the design and assets, prepares the data for handover, and ensures all

deliverables are complete.

642



3. Final Approval

Responsibility: Lena, Cesar, Nishikawa-san

First Lena and Cesar check the result of Robin work. Then Cesar send them to Nishikawa-

san. Nishikawa-san gives final approval for the completed design and assets.

4. Implementation

Responsibility: Engineering Team

Engineers implement the approved design into the project.

Each step must be completed and approved before moving on to the next to maintain design

consistency and implementation quality.

643



Pipeline and Standards

The aim of this document is to provide some rules to manage the project. The rules:

All variable must follow the camel case notation beginning with a lowercase.

Eg: bool isVisible = true;

Property class or stuct variable names must follow Pascal case notation.

All function names, records and class names must follow the Pascal case notation beginning
with an Upper case.

Eg: void UpdateCharacterAnimation(float deltaTime)

Member variable names must begin with lowercase 'm'. 
Eg: int mNumberOfCharacters = 0;

Property accessor names should begin with lowercase 'p'. 
Eg: int pCurrentRank {get; set;}

Function input parameter must be tagged p_ to differentiate from local variables.

Eg: private void HitBall(LaunchParameters p_parameters)

Variables exposed in scripts for editing in Unity's inspector can be either public or private
(preferred). Private variables must be tagged with [SerializeField] and begin with an
underscore ‘m_'. Public variables must begin with '_’

Eg: [SerializeField] private float m_MaxAcceleration = 10.0f;Eg: public float _MaxAcceleration
= 10.0f;

Any UI related class file or class name should be prefixed with “UI”. 

Eg: public class UICharacterEditor : UI

Any network related class file or class name should be prefixed with “Net_”. 

Eg: public class Net_PlayerController

When creating a prefab, prefix Pf to the name. 

Eg: PfUIInventory

Constants and Enums should be all uppercase and words must be separated by an
underscore.

Eg: public const string DEFAULT_NAME = “John Doe”;

Remove all warnings from your script before committing the code.

644



Ensure that all scripts have Windows style line endings (CR/LF) and not Unix line endings.

Do not use braces for one line of code. If using a brace every brace must appear on its own
line, except in the case of get; set; if they are no longer than a line worth of code.

Folder Structure

|-- Assets

|-- Art

|   |-- 2D

|   |   |-- Sprites

|   |-- 3D

|   |   |-- Models

|   |   |-- Characters

|-- Editor //Special Folder

|-- Media

|   |-- Audio

|   |-- Video

|-- Plugins

|   |-- Android

|   |-- iOS

|   |-- Special

|-- Prefabs

|-- Resources

|   |-- Android

|   |-- iOS

|   |-- Common

|-- Scenes

|   |-- Levels

|   |-- Others

645



|-- Scripts

|   |-- Editor

|-- Shaders

|-- StreamingAssets //Special Folder

Some Important points to remember:

1. Don’t use spaces in file and folder names, in Unity3D command line tools can’t automatically
process paths with spaces.

2. Do not store any asset files in the root directory. Use subdirectories whenever possible.

3. Do not create any additional directories in the root directory, unless you really need to.

4. Use separate ‘Third_Party folder’ to store assets imported from the Asset Store. They usually
have their own structure that shouldn’t be altered.

5. Use ‘SandBox’ directory for any experiments you’re not entirely sure about. When you’re
working on a project with other people, create your personal Sandbox subdirectory like:

‘SandBox/ DevName’

GIT rules

1. When naming branches use _ as the separator

2. develop branch will always be the stable branch and ready for the build

3. In the starting phase of the development, create a separate branch under your name and
work on it.

4. In the later phases we will be creating the branches based on the bug or feature and merging
it to the main branch after the QA/Designer review.

5. Before you start your day, always merge the main branch to your working branch.

6. After a peer review is done raise a pull request to merge the branch to the main branch

Peer review and unit testing

1. Peer review is to unit test and check the code written and provide feedback back to the dev

2. After a certain ticket is completed, assign the ticket to your peer for the unit test and review.

646



Development cycle

Create high level task estimation based on the design

This includes features, sub tasks, time estimates

Create high level milestone plan based on the estimations

Add the plan to the Jira and create sprints and milestones

Tickets in the Jira will be only be created by the leads

Before start of each sprint, 

Assign the tickets to the developers and get the estimation from them

Estimation should include development time and bug fixing

At the end of each day, add the numbers of hours worked on the ticket

Once the ticket is completed, assign the ticket to your peer for the review. 

Once the review is completed, assign the ticket to the team lead for review and merge

Any doubts and changes w.r.t tickets should be commented on the tickets.

Time tracking

Time worked on each time will be logged in the Jira under their respective tickets.

If any task unrelated to the project should be added in the Company Notion page.

At the end of each day log your working hours in the Notion and as well as in the tickets you
have worked on.

Build delivery

All builds will be should have proper naming and versioning 

Version format 

[phase cycle].[major].[minor].[patches]

Phase cycles starts from POC i.e 0

Unity pipeline

Use sprite sheets wherever assets can be put together

Addressable system will be used for addressing, building and loading the assets

Use Scriptable objects for storing data such as club properties, prefabs, links etc

injection principle.

651



Gameplay Mechanics

Google docs 

Gameplay Mechanics

Metrics

Metric sheet

GAMEPLAY

Standard golf game, with all game rules following the rules of real golf.

The gameplay consists of playing holes (rounds) of golf in a course (stage). 

Each course has certain number of holes.

Each hole has a target Par (more details in Game Mechanics section).

Score is awarded based on the number of shots taken to clear.

The main gameplay involves taking a shot with a suitable type of club, with the right amount

of power and accuracy.

There are other gameplay factors that affect the shot trajectory - such as wind, curve, spin,

and more.

The gameplay area is divided into different terrains based on the type of surface. The power,

accuracy, and trajectory varies based on these surfaces. More details in the Game Mechanics

section.

The round is cleared when the ball is shot into the hole. The aim of the game is to clear the

hole in as few shots as possible.

TUTORIAL

The game will have a basic interactive tutorial for First TIme Experience (FTE) of the

gameplay. This is optional and can be skipped.あ
This will be in the form of arrow indicators and hand gesture indicators, that pop up when the

player is doing certain actions.

The indicators etc will be minimal and unintrusive.

652



The gameplay tutorial will be a fixed one with a fixed course and fixed actions, and therefore a

fixed outcome.

The tutorial will not last longer than 1-2 minutes.

Once the tutorial is completed/skipped, the user returns to the main menu.

The tutorial can be accessed and replayed at any time from the menu.

CLUB PARAMETERS

DISTANCE

The distance a ball travels

Higher distance allows club to hit the ball further

ACCURACY

Accuracy defines the speed of the shot gauge

Higher accuracy will have slower shot gauge, allowing more accurate shots

CURL

Increase the range of curve for Draw and Fade shots (curved trajectory)

Higher curl allows for increased curve in the trajectory

SPIN

Increases the range of topspin and backspin, which allow for higher and lower trajectories

Higher backspin means the ball will travel higher and less roll distance

Higher topspin means the ball will travel longer with high roll distance

RECOVERY

The percentage increase at which the club’s durability will be recovered for the next game

Higher recovery will increase the durability of the club faster for the next game

PUTT

Increase the distance your Putting guideline is displayed, thereby increasing the putting

stability for the long putts

CONTROL

control of the club affects the amount of distance when accuracy is off

Higher control of the club decreases the amount of durability loss after each hit

Lower control will add some face angle to the ball which affects the fade or draw 

High control  will add more "forgiveness" to badly missed shots, sending them less off-

course

DURABILITY

Each hit will decrease the durability of the club

653



As durability decreases, distance and accuracy will decrease

If durability reaches certain threshold, it can not be recovered unless it is repaired

WEIGHT

Weight does not directly affect the ball

Weight affects the club handling based on the user strength

 HIgher user’s strength will have better handling over the heavy clubs

HANDLING

Handling affects the ease of using the controls

Lower handling will have some resistance when using the controls

PENALTY REDUCTION

Penalty Reduction decreases the impact of penalties applied when the ball is in hazards

such as rough and sand. This includes:

Carry distance penalty

Spin control penalty

Mishit tolerance window penalty

Accuracy penalty

Durability penalty

BALL PARAMETERS

SPIN

Higher spin will allow to apply more backspin or topspin

FLIGHT

Boosts the distance a ball can travel

BOUNCE

Increases or decreases the bounciness of the ball

ROLL

Increases or decreases the friction of the ball

Lower roll will stop the ball faster and vice versa 

USER PARAMETERS

STRENGTH

Strength influences your swing speed which determines the distance all of your shot go

Higher strength allows to use heavy clubs 

654



Total strength applied on the ball is higher than the accuracy then speed of the shot gauge

increases and  becomes harder to hit

Higher strength also provided distance boost to the club distance but at a cost of accuracy

DRIVING

Driving influences the driving swing.

Higher driving will boost control and handling when driving

It affects only at the time of driving

CLUB CONTROL

Club control stat influences how much of the club’s potential can be used

HIgher club control allows the user to use the club to its maximum

SPIN

Spin affects how much maximum spin can be applied to the ball

PUTT

Affects how much of the club putt parameter can be used

STAMINA

Stamina influences the strength of the user

Lower stamina will decrease the strength thereby decreasing the distance and accuracy of

the swing

Stamina decreases after each hit

RECOVERY

Percentage increase of stamina based on time

CONDITION

Increases or decreases the strength, club control, stamina decrease percent, recovery

Condition increases if the user performs better in the games consistently.

If the user haven’t played for long time will decrease the condition

Higher condition will provide boost to all the parameters

CONTROLS

CONTROL TYPE FUNCTION

Tap UI interactions

655



When tap on empty space :

Open/Close Map view

Drag ・During player camera: adjust hit

direction (left/right)

・During top camera: adjust hit

direction 

Drag and flick ・During shot camera: 

　→Drag shot indicator down to

increase strength. Range based on

club and ball parameters

　→Flick towards the accuracy to

gauge to hit the ball.

→When not flicked at the center

of the gauge. You get draw or fade

based on how far the center and

which side it is.

→When not flicked on the moving

gauge. It is considered as a miss

shot.

Story Mode Outline

Description

Story mode will consists of missions/scenarios. Each mission will have a unique completion

requirement. On completion of a mission, user will be awarded with stars based on the

performance. 

ストーリーモードはミッションやシナリオから成り立っています。各ミッションには独自の達
成要件があります。ミッションを完了すると、パフォーマンスに基づいてユーザーに星が授与さ
れます。

Features

All missions will be arranged in a tree pattern sequentially. Where user has to obtain minimum

number of stars to progress to the next mission. 

Each mission will have a unique requirements. Completing 100% will award you maximum

stars.

すべてのミッションは木構造で順次配置されます。ユーザーは次のミッションに進むために
最小限の星を獲得する必要があります。
各ミッションにはユニークな要件があります。100%完了すると、最大の星が授与されます。

Missions(TBD)

Rewards

Stars

Experience points

In-game vanity items

In-game tools (Eg : repair tool)

Golf bag Customization

Depending on the golf bag level, number of clubs carried to the gameplay is determined

By default all the golf bags will be able to carry minimum of clubs required to play the game.

No two clubs of same type can be present in the bag

Max golf bag level is determined by the rarity of the bag.

ゴルフバッグのレベルによって、ゲームプレイに持ち込むクラブの数が決まる
デフォルトでは、すべてのゴルフバッグは、ゲームをプレイするために必要な最小限のクラ
ブを運ぶことができるようになります
バッグの中に同じ種類のクラブを2本入れることはできない。

ゴルフバッグの最高レベルはバッグの希少性によって決まる。

Alpha Release Plan
Goals

To create a playable game for the users. Which includes smooth controls, smooth ball

movement, able to put  in hole easily and simple camera movements. Refer to Game Mechanics

document for more info.

Tasks

1. Gameplay improvements

a. Ball roll and friction improvements

b. Managing Ball bounce based on the surface

c. Putt controls

d. Putt camera improvements

e. Painting 1 hole course with different surfaces in such a way that it contains all surfaces

f. Reducing the size of the putt mesh

g. Play testing

2. UI

Screens: Loading, Main Menu, Game HUD, Map, Gameover

a. Wireframe Alpha version 

b. Create assets list 

c. Create UI

d. Brush up design

Milestones

1. April 29, 2024

a. Smooth ball movement

b. Smooth Putt camera and Putt controls

2. May 15, 2024

a. Bug fixes

b. Gameplay improvements

3. May 24, 2024

a. Painted course with all surfaces

670



b. Loading screen

4. May 31, 2024

a. Gameplay HUD

b. Gameplay controls

671



3D Team Management

Rules:

1. Please follow the concept art exactly as it is (strive for 100% similarity as much as

possible)

2. For clearer communication within the team: 

all questions related to the task should be addressed within the task in Jira. Direct

messages are allowed only if the person hasn’t responded in Jira for an extended period.

3. We use base faces for all characters. 

Please ask permission if you want to change a face (if the desired changes were not written

in the task). 

It is very difficult to edit what has been corrected, for this purpose the base faces were

created. 

The differences between some characters from others are based on different colors, makeup,

hairstyles, clothes, etc.

4. Listen to all the feedback from Olga-san (as she represents the voice and opinion of

Nishikawa-san, Seko-san and Ken-san). 

Olga does not judge art according to her own taste, she follows the vision of the

management team

5. Implement all feedback and please ensure you haven’t missed anything. 

Double-check before posting if necessary.

6. Don’t rush. It’s better to make all the revisions yourself and redo something 20 times before

posting in Slack than to receive the same 20 revisions from someone else. 

Remember that management's time is more valuable than yours.

7. Please respect the reviewer’s time and remember your responsibility for your work.

8. If you want to change the design, ask for permission first and explain your reasoning. 

Making changes without permission and approval is prohibited.

9. If you have any questions, ask Olga or Nishikawa-san.

10. Mandatory: 

Before presenting your model or texture, create a comparison in Photoshop. 

672



Place the concept art on the left and a screenshot of your 3D model on the right. 

When a 3D artist upload to Jira their screenshots, it means that in their opinion, the 3D model

closely resembles the 2D concept, and they see no further differences.

11. Screenshots and textures are accepted from four angles: front, left, back, right. 

Other angles will not be accepted.

12. The focal length should match the focal length in the game (i.e., character features should

not be distorted).

13. Sometimes Olga or the management team may ask you to take a step back and redo work

that was previously approved. 

Please don’t argue or say you’re wasting time. This can happen and it’s normal.

Example of comparison of 3D model and design concept from 4 angles

Pipeline for working with the Art Lead and Managment team:

block diagram

1. A ticket is created in Jira with a 3D label.

2. The 3D artist reviews the task and requests all necessary files (e.g., textures, logos, colors,

additional references and angles). 

Files can also be requested later during the process, it’s not a problem.

3. The 3D artist creates the model without textures (basic textures can be added optionally). 

4. Olga and 3D artist make a video conference with correction of 3D model

5. A comparison screenshot after the video meeting of the 3D model with the concept art

from the same angle is attached to the post. 

673



6. The 3D artist creates the textures

7. Olga and 3D artist make a video conference with correction of textures

8. A comparison screenshot after the video meeting of the 3D model with the concept art

from the same angle is attached to the post. 

9. 3D artist moves the task to the "Review" column

10. After Olga’s approval, Olga will ask Nishikawa-san for feedback. 

11. Approval from Nishikawa-san.

12. The 3D artist moves on to technical work. 

From this point forward, there is no further communication with Olga, only communication

with engineers and developers.

13. After completing all technical processes, the 3D artist reports it in a comment and moves

the task to the "Done" column.

GPS : Maintenance mode

(English)

Implementing Maintenance Mode using CloudFront

Objectives

Notify users that the system is under maintenance while minimizing changes to the application

and backend servers during maintenance work. Implement maintenance mode at the

infrastructure level to enhance operational flexibility.

Design Overview

Place the JSON content for maintenance mode in a storage service that serves as the origin for

CloudFront. Configure the CloudFront distribution to return the maintenance mode JSON

content for all requests during maintenance. Update the domain's DNS records to direct all

access to CloudFront. Toggle maintenance mode by changing the origin of CloudFront.

Steps

1. Creating and Placing the JSON Content for Maintenance Mode

Create a JSON content that includes information such as the reason for maintenance, estimated

duration, and message. Place the JSON content in a storage service (e.g., Amazon S3) that

serves as the origin for CloudFront. Example JSON content:

1 {
2 "maintenance": true,
3 "reason": "システムのアップグレードとメンテナンス",
4 "estimatedDuration": "約2時間",
5 "message": "ご不便をおかけしております。メンテナンスは約2時間を予定しております。"
6 }
7

2. Configuring CloudFront

Create or update the CloudFront distribution. Specify the storage service where the

maintenance mode JSON content is placed as the origin. In the behavior settings, configure to

redirect HTTP requests to HTTPS. During maintenance mode, set to return the maintenance

mode JSON content for all requests.

686



3. Configuring DNS

Update the domain's DNS records (A record or CNAME record). Specify the domain name of the

CloudFront distribution as the value for the record.

4. Configuring the Application

Direct API requests from the application to the usual URL. Check the response returned from

CloudFront, and if the maintenance mode JSON content is returned, display the maintenance

screen.

5. Toggling Maintenance Mode

When starting maintenance mode, switch the origin of CloudFront to the maintenance mode

JSON content. When ending maintenance mode, switch the origin of CloudFront back to the

normal content.

Considerations

The maintenance mode JSON content needs to have appropriate CORS settings to allow access

from CloudFront. Configure the caching settings of CloudFront appropriately to ensure that the

toggle of maintenance mode is reflected immediately. Since the start and end of maintenance

mode are controlled by changing the CloudFront settings, proper access permission

management is necessary.

(日本語)

CloudFrontを用いたメンテナンスモードの実装

目的

メンテナンス作業中に、アプリやバックエンドサーバーの変更を最小限に抑えつつ、ユーザー
にメンテナンス中であることを通知する。
インフラストラクチャレベルでメンテナンスモードを実装し、運用の柔軟性を高める。

設計概要

1. メンテナンスモード用のJSONコンテンツをCloudFrontのオリジンとなるストレージサービス
に配置する。

2. CloudFrontのディストリビューションを設定し、メンテナンスモード中は全てのリクエスト
に対してメンテナンスモード用のJSONコンテンツを返すようにする。

3. ドメインのDNSレコードを更新し、全てのアクセスをCloudFrontに向ける。

687



4. メンテナンスモードの切り替えは、CloudFrontのオリジンを変更することで行う。

手順

1. メンテナンスモード用のJSONコンテンツの作成と配置

メンテナンスの理由、目安時間、メッセージなどの情報を含むJSONコンテンツを作成する。

JSONコンテンツをCloudFrontのオリジンとなるストレージサービス（例：Amazon S3）に配
置する。
JSONコンテンツ例

1 {
2 "maintenance": true,
3 "reason": "システムのアップグレードとメンテナンス",
4 "estimatedDuration": "約2時間",
5 "message": "ご不便をおかけしております。メンテナンスは約2時間を予定しております。"
6 }
7

2. CloudFrontの設定

CloudFrontのディストリビューションを作成または更新する。

オリジンとして、メンテナンスモード用のJSONコンテンツが配置されたストレージサービス
を指定する。
ビヘイビアの設定で、HTTPリクエストをHTTPSにリダイレクトするように設定する。

メンテナンスモード中は、全てのリクエストに対してメンテナンスモード用のJSONコンテン
ツを返すように設定する。

3. DNSの設定

ドメインのDNSレコード（AレコードまたはCNAMEレコード）を更新する。
レコードの値として、CloudFrontのディストリビューションのドメイン名を指定する。

4. アプリの設定

アプリからのAPIリクエストは、通常通りのURLに向ける。
CloudFrontから返されたレスポンスを確認し、メンテナンスモード用のJSONコンテンツが返
された場合は、メンテナンス画面を表示する。

5. メンテナンスモードの切り替え

メンテナンスモードを開始する際は、CloudFrontのオリジンをメンテナンスモード用のJSON
コンテンツに切り替える。
メンテナンスモードを終了する際は、CloudFrontのオリジンを通常のコンテンツに戻す。

688



留意点

メンテナンスモード用のJSONコンテンツは、適切なCORSの設定を行い、CloudFrontからの
アクセスを許可する必要がある。
CloudFrontのキャッシュ設定を適切に行い、メンテナンスモードの切り替えがすぐに反映され
るようにする。
メンテナンスモードの開始と終了は、CloudFrontの設定変更により制御するため、適切なアク
セス権限の管理が必要である。

689



GPS : Locator Fraud Monitoring Batch

Locator Fraud Monitoring Batch Processing Design Document(English)

1. Objective

The objective of this design document is to define the design of a batch processing system for

detecting fraudulent activities in golf course check-ins.

2. Overview

This batch processing system focuses on detecting fraudulent activities based on the analysis

of user check-in times and locations, specifically:

Check-ins outside of golf course operating hours

Long-distance travel at impossibly high speeds

3. Processing Flow

3.1. Database Preparation

Register golf course location information (latitude and longitude) and operating hours in the

database.

3.2. Check-in Time Analysis

Record user check-in times.

If a check-in time is outside of the golf course's operating hours, consider it a potential fraud

and flag the corresponding user.

3.3. Long-distance Travel Detection

Set rules for travel distance and time difference (e.g., traveling more than 100km within 1

hour).

Record user check-in locations (latitude and longitude) and times.

Calculate the distance and time difference between consecutive check-ins.

If the calculated result violates the rules, consider it a potential fraud and flag the

corresponding user.

690



3.4. Exception Case Handling

Set additional rules to identify legitimate check-ins outside of operating hours and long-

distance travel.

3.5. Batch Processing Execution

Execute the above processes at regular intervals (e.g., daily or weekly).

4. Input Data

User check-in times

User check-in locations (latitude and longitude)

5. Master Data

Golf course location information (latitude and longitude)

Golf course operating hours

6. Output Data

List of users flagged for potential fraudulent activities

7. Exception Handling

Identify and properly handle legitimate rule violations (e.g., playing outside of operating hours,

long-distance travel).

8. Future Enhancements

Introduce machine learning-based anomaly detection to strengthen the system's ability to

detect new fraud patterns.

Regularly review and update rules to adapt to changing fraud methods.

ゴルフ場チェックイン不正行為検出バッチ処理設計書(日本語)

1. 目的

本設計書は、ゴルフ場のチェックインにおける不正行為を検出するためのバッチ処理の設計を定
義するものである。

2. 概要

本バッチ処理では、ユーザーのチェックイン時間とチェックイン位置の分析に基づき、以下の2
点に焦点を当てて不正行為を検出する。

ゴルフ場の営業時間外のチェックイン

691



現実的に不可能な速度での広域移動

3. 処理フロー

3.1. データベース準備

ゴルフ場の位置情報（緯度・経度）と営業時間をデータベースに登録する。

3.2. チェックイン時間の分析

ユーザーのチェックイン時間を記録する。
チェックイン時間がゴルフ場の営業時間外である場合、不正の可能性があるとみなし、該当ユ
ーザーにフラグを付ける。

3.3. 広域移動の検出

移動距離と時間差のルールを設定する（例: 1時間以内に100km以上の移動）。
ユーザーのチェックイン位置（緯度・経度）と時間を記録する。
連続するチェックイン間の距離と時間差を計算する。

計算結果がルールに抵触する場合、不正の可能性があるとみなし、該当ユーザーにフラグを付
ける。

3.4. 例外ケースの処理

正当な理由による営業時間外のチェックインや長距離移動を識別するための追加ルールを設定
する。

3.5. バッチ処理の実行

一定期間（例: 毎日または毎週）ごとに上記の処理を実行する。

4. 入力データ

ユーザーのチェックイン時間
ユーザーのチェックイン位置（緯度・経度）

5. マスタデータ

ゴルフ場の位置情報（緯度・経度）
ゴルフ場の営業時間

6. 出力データ

不正行為の可能性があるユーザーのフラグ付けリスト

692



7. 例外処理

正当な理由によるルール違反（営業時間外のプレイ、長距離移動など）を識別し、適切に処理
する。

8. 今後の拡張可能性

機械学習による異常検知の導入により、新たな不正パターンへの対応力を強化する。
ルールの定期的な見直しと更新により、変化する不正手法へ適応する。

693



GPS : Reward points Distribution and Assumptions
(English)

*Please note that this information is as of June 13th, 2024. Since the management is currently

discussing this reward points allocation, the information provided here is subject to change.

Nature of the reward points

reward point Issuance:The total number of issued reward points is predetermined and

cannot be increased or decreased.The number of reward points issued per day is also fixed.

Distribution Timing:reward points are distributed in a batch process every night.They are not

distributed during checkouts throughout the day.

Reward Point Distribution Mechanism:Users cannot know the exact number of reward

points they will receive at checkout, as the distribution is determined after aggregating all

player data for the day, making it unpredictable in advance.

Reward Point Data Type and Rounding Method

Data Type: Reward points are stored as fixed-point numbers, and the specific number of

decimal places depends on the point design and is pending confirmation.

Rounding Down: Any fractional parts in the point distribution calculations are truncated. (If

there are remainders, they are recorded in a table.)

Conditions that Affect Distribution

Affiliation Status and Point Allocation Ratio:

Affiliated golf courses are allocated X% of the total reward points, and non-affiliated golf

courses are allocated Y% of the reward points. (Since the detailed rules for point allocation

are undecided, the point allocation ratio based on the affiliation status of golf courses is

also undecided.)

Presence of Play at Golf Courses:

Reward points are allocated only to golf courses where play occurred on that day.

Number of Players:

The reward points allocated to a golf course are evenly divided among the players who

played there that day.

Daily Limit on Golf Course Visits:

694



Users can visit up to two golf courses per day. Visits beyond the first two are not included

in the calculations.

Distance Limitation Between Visited Golf Courses:

If visiting more than one course, the courses must be within a straight-line distance of

30km from each other.

Conditions that Do Not Affect Distribution

Play Duration:

The duration of play does not affect point distribution.

Multiple Visits by a User:

Even if a user visits multiple golf courses in one day, the point distribution is only affected

by the first two visits.

Specific Example

Assumptions

Daily total point amount: 1000 reward points

Affiliated golf course: Golf Course A (with play), Golf Course B (no play)

Non-affiliated golf course: Golf Course C (with play)

Point Allocation

Golf Course A: 700 reward points (70% due to affiliation)

Golf Course B: 0 reward points (no play)

Golf Course C: 300 reward points (30% due to non-affiliation)

Number of Users

Users who played at Golf Course A: 6

Users who played at Golf Course C: 4

Point Distribution (with truncation applied)

reward points allocated per user at Golf Course A:

700/6≈116.67 (rounded down to 116 reward points per person)

reward points allocated per user at Golf Course C:

300/4=75 reward points per person (no truncation needed)

(日本語)

695



*この情報は2024年6月14日時点のものである。現在経営陣はこのトークアロケーションにちて
議論している最中であるため、ここに書かれた情報は変更される可能性が高いことに留意して、
この情報を参照してください。

リワードポイントの性質

リワードポイントの発行枚数:

リワードポイントの総発行数は予め決まっており、増減することはない。
1日あたりの発行数も固定されている。

配布のタイミング:

リワードポイントは毎日、夜間に一括でバッチ処理によって配布される。

日中のチェックアウト時には配布されない。
リワードポイント配布の仕組み:

ユーザーはチェックアウト時にその日に獲得できるリワードポイントの正確な数を知るこ
とができず、配布はその日の全てのプレイヤーデータを集計した後に決定されるため事前
に予測できない。

リワードポイントのデータ型と端数処理

リワードポイントのデータ型: リワードポイントは固定小数点型で保持され、具体的な少数桁
数はリワードポイントの設計に依存し、確定を待っている。

端数処理: リワードポイントの配分計算において生じる端数は切り捨てる。

影響する条件

ゴルフ場の提携状態とリワードポイント割当比率:

提携ゴルフ場には総リワードポイントの70%が、非提携ゴルフ場には30%が割り当てられ
る。

ゴルフ場でのプレイ有無:

リワードポイントはその日にプレイがあったゴルフ場にのみ割り当てられる。

プレイしたユーザー数:

ゴルフ場に割り当てられたリワードポイントは、その日にプレイしたユーザー数で等分さ
れる。

1日のゴルフ場訪問上限:

ユーザーは1日に最大1件のゴルフ場を訪れることができる。2件目以上の訪問は計算に含ま
れない。

訪問するゴルフ場の距離制限:

2件以上訪問する場合、訪れるゴルフ場は直線距離で30km以内である必要がある。

696



影響しない条件

プレイ時間:

プレイ時間はリワードポイントの配分に影響を与えない。
ユーザーの複数回訪問:

ユーザーがその日に複数のゴルフ場を訪れても、リワードポイントの配分には影響されな
い。ただし、最初の2件の訪問のみが考慮される。

具体例

仮定

日ごとのリワードポイント総量: 1000リワードポイント

提携ゴルフ場: ゴルフ場A（プレイあり）、ゴルフ場B（プレイなし）
非提携ゴルフ場: ゴルフ場C（プレイあり）

リワードポイント割当

ゴルフ場A: 700リワードポイント（提携のため70%）
ゴルフ場B: 0リワードポイント（プレイなしのため）

ゴルフ場C: 300リワードポイント（非提携のため30%）

ユーザー数

ゴルフ場Aでプレイしたユーザー: 6人

ゴルフ場Cでプレイしたユーザー: 4人

リワードポイント配分（切り捨てを適用）

ゴルフ場Aのユーザーに割り当てられるリワードポイント:

700/6≈116.67（切り捨てを適用して116リワードポイント/人）

ゴルフ場Cのユーザーに割り当てられるリワードポイント:

300/4=75リワードポイント/人（切り捨て不要）

697



GPS : Table Design (v04)

ER Diagram

※ER図は若干バージョンが古いです。各テーブルの細かい修正が完了した後にアップデートしま
す。

Online FlowChart & Diagrams Editor - Mermaid Live Editor

GPS : API Interface (v02) ja

目次

1. はじめに

2. 認証
3. バージョニング

4. レート制限
5. エンドポイント

a. チェックイン

b. チェックアウト
c. タイムアウトチェックアウト

d. チェックインのキャンセル
e. チェックイン履歴取得

6. ステータスの定義

7. エラーレスポンス
8. セキュリティの考慮事項

凡例：
○ : 必須項目

: 任意項目

1. はじめに

このAPIは、ゴルフ場でのチェックインとチェックアウト、および位置情報の記録を管理するた
めのものである。

2. 認証

このAPIはAmazon Cognitoを使用して認証を行う。

2.1 ユーザー認証

1. Amazon Cognitoユーザープールを使用してユーザーを認証する。
2. 認証が成功すると、IDトークン、アクセストークン、更新トークンが発行される。

728



2.2 APIリクエストの認証

すべてのAPIリクエストには、Cognitoが発行したIDトークンを使用して認証を行う。

1 Authorization: Bearer <id_token>

IDトークンの有効期限が切れた場合は、更新トークンを使用して新しいIDトークンを取得する必
要がある。

3. バージョニング

APIのバージョンはURLパスに含まれる。現在のバージョンは v1 である。

例： <https://xxxxxx.com/v1/user/check_in_history >

4. レート制限

APIには以下のレート制限が適用される：

通常のエンドポイント: 1分あたり60リクエスト
チェックイン履歴取得エンドポイント: 1分あたり10リクエスト

制限を超えた場合、429 (Too Many Requests) エラーが返される。

4.1日時フィールドの型

すべての日時フィールドはUTC（協定世界時）で指定され、"YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm:ss"形式で
表現されます。 クライアント側で、ローカルタイムとUTCを変換してください。

5. エンドポイント

5.1 チェックイン

新しいチェックインを作成する。

エンドポイント

1 POST /v1/check_in

リクエストボディ

ロパティ データ型 説明 必須 NULL許可

golf_course_i integer チェックイ ○ 不可
d ンするゴル

フ場ID

check_in_at string (UTC) チェックイ ○ 不可
ン日時

729



リクエスト例

1 {
2 "golf_course_id": 1,
3 "check_in_at":"2023-12-19T09:00:00"
4 }

ステータスコード: 201 (Created)

レスポンスボディ

プロパティ データ型 説明 必須 NULL許可

ンID

ンのステータ
ス

4 "status": "in_progress"
5 }

6. ステータスの定義

チェックインには以下のステータスがある：

736



ステータス 説明

Playing チェックイン直後の状態 

Applying 正常にチェックアウトされた状態 

Points Distributed ポイント配布が完了した状態

Not eligible for point 不正によりポイント配布ができなか
った状態

Application not possible (Cancelled ユーザーによってキャンセルされた
By User) 状態 

Application not possible (timeout) タイムアウトによりチェックアウト
された状態 

7. エラーレスポンス

エラー時のレスポンスボディは以下の形式で返される：

1 {
2 "error": {
3 "code": "ERROR_CODE",
4 "message": "エラーの詳細な説明"
5 }
6 }

共通のエラーレスポンス：

ステータスコード 説明

400 リクエストが不正な場合 

401 認証エラー（IDトークンが無効また
は期限切れ） 

403 操作権限がない場合 

404 リソースが見つからない場合 

409 リソースの状態が操作と競合する場
合 

429 レート制限超過 

500 内部サーバーエラー 

737



8. セキュリティの考慮事項

1. すべての通信はHTTPS経由で行われる。

2. 認証にはAmazon Cognitoを使用し、IDトークンによる認証を行う。

738



GPS :  API Interface v3

2. 認証
3. バージョニング

4. レート制限
5. エンドポイント
5.1 チェックイン
5.2 チェックアウト
5.3 タイムアウトチェックアウト
5.4 チェックインのキャンセル
5.5 チェックイン履歴取得

6. ステータスの定義

7. エラーレスポンス
8. セキュリティとプライバシーの考慮事項

1. はじめに

このAPIは、ゴルフ場でのチェックインとチェックアウト、および位置情報の記録を管理するた
めのものである。

2. 認証

このAPIはAmazon Cognitoを使用して認証を行う。

2.1 ユーザー認証

Amazon Cognitoユーザープールを使用してユーザーを認証する。
認証が成功すると、IDトークン、アクセストークン、更新トークンが発行される。

2.2 APIリクエストの認証

すべてのAPIリクエストには、Cognitoが発行したIDトークンを使用して認証を行う。

1 Authorization: Bearer <id_token>

739



IDトークンの有効期限が切れた場合は、更新トークンを使用して新しいIDトークンを取得する必
要がある。

3. バージョニング

APIのバージョンはURLパスに含まれる。現在のバージョンはv1である。

例： <https://xxxxxx.com/v1/users/check_ins_history >

4. レート制限

APIには以下のレート制限が適用される：

通常のエンドポイント: 1分あたり60リクエスト
チェックイン履歴取得エンドポイント: 1分あたり10リクエスト

制限を超えた場合、429 (Too Many Requests) エラーが返される。

5. エンドポイント

5.1 チェックイン

新しいチェックインを作成する。

エンドポイント

POST /v1/check_in

るゴルフ場ID

るユーザーID

3 "user_id": 12345

4 }

ステータスコード: 201 (Created)

タス

6. ステータスの定義

チェックインには以下のステータスがある：

ステータス 説明

in_progress チェックイン直後の状態 

completed 正常にチェックアウトされた状態 

cancelled ユーザーによってキャンセルされた
状態 

timeout_completed タイムアウトによりチェックアウト
された状態 

7. エラーレスポンス

エラー時のレスポンスボディは以下の形式で返される：

1 {
2 "error": {
3 "code": "ERROR_CODE",
4 "message": "エラーの詳細な説明"
5 }
6 }

共通のエラーレスポンス：

ステータスコード 説明

400 リクエストが不正な場合 

401 認証エラー（IDトークンが無効また
は期限切れ） 

403 操作権限がない場合 

747



404 リソースが見つからない場合 

409 リソースの状態が操作と競合する場
合 

429 レート制限超過 

500 内部サーバーエラー 

8. セキュリティとプライバシーの考慮事項

すべての通信はHTTPS経由で行われる。
認証にはAmazon Cognitoを使用し、IDトークンによる認証を行う。

位置情報データは暗号化されて保存される。
ユーザーの位置情報は、必要最小限の期間のみ

748



GPS : Monthly Ranking System

GPSアプリはまもなくリリース1周年を迎える。1周年を記念して新たにランキングシステムを提
供し、ユーザーの行動を可視化する。ランキング上位者には追加リワードポイントの付与を行う

ランキングは主に2つの指標で構築する

1. 月間のチェックイン数

2. 月間のチェックインコース数
配布ポイントは2つの指標合わせて50万ポイントとする。

表示方法は、専用のWebページを公開する。
当月の現在ランキングは1日に一度更新される。

月間チェックイン数 / 月間チェックインコース数

上位10名に対してボーナスポイントを配布する
それぞれ合計10万ポイントを下記方式で分配する

分配ポイント

順位 ポイント数

No.1 30,000

No.2 20,000

No.3 15,000

No.4 8,000

No.5 7,000

No.6 5,000

No.7 4,500

No.8 4,000

No.9 3,500

No.10 3,000

749



前提条件

対象とするチェックイン

全ての集計対象データは、ポイント付与されたチェックインに限り有効とする。

同率の場合

同率の場合は、集計期間最後のチェックイン時刻が早い方を上位とする。

Release Note (Backend) 2020926
リリース日: 2025年9月26日

環境: staging / production

ブランチ: dev → main

APIバージョン: v1.4.0

新機能

Ticket機能の拡張

無料チケット一括交換:

POST /api/v1/game/user/ticket/redeem_all_free_tickets

無料チケット個別交換:

POST /api/v1/game/user/ticket/redeem_free_ticket

チケット履歴取得の改善:

ページネーション機能を強化（GETクエリパラメータ対応）

Wallet機能（新規）

ウォレット登録メッセージ取得:

GET /api/v1/game/user/wallet/registration-message/{wallet_address}

ウォレット登録:

POST /api/v1/game/user/wallet/register

プライマリウォレット設定:

POST /api/v1/game/user/wallet/{wallet_id}/set-primary

EIP-712署名による安全なウォレット認証を実装

Maintenance機能（新規）

メンテナンス管理:

POST / PATCH / GET /api/v1/maintenance

メンテナンス状態確認:

GET /api/v1/maintenance/status

多言語メッセージ対応、IP制限機能付き

Level Up Validation（新規）

アイテム・キャラクター・クラブのレベルアップ条件管理機能

755



API変更（互換性に注意）

破壊的変更

GET /api/v1/game/user/ticket/free_tickets

旧: POST + PaginationRequest in body

新: GET + query parameters (cursor, direction, elements_per_page, page_jump)

GET /api/v1/game/user/ticket/free_ticket_history

同上の変更

スキーマ変更: ObjectDetailsResponse

item_name → object_name

specific_item_id → specific_object_id

廃止

ページ番号系エンドポイント（コメントアウト）

/free_tickets_pages

/free_ticket_history_pages

データベース変更

新規テーブル

signature_request: ウォレット署名リクエスト管理
maintenance_base: メンテナンス設定

maintenance_messages: 多言語メンテナンスメッセージ
level_up_condition: レベルアップ条件

テーブル変更

wallet

public_key → wallet_address (長さ42に変更)

追加: signature, signature_payload, verified_at

削除: balance

reward_point_transaction

noteカラム追加 (VARCHAR(500))

影響・注意事項

フロントエンド対応必須

Ticket API のリクエスト形式変更 (POST→GET+query)

レスポンススキーマのキー名変更対応

廃止エンドポイントの置き換え

756



運用設定

Wallet: 環境変数設定 (ドメイン、チェーンID、署名有効期限)

Maintenance: 初期データ投入、許可IP設定
監視: 新エラーステータスコード (422, 409, 503) の監視設定

Marketplace

769



RDD: Requirement Specifications

Overview

GolfinのキャラクターやアイテムはNFTに対応しており、それらの売買が行える環境を提供する
必要がある。アプリにインプリメントすることが望ましいが、NFT等のブロックチェーンに対応
させたアプリケーションの場合、App StoreやPlay Storeの審査が厳しくなり、リリースにかかる
時間が多くなること、アップデートの頻度が下がってしまう問題によりユーザーにとっても嬉し
くない結果につながる。そのためマーケットプレイスのウェブサイトを構築することとし、そ
の要求仕様をここに定義する。

アイテムを売買する際にはNFTとしてブロックチェーンには書き込まないが、ゲームの外に出す
場合には手数料としてトークンを支払う必要がある。これはNFTとしてトランザクションをブロ
ックチェーンに書き込む際に手数料が発生することに起因する。アイテムをマーケットプレイス
に制限なく出品できると売れ残るような状態のアイテムが乱立してしまうことから、それらを
防ぐために出品時に手数料としてリワードポイントをユーザーが支払うこととする。

このようなアイテムのGOLFIN内での売買と外部との出し入れを可能にしたものが、マーケット
プレイスである。

Requirements

GOLFINのバックエンドAPIを共通利用したWebアプリケーションを構築する。

Programing Languages

TypeScript

React (or React based Framework, like Next.JS)

SCSS

Devices

また、モバイルデバイスとPCからの双方のアクセスが想定されるため、MediaQueryによるレス
ポンシブ対応をする。ブラウザのUserAgent等を利用せずに、サイズで判定すること。

Device Browser

PC (Windows, Mac, Google Chrome

Linux) Safari

Firefox

770



Edge (Chromium)

リリース時点で最新版のVerに対応していること

Mobile (iPhone, Chrome

Android) Safari

Windows Phone等は最初は対応を想定しなくても
良い

保守性

バックエンド・フロントエンドそれぞれ異なるタイミングで実行されるメンテナンスに対応で
きる機構を有すること。

Target User

対象顧客はGOLFINユーザーに加え、GPSアプリやゲームアプリを利用しないが、投機的な目的
のユーザーも存在することを理解する。投機的な目的でのみGOLFINを利用することは希望しな
いがWEB3に関連するアプリケーションであることから、このようなユーザーが存在することを
想定すること。

利用者の国籍は様々であり、次の言語に対応すること。

1. 英語 (Primary)

2. 日本語 (Secondary)

将来追加で他の言語も加わることがある。言語はアクセスユーザーのブラウザ設定第一位が
ja_JPである場合に日本語を表示し、その他は英語を表示する。

Functions

マーケットプレイスに求める機能をここに定義する。
なお、詳細は詳細設計書にて定義するものとし、ここでは最低限必要な概要のみを記載する。

登録 / ログイン
ウォレット機能
リワードポイント

アイテムの購入
アイテムの出品

サードパーティマーケットプレイスとの出し入れ
