Telegram: MiniApp

1015



Telegram Mini App Settings

Follow the below instruction to create the bot and adding the bot to the mini app 

Instructions

1. First, generating the bot from the telegram 

a. Go to telegram, search for BotFather

b. Input /start

1016



c. Input /newbot

d. Input the bot name

1017



e. Input the bot username

f. Get the telegram token, start with HTTP API: XXXXXX, then the telegram token of that bot
is XXXXXX

1018



2. Second, make the webapp from the telegram 

a. Go to telegram, search for BotFather

b. List out the existing bot by /mybots

1019



c. Input /newapp

d. Assign the existing bot for that webapp: golfin_dev_demo_bot

e. Assign the title for that webapp, for example: game

1020



f. Assign the short description for that webapp, for example, Golf-based Tap and play gameFi

in Tokyo

g. Upload the photo with 640*360 pixel for the webapp

1021



h. Upload the gif for webapp demo if any, you can skip it by /empty

i. Edit the gif afterward, by /editapp command

j. Assign the existing the hosted website for that app, for example, https://golfin.io

k. Assign the short name for the webapp, it will be used as 

t.me/<BOT_NAME>/<SHORT_NAME> later on, for example, assign the short name as click,

1022



it is as short name parameter value in Bot API, you can click the link to test if the webapp
can be opened

3. Third, add the bot to the channel
a. Create a channel, if there is existing channel, skip this step

1023



b. Assign name and icon for that channel: Golfin-dev-demo

c. Assign channel as public type

1024



d. Assign the public link for channel, for example: golfinDevDemo

e. Add bot to channel: golfin-dev-demo

1025



f. Select Administrators

g. Add bot as admin: golfin-dev-demo

1026



h. Assign admin right for bot

i. Added bot as admin

1027



4. Fourth, add controlling to the bot
a. Go to telegram, search for Controller Bot

b. Input /addchannel

1028



c. If existing bot is not shown, choose Change Bot, Connect Bot

d. Go to BotFather to forward the token or copy and paste to the Controller Bot

e. Add the bot to the channel and assign the bot to be admin, if it is, skip this step

f. Go to the channel with that bot, and input anything, and forward to the Controller Bot, for
example: Hello from golfin-dev-demo. Input the current timezone if needed, for example:

1029



Tokyo

5. Fifth, add new post to the channel
a. Go to telegram, search for Controller Bot 

b. Input /newpost and select the channel you want to add the post, for example: golfin-dev-
demo

1030



c. Redirect to the bot with adding post

d. Enter the 1 or multiple message, it can be text, sticker, video, or emoji

1031



e. Attach Media if there is any

f. Add comments if there are any

1032



g. Add native comments if there are any

h. Add reactions if there are any

i. Add URL Buttons if there are any
i. Input the display on the buttons with the link on the  

t.me/<BOT_NAME>/<SHORT_NAME>/ on the step of 2j

It can be in single, for example
Play - https://t.me/golfin_dev_demo_bot/click/

1033



Or in multiple as, for example
Play - golfin-dev-demo   | 
Golfin - https://golfin.io
X - GOLFIN | 次世代WEB3ゴルフゲーム (@GOLFIN_official) on X

ii. Send the message, on this step, 

1. Show that the post has reactions and url button, the url button will not shown for that
case

1034



2. Select the time, now or schedule or self the destruct timer for that post
a. Choose now

i. Select send on the confirmation modal

ii. Post is on the channel

1035



iii. Post with reactions and url button

iv. Post with multiple buttons

1036



v. Pin the post on the channel

b. Choose schedule with self-destruct
i. Select send and choose the self-Destruct Timer

1037



ii. Select 1h, means that post will be deleted after 1 hour on the channel

iii. The 1h will be marked on the send options

1038



iv. Choose Enqueue to send the post on specific time

v. There are options for today, tomorrow and overmorrow, choose today and input
the time, for example, schedule the post when it is 13:34 on 13:35, then input
13:35. If any post is scheduled, there are post to be checked when checking on
the scheduled posts

1039



vi. Go to channel to see the scheduled post is not existed

vii. When 13:35, the post is existed by scheduled post

1040



j. Delete the message if there are any

k. Allow notification, push notification when that post is pushed to the channel

l. Allow link previews, allow the preview for the link on the post

m. Select the inline button
i. Delete all 

ii. Preview 

1. Review the existing post 

2. Send the existing post
a. Select

i. Set Self destroy Timer

ii. Send now

iii. Set a time to send

b. Confirm 

i. Send

ii. Cancel

3. Delete the post if needed

6. General 
a. IF the /start command is not working on the bot, go to Controller Bot to use /newpost
command and select the bot you want to use, for example: golfin-dev-demo

1041



b. Create new post

c. Scheduled posts

d. Edit post
i. Forward the existing post from channel to the Controller Bot

ii. Start editing, which is similar to the post creation

e. Channel Stats

1042



f. Settings
i. Auto Formatting 

1. HTML 

2. Markdown

1043



ii. Silent Broadcast (no notification when post is pushed): On / Off

iii. Link Preview (no preview on any link on the post): On / Off

iv. Default Reactions, the reactions will be added if no reactions are added on single post. If
there are reactions on the single post, it will override the default reactions: On / Off

Next Phase

Overview

This API covers the services of USER, ACTIVITY, POINT, FRIEND, GAME CHARACTER, GAME

CHARACTER STAT, SOCIAL MEDIA, RECORD for Telegram Mini App

Rewards

Check In

Overview

Daily Check In and Weekly Check In

For user check in every day, the reward will be given

1052



check if the last login time date is none

if true 

mean that it is the new user without any daily check in before 

update the logged in to true 

update the total login with +1 

update the last login time as current time with respect to the Singapore in UTC

update the login streak with +1

update the point with +2

if false 

check if the user logged in date is the day after the last login time date

if true

update the logged_in to be true

update the total logins with +1

if the date difference from current date to the last login time date is more than 1

single day 

true add the login streak with 1, mean reset it, 

false mean the user logged in before and it was just yesterday, update the login

streak with +1

update the last login time as current date time with respect to the Singapore in UTC

check if the total login is just hitting 7

mean that the user has logged in for 7 continuous days

trigger the weekly reward

update the logged_in to be true 

reset the login streak to be 0

update the point with +15

update the last_login_time to current time with respect to the Singapore in UTC

update the point with +2

Referral

Overview

Referral Per Invitation

For user who sends the friend request to other, when receiver open that invitation link

client side check if the app open with friend request link with friend telegram id 

1053



client side check if the receiver has already been created on the DB

if true

User already on the DB, no point will be given to the sender

check the friend for current user and return the friendship that has not yet been claimed

before

if false 

create friendship, sender as the one who sends the friend request, receiver as the one

who gets the friend request

get the current point on the sender 

add 100 points for sender 

Referral Per 10 Invitations

For user who sends 10 invitation and there are 10 new users made by his/her invitation

client side check if there are 10 friendship of that sender 

if true

check if current friendships are all having has_claimed as false case

get current point for sender 

add 3000 points for sender 

trigger batchUpdateRewardClaimBySender, mark all the has_claimed on that 10 payloads

as true

update client side friend provider and context

Models

Notations

✅: True case 

❌: False case 

⏳: Pending to be implemented but already prepared

N.A.: Not applicable 

int: Optional field

1054



User

Overview

User is the important part on the backend of Telegram Mini App, it holds and controls the user

informations provided from Telegram Mini App, personal informations and app informations.

Telegram Information 

It refers to the informations provided from telegram itself, including the id, username,

is_premium.

Personal Information 

It refers to the personal informations provided from the user, including location, nationality, age,

gender, email.

App Information

It refers to the app informations from the app, where those are informations for accessing

control, including admin, in_game_items, admin, skin, custom_logs.

1163



[Work Report] GCP-AWS Workload Identity Federation Setup (Dev Environment)

■ Overview 

We have configured Workload Identity Federation (WIF) to enable secure API calls from AWS servers (EC2) to Google

Cloud (GCP). This setup allows authentication via AWS IAM roles without issuing GCP service account secret keys

(JSON keys). The primary use case is server-to-server communication for Google Play receipt verification (Play

Developer API).

■ Authentication Flow

EC2 → AWS Authentication (Steps 1-3)

Obtain EC2 instance IAM role credentials using IMDSv2

AWS → GCP Authentication Exchange (Step 4)

Exchange AWS credentials for GCP token using Workload Identity Federation

Process based on gcp-wif-settings.json  configuration

GCP Service Account Impersonation (Step 5)

Impersonate play-billing-validator  service account using temporary token

Obtain GCP access token

Play API Call (Step 6)

Call Play Developer API using GCP access token

Execute receipt verification based on permissions configured in Play Console

1164



GCP Configuration

■ Implementation Details

(1) API Activation Google Play Android Developer API 　→ Used for receipt verification processing.

IAM Service Account Credentials API 　→ Required for issuing temporary authentication tokens via WIF.

Location: GCP Console → [APIs & Services] → [API Library]

(2) Service Account Creation Location: GCP Console → [IAM & Admin] → [Service Accounts]

Item Value

Name play-billing-validator

Description For Google Play receipt verification

Key Not issued (using Workload Identity

Federation)

■ 概要 

AWS上のサーバー（EC2）から Google Cloud（GCP）のAPIを安全に呼び出せるようにするため、 Workload Identity

Federation（以下 WIF） を構築しました。 これにより、GCPサービスアカウントの秘密鍵（JSONキー）を発行せず
に、AWS IAMロール経由で認証が可能になっています。 主な用途は、Google Play のレシート検証（Play Developer

API） におけるサーバー間通信です。

■ 認証フロー

EC2 → AWS認証 (ステップ1-3)

IMDSv2を使用してEC2インスタンスのIAMロール認証情報を取得
AWS → GCP認証交換 (ステップ4)
Workload Identity Federationを使用してAWS認証情報をGCPトークンに交換

gcp-wif-settings.json  の設定に基づいて処理

GCP Service Accountなりすまし (ステップ5)

一時トークンを使って play-billing-validator  サービスアカウントをなりすまし

1168



GCPアクセストークンを取得
Play API呼び出し (ステップ6)

GCPアクセストークンを使用してPlay Developer APIを呼び出し
Play Consoleで設定した権限に基づいてレシート検証実行

IAP Master Data Architecture and Management Guide

Overview

This document explains the parent-child relationships, foreign key references, and data dependencies between tables.

This will help you understand the order of data insertion and the impact scope when deleting records.

Overall Data Structure

1 ■ Independent Masters (Level 1)
2 │

3 ├─ LocalizationLanguage (Language Master)
4 │   └─→ Referenced by LocalizationTranslation
5 │

6 └─ GameTicketMaster (Ticket Master)
7 └─→ Referenced by ProductMaster's reference_master_id
8

9 ■ Product Definition (Level 2)
10 │

11 └─ ProductMaster (Product Master)
12 └─→ Referenced by ProductComponent
13

14 ■ Package Definition (Level 3)
15 │

16 └─ ProductPackageMaster (Package Master) ★1:1 correspondence with App
Store/Google Play products

17 ├─→ Referenced by ProductComponent
18 ├─→ Referenced by ProductPriceEntry
19 └─→ Referenced by LocalizationTranslation
20

21 ■ Price Management (Level 4)
22 │

23 ├─ ProductPrice (Price Header)
24 │   └─→ Referenced by ProductPriceEntry
25 │

26 └─ ProductPriceEntry (Price Entry)
27 └─→ Referenced by ProductPriceChannel
28

29 ■ Sales Management (Level 5)
30 │

31 └─ ProductPriceChannel (Sales Channel)
32

33 ■ Composition & Translation (Level 4-5)
34 │

35 ├─ ProductComponent (Product Composition)
36 │

37 └─ LocalizationTranslation (Multilingual Translation)
38

Parent-Child Relationship Details

Level 1: Master Data (Top-level Parents)

These tables are independent masters that don't depend on other tables, but are referenced by child tables.

1. LocalizationLanguage (Language Master)

Role: Definition of supported languages

Primary Key: language_code  (string)

1173



Child Tables: LocalizationTranslation

Dependencies: None (completely independent)

Referenced By: LocalizationTranslation.language_code

Data Insertion Order: First

2. GameTicketMaster (Ticket Master)

Role: Definition of in-game tickets

Primary Key: id

Child Tables: ProductMaster

Dependencies: None (completely independent)

Referenced By: ProductMaster.reference_master_id (when reference_table="game_ticket_master")

Important:

GameTicketMaster is an independent master table but is dynamically referenced by ProductMaster

When ProductMaster's reference_table  field is "game_ticket_master", reference_master_id

points to this table's id

This reference is a logical foreign key, managed at the application level rather than as a database constraint

Reference Mechanism:

1 ProductMaster (id=1)
2 reference_table = "game_ticket_master"
3 reference_master_id = 1
4 ↓
5 GameTicketMaster (id=1: Regular Ticket)
6

Data Insertion Order: First

Level 2: Product Definition

3. ProductMaster (Product Master)

Role: Definition of saleable products

Primary Key: id

Parent Tables:

GameTicketMaster (when reference_table  = "game_ticket_master")

Other master tables can be referenced in the future (e.g., club_master, ball_master, etc.)

Child Tables: ProductComponent

Dependencies:

1 When reference_table = "game_ticket_master"
2 reference_master_id → game_ticket_master.id (logical foreign key)
3

Example:

1 ProductMaster (id=1)

1174



2 product_code = "TICKET_REGULAR_001"
3 category = "TICKET"
4 reference_table = "game_ticket_master"
5 reference_master_id = 1
6 ↓ References
7 GameTicketMaster (id=1)
8 ticket_name = "Regular Ticket"
9 ticket_type = 1
10

Key Points:

The combination of reference_table  and reference_master_id  allows dynamic referencing of

different master tables

In Phase 1, reference_table  is only "game_ticket_master"

In the future, "club_master", "ball_master", etc. can be added

Data Insertion Order: After GameTicketMaster

Level 3: Package Definition

4. ProductPackageMaster (Product Package Master)

Role: Definition of sales units (bundles)

Primary Key: id

Parent Tables: None (independent)

Child Tables:

ProductComponent

ProductPriceEntry

LocalizationTranslation

Dependencies: None

🔴 Important: 1:1 Correspondence with Store Products

ProductPackageMaster (1 record) ⇔ App Store/Google Play Store Product

A 1:1 correspondence relationship exists. This mapping is managed by Unity Addressables.

Correspondence Mechanism:

1 [Backend]
2 ProductPackageMaster (id=105)
3 ↕ 1:1 Correspondence (Managed by Unity Addressables)
4 [App Store Connect]
5 Product: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
6 ↕ Same Product
7 [Google Play Console]
8 Product: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
9

Management in Unity Addressables:

Addressables configuration files hold mapping information between ProductPackageMaster.id and store product

IDs

Example: { "package_id": 105, "apple_product_id":

"com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2", "google_product_id":

1175



"com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2" }

Unity uses the appropriate store product ID during purchase processing

Links with backend using ProductPackageMaster.id during receipt verification

Price Change Correspondence:

1 Old Version:
2 - ProductPackageMaster (id=101, is_active=FALSE)
3 ↕ Corresponds to
4 - App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1 (Unpublished)
5 - Google Play: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1 (Unpublished)
6

7 New Version:
8 - ProductPackageMaster (id=105, is_active=TRUE)
9 ↕ Corresponds to
10 - App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2 (Published)
11 - Google Play: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2 (Published)
12

Key Points:

One ProductPackageMaster corresponds to one store product

When changing prices, create a new ProductPackageMaster = create a new store product

Unity Addressables manages the linkage, so the backend doesn't need to directly hold store product IDs

Data Insertion Order: After ProductMaster

Level 4: Package Composition and Pricing

5. ProductComponent (Product Composition)

Role: Products and quantities included in packages

Primary Key: id

Parent Tables:

ProductPackageMaster  (product_package_master_id)

ProductMaster  (product_master_id)

Dependencies:

1 product_package_master_id → product_package_master.id (foreign key)
2 product_master_id → product_master.id (foreign key)
3

Example:

1 ProductComponent (id=1001)
2 product_package_master_id = 101
3 product_master_id = 1
4 quantity = 10
5 ↓ References
6 ProductPackageMaster (id=101: 10 Ticket Pack)
7 ↓ Corresponds via Unity Addressables
8 App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1
9 ↓ References
10 ProductMaster (id=1: Regular Ticket)
11 ↓ References
12 GameTicketMaster (id=1: Regular Ticket)
13

Data Insertion Order: After ProductPackageMaster and ProductMaster

1176



6. ProductPrice (Price Header)

Role: Managing effective periods for price settings

Primary Key: id

Parent Tables: None (independent)

Child Tables: ProductPriceEntry

Dependencies: None

Data Insertion Order: Anytime

7. ProductPriceEntry (Price Entry)

Role: Specific currency-based pricing

Primary Key: id

Parent Tables:

ProductPrice  (product_price_id)

ProductPackageMaster  (product_package_master_id)

Child Tables: ProductPriceChannel

Dependencies:

1 product_price_id → product_price.id (foreign key)
2 product_package_master_id → product_package_master.id (foreign key)
3

Example:

1 ProductPriceEntry (id=3009)
2 product_price_id = 2001
3 product_package_master_id = 105
4 currency_code = "USD"
5 amount = 129
6 ↓ References
7 ProductPrice (id=2001: Regular Price)
8 ↓ References
9 ProductPackageMaster (id=105: 10 Ticket Pack New Version)
10 ↓ Corresponds via Unity Addressables
11 App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
12

Data Insertion Order: After ProductPrice and ProductPackageMaster

8. ProductPriceChannel (Price Channel)

Role: Sales availability by channel

Primary Key: id

Parent Tables:

ProductPriceEntry  (product_price_entry_id)

Dependencies:

1 product_price_entry_id → product_price_entry.id (foreign key)

1177



2

Example:

1 ProductPriceChannel (id=4009)
2 product_price_entry_id = 3009
3 channel = "GAME"
4 is_sellable = TRUE
5 ↓ References
6 ProductPriceEntry (id=3009: 10 Ticket Pack New Version USD)
7

Data Insertion Order: After ProductPriceEntry

9. LocalizationTranslation (Multilingual Translation)

Role: Translations for specific fields in each table

Primary Key: id

Parent Tables:

LocalizationLanguage  (language_code)

Dynamic reference: table_name  + record_id

Dependencies:

1 language_code → localization_language.language_code (foreign key)
2 (table_name, record_id) → (each table).id (logical foreign key)
3

Example:

1 LocalizationTranslation (id=17)
2 language_code = "ja"
3 table_name = "product_package_master"
4 record_id = 105
5 field_name = "name"
6 translated_text = "10レギュラーチケットパック"
7 ↓ References
8 LocalizationLanguage (language_code="ja")
9 ↓ References
10 ProductPackageMaster (id=105)
11 ↓ Corresponds via Unity Addressables
12 App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
13

Data Insertion Order: Last (after the tables to be translated)

Correct Data Insertion Order

1 1. LocalizationLanguage (Language Definition)
2 2. GameTicketMaster (Ticket Definition)
3 3. ProductMaster (Product Definition) ※References GameTicketMaster
4 4. ProductPackageMaster (Package Definition)
5 5. ProductComponent (Package Composition)
6 6. ProductPrice (Price Period)
7 7. ProductPriceEntry (Specific Prices)
8 8. ProductPriceChannel (Sales Availability)
9 9. LocalizationTranslation (Translation Data)
10

Important:

Order 2 → 3 is required: ProductMaster references GameTicketMaster.id

1178



Order 1 → 9 is required: LocalizationTranslation references LocalizationLanguage.language_code

Step 4 timing: The order of creating ProductPackageMaster and store products doesn't matter (managed by Unity

Addressables)

Important Dependency Map

Relationship Diagram Centered on Product Package (id=105)

1 ProductPackageMaster (id=105)
2 ↕ Managed by Unity Addressables
3 App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
4 Google Play: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
5 │

6 ├── ProductComponent (id=1005)
7 │   └── ProductMaster (id=1)
8 │       └── GameTicketMaster (id=1) ← Referenced via

reference_master_id
9 │

10 ├── ProductPriceEntry (id=3009)
11 │   ├── ProductPrice (id=2001)
12 │   └── ProductPriceChannel (id=4009)
13 │

14 └── LocalizationTranslation (id=17, 18, 19, 20)
15 └── LocalizationLanguage (ja, en)
16

Correspondence with Store Products

Backend ⇔ Unity ⇔ Store Integration

1 ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

2 │ Backend (PostgreSQL)                                    │
3 ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤

4 │ ProductPackageMaster (id=105)                           │
5 │   is_active = TRUE                                      │
6 └────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────────┘

7 │ Retrieved via API
8 ↓
9 ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

10 │ Unity Addressables                                      │
11 ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤

12 │ Mapping:                                                │
13 │   package_id: 105                                       │
14 │   apple_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2"      │
15 │   google_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2"     │
16 └────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────────┘

17 │ Purchase Request
18 ↓
19 ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

20 │ App Store Connect / Google Play Console                │
21 ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤

22 │ Product ID: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2                 │
23 │ Price: $1.29 / ¥160                                     │
24 │ Type: Consumable                                        │
25 └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

26

Purchase Flow:

1. User displays product list in game → Retrieve ProductPackageMaster info from backend API

2. Unity Addressables retrieves corresponding store product ID from ProductPackageMaster.id

3. User taps purchase button → Unity IAP processes purchase with store product ID

4. Store processes payment → Issues receipt

1179



5. Unity → Sends receipt and ProductPackageMaster.id to backend

6. Backend verifies receipt with store

7. Verification successful → Retrieves ProductComponent from ProductPackageMaster.id and grants items

Impact Scope When Deleting Data

❌ Records That Should Not Be Deleted

Deleting parent records will orphan child records:

Delete LocalizationLanguage  → LocalizationTranslation becomes invalid

Delete GameTicketMaster  → ProductMaster reference error (reference_master_id becomes invalid)

Delete ProductMaster  → ProductComponent reference error

Delete ProductPackageMaster  → Component, PriceEntry, Translation become orphaned + store

product correspondence breaks

Delete ProductPrice  → ProductPriceEntry becomes orphaned

Delete ProductPriceEntry  → ProductPriceChannel becomes orphaned

Special Attention:

GameTicketMaster is dynamically referenced by ProductMaster, so deletion invalidates the product master

ProductPackageMaster has a 1:1 correspondence with store products, so deletion causes errors during receipt

verification

Logical foreign keys (no database constraints) don't cause immediate errors upon deletion, but will cause runtime

errors

✅ Operations to Perform Instead

Deactivate instead of deleting:

GameTicketMaster.is_active = FALSE

ProductPackageMaster.is_active = FALSE  + Unpublish on store side

ProductPriceChannel.is_sellable = FALSE

Changes in Dependencies During Price Changes

Before Price Change (Old Version id=101)

1 [Backend]
2 ProductPackageMaster (id=101, is_active=FALSE)
3 ├── ProductComponent (id=1001)
4 │   └── ProductMaster (id=1) × 10
5 │       └── GameTicketMaster (id=1)
6 ├── ProductPriceEntry (id=3001: USD 99¢)
7 │   └── ProductPriceChannel (id=4001, is_sellable=FALSE)
8 └── LocalizationTranslation (id=1, 2, 3, 4)
9

10 [Unity Addressables]
11 package_id: 101
12 apple_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1"
13 google_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1"
14

15 [App Store/Google Play]
16 Product ID: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1 (Unpublished)
17 Price: $0.99

1180



18

After Price Change (New Version id=105)

1 [Backend]
2 ProductPackageMaster (id=105, is_active=TRUE)
3 ├── ProductComponent (id=1005)
4 │   └── ProductMaster (id=1) × 10  ← References same product
5 │       └── GameTicketMaster (id=1) ← References same ticket
6 ├── ProductPriceEntry (id=3009: USD 129¢)
7 │   └── ProductPriceChannel (id=4009, is_sellable=TRUE)
8 └── LocalizationTranslation (id=17, 18, 19, 20)  ← Newly created
9

10 [Unity Addressables]
11 package_id: 105
12 apple_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2"
13 google_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2"
14

15 [App Store/Google Play]
16 Product ID: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2 (Published)
17 Price: $1.29
18

Key Points:

GameTicketMaster is shared (top-level master data)

ProductMaster is shared (references same ticket)

ProductPackageMaster is different ID (different price + different store product)

Component is newly created (linked to different package)

PriceEntry is newly created (linked to different package)

Translation is newly created (linked to different package)

Create new mapping in Unity Addressables

Create new product ID in stores

Price Change Work Checklist (Including Store Integration)

Backend Side

[ ] Create new ProductPackageMaster (is_active=TRUE)

[ ] Deactivate old ProductPackageMaster (is_active=FALSE)

[ ] Create ProductComponent (for new version)

[ ] Create ProductPriceEntry (new prices)

[ ] Create ProductPriceChannel (new version: is_sellable=TRUE)

[ ] Update ProductPriceChannel (old version: is_sellable=FALSE)

[ ] Add LocalizationTranslation (for new version, both ja/en)

Unity Side

[ ] Add new mapping to Addressables (package_id=105 with new store product IDs)

[ ] Delete or deactivate old mapping

[ ] Build and test

App Store Connect Side

[ ] Create new product ID (com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2)

[ ] Set price ($1.29)

1181



[ ] Unpublish old product ID

[ ] Test in Sandbox environment

Google Play Console Side

[ ] Create new product ID (com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2)

[ ] Set price ($1.29)

[ ] Unpublish old product ID

[ ] Test in test track

FAQ

Q: Does ProductMaster need to be newly created when changing prices?

A: No. ProductMaster only defines products and doesn't contain price information.

Q: Should old ProductComponent be deleted?

1182



A: No. Purchase history may reference the old version.

Q: What happens if GameTicketMaster is deleted?

A: ProductMaster's reference_master_id becomes invalid, causing errors when retrieving product information.

Deactivate with is_active=FALSE instead of deleting.

Q: How is mapping information managed in Unity Addressables?

A: Typically, a mapping table of ProductPackageMaster.id and store product IDs is held in Addressables'

ScriptableObject or JSON configuration files. This configuration is updated during app updates to support new

products and price changes.

Q: Do Apple and Google need different product IDs?

A: Not mandatory, but must follow each store's naming conventions. Usually using the same ID (e.g.,

com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2) simplifies management. However, since Apple recommends reverse domain format, follow

each store's guidelines in actual operation.

Q: What does LocalizationTranslation's record_id point to?

A: It points to the primary key of the table specified in table_name.

table_name="product_package_master", record_id=105  → 

product_package_master.id=105

Q: Can one ProductPackageMaster contain multiple ProductMasters?

A: Yes. This can be achieved by creating multiple ProductComponent records.

1 Example: Starter Pack
2 - ProductComponent (package=201, product=1: Ticket × 10)
3 - ProductComponent (package=201, product=101: Club × 1)
4 - ProductComponent (package=201, product=201: Ball × 5)
5

Q: What if I want to change product contents without changing price?

A: Create a new ProductPackageMaster and set different ProductComponents. Even with the same price, separating

package_master_ids allows independent management of product composition. However, you must also create a new

product ID on the store side and set up a new mapping in Unity Addressables.

Q: How do I sell the same product on multiple sales channels (GAME, MKT)?

A: Create multiple ProductPriceChannel records for the same ProductPriceEntry.

1 ProductPriceEntry (id=3009: 10 Ticket Pack New Version USD 129¢)
2 ├── ProductPriceChannel (id=4009: channel=GAME, is_sellable=TRUE)
3 └── ProductPriceChannel (id=4010: channel=MKT, is_sellable=TRUE)
4

1183



Q: How does the API behave if translation data is insufficient?

A: When translation for a language is not found, the API returns default values (English or master table values) or

returns an error. Behavior varies by implementation, so always prepare translations for required languages (ja, en) for

all products.

Q: How to manage when reference_table expands in the future?

A: ProductMaster's reference_table field allows dynamic switching of reference destinations.

1 Example: Club product
2 ProductMaster (id=101)
3 category = "CLUB"
4 reference_table = "club_master"
5 reference_master_id = 5
6 ↓ References
7 ClubMaster (id=5: Driver Club)
8

This design eliminates the need to change table structure when adding new categories.

Q: How is ProductPackageMaster.id used during receipt verification?

A: Receipt verification flow:

1. Unity → Sends purchase receipt and ProductPackageMaster.id to backend

2. Backend verifies receipt with App Store/Google Play

3. Confirms receipt is valid

4. Retrieves items to grant from ProductComponent using ProductPackageMaster.id

5. Grants items to user

Since Unity Addressables links ProductPackageMaster.id and store product IDs, the backend doesn't need to

directly manage store product IDs.

概要

このドキュメントでは、各テーブルの親子関係、外部キー参照、データの依存関係を説明します。 これにより、デー
タ投入の順序や、レコード削除時の影響範囲が理解できます。

データ構造の全体像

1 ■ 独立マスター（Level 1）
2 │

3 ├─ LocalizationLanguage (言語マスター)
4 │   └─→ LocalizationTranslation に参照される
5 │

6 └─ GameTicketMaster (チケットマスター)
7 └─→ ProductMaster の reference_master_id に参照される
8

9 ■ 商品定義（Level 2）
10 │

11 └─ ProductMaster (商品マスター)
12 └─→ ProductComponent に参照される
13

14 ■ パッケージ定義（Level 3）
15 │

1184



16 └─ ProductPackageMaster (パッケージマスター) ★App Store/Google Playのプロ
ダクトと1:1対応

17 ├─→ ProductComponent に参照される
18 ├─→ ProductPriceEntry に参照される
19 └─→ LocalizationTranslation に参照される
20

21 ■ 価格管理（Level 4）
22 │

23 ├─ ProductPrice (価格ヘッダー)
24 │   └─→ ProductPriceEntry に参照される
25 │

26 └─ ProductPriceEntry (価格エントリ)
27 └─→ ProductPriceChannel に参照される
28

29 ■ 販売管理（Level 5）
30 │

31 └─ ProductPriceChannel (販売チャネル)
32

33 ■ 構成・翻訳（Level 4-5）
34 │

35 ├─ ProductComponent (商品構成)
36 │

37 └─ LocalizationTranslation (多言語翻訳)
38

親子関係の詳細

レベル1: マスターデータ（最上位・親）

これらのテーブルは他のテーブルに依存しない独立したマスターですが、子テーブルから参照されます。

1. LocalizationLanguage（言語マスター）

役割: 対応言語の定義

主キー: language_code （文字列）

子テーブル: LocalizationTranslation

依存関係: なし（完全独立）

参照元: LocalizationTranslation.language_code

データ投入順序: 最初

2. GameTicketMaster（チケットマスター）

役割: ゲーム内チケットの定義

主キー: id

子テーブル: ProductMaster

依存関係: なし（完全独立）

参照元: ProductMaster.reference_master_id（reference_table="game_ticket_master"の場合）

重要:

GameTicketMasterは独立したマスターテーブルですが、ProductMasterから動的に参照されます

ProductMasterの reference_table フィールドが"game_ticket_master"の場合、

reference_master_id がこのテーブルの id を指します

この参照は論理的な外部キーで、データベース制約ではなくアプリケーションレベルで管理されます

1185



参照の仕組み:

1 ProductMaster (id=1)
2 reference_table = "game_ticket_master"
3 reference_master_id = 1
4 ↓
5 GameTicketMaster (id=1: Regular Ticket)
6

データ投入順序: 最初

レベル2: 商品定義

3. ProductMaster（商品マスター）

役割: 販売可能な商品の定義

主キー: id

親テーブル:

GameTicketMaster（ reference_table  = "game_ticket_master"の場合）

将来的には他のマスターテーブルも参照可能（例: club_master, ball_master等）

子テーブル: ProductComponent

依存関係:

1 reference_table = "game_ticket_master" の場合
2 reference_master_id → game_ticket_master.id（論理的外部キー）
3

例:

1 ProductMaster (id=1)
2 product_code = "TICKET_REGULAR_001"
3 category = "TICKET"
4 reference_table = "game_ticket_master"
5 reference_master_id = 1
6 ↓ 参照
7 GameTicketMaster (id=1)
8 ticket_name = "Regular Ticket"
9 ticket_type = 1
10

重要ポイント:

reference_table と reference_master_id の組み合わせで、動的に異なるマスターテーブルを参照
できる

Phase 1では reference_table は"game_ticket_master"のみ

将来的には"club_master", "ball_master"等も追加可能

データ投入順序: GameTicketMasterの後

レベル3: パッケージ定義

4. ProductPackageMaster（商品パッケージマスター）

役割: 販売単位（バンドル）の定義

主キー: id

1186



親テーブル: なし（独立）

子テーブル:

ProductComponent

ProductPriceEntry

LocalizationTranslation

依存関係: なし

🔴 重要: ストアプロダクトとの1:1対応

ProductPackageMaster（1レコード）⇔ App Store/Google Playのストアプロダクト

という1:1の対応関係が存在します。この対応関係（マッピング）はUnity Addressablesで管理されます。

対応関係の仕組み:

1 [バックエンド]
2 ProductPackageMaster (id=105)
3 ↕ 1:1対応（Unity Addressablesで管理）
4 [App Store Connect]
5 Product: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
6 ↕ 同一商品
7 [Google Play Console]
8 Product: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
9

Unity Addressablesでの管理:

Addressablesの設定ファイルに、ProductPackageMaster.idとストアプロダクトIDのマッピング情報を保持

例: { "package_id": 105, "apple_product_id":

"com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2", "google_product_id":

"com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2" }

Unity側で購入処理時に適切なストアプロダクトIDを使用
レシート検証時にProductPackageMaster.idでバックエンドと連携

価格変更時の対応:

1 旧版:
2 - ProductPackageMaster (id=101, is_active=FALSE)
3 ↕ 対応
4 - App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1（非公開）
5 - Google Play: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1（非公開）
6

7 新版:
8 - ProductPackageMaster (id=105, is_active=TRUE)
9 ↕ 対応
10 - App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2（公開）
11 - Google Play: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2（公開）
12

重要ポイント:

1つのProductPackageMasterは1つのストアプロダクトに対応

価格変更時は新しいProductPackageMasterを作成 = 新しいストアプロダクトを作成
Unity Addressablesが両者の紐付けを管理するため、バックエンドは直接ストアプロダクトIDを保持する必要がない

データ投入順序: ProductMasterの後

1187



レベル4: パッケージ構成と価格

5. ProductComponent（商品構成）

役割: パッケージに含まれる商品と数量

主キー: id

親テーブル:

ProductPackageMaster  (product_package_master_id)

ProductMaster  (product_master_id)

依存関係:

1 product_package_master_id → product_package_master.id（外部キー）
2 product_master_id → product_master.id（外部キー）
3

例:

1 ProductComponent (id=1001)
2 product_package_master_id = 101
3 product_master_id = 1
4 quantity = 10
5 ↓ 参照
6 ProductPackageMaster (id=101: 10チケットパック)
7 ↓ Unity Addressablesで対応
8 App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1
9 ↓ 参照
10 ProductMaster (id=1: Regular Ticket)
11 ↓ 参照
12 GameTicketMaster (id=1: Regular Ticket)
13

データ投入順序: ProductPackageMasterとProductMasterの後

6. ProductPrice（価格ヘッダー）

役割: 価格設定の有効期間管理

主キー: id

親テーブル: なし（独立）

子テーブル: ProductPriceEntry

依存関係: なし

データ投入順序: いつでも可

7. ProductPriceEntry（価格エントリ）

役割: 具体的な通貨別価格

主キー: id

親テーブル:

ProductPrice  (product_price_id)

ProductPackageMaster  (product_package_master_id)

子テーブル: ProductPriceChannel

1188



依存関係:

1 product_price_id → product_price.id（外部キー）
2 product_package_master_id → product_package_master.id（外部キー）
3

例:

1 ProductPriceEntry (id=3009)
2 product_price_id = 2001
3 product_package_master_id = 105
4 currency_code = "USD"
5 amount = 129
6 ↓ 参照
7 ProductPrice (id=2001: 通常価格)
8 ↓ 参照
9 ProductPackageMaster (id=105: 10チケット新版)
10 ↓ Unity Addressablesで対応
11 App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
12

データ投入順序: ProductPriceとProductPackageMasterの後

8. ProductPriceChannel（価格チャネル）

役割: 販売チャネルごとの販売可否

主キー: id

親テーブル:

ProductPriceEntry  (product_price_entry_id)

依存関係:

1 product_price_entry_id → product_price_entry.id（外部キー）
2

例:

1 ProductPriceChannel (id=4009)
2 product_price_entry_id = 3009
3 channel = "GAME"
4 is_sellable = TRUE
5 ↓ 参照
6 ProductPriceEntry (id=3009: 10チケット新版 USD)
7

データ投入順序: ProductPriceEntryの後

9. LocalizationTranslation（多言語翻訳）

役割: 各テーブルの特定フィールドの翻訳

主キー: id

親テーブル:

LocalizationLanguage  (language_code)

動的参照: table_name  + record_id

依存関係:

1 language_code → localization_language.language_code（外部キー）

1189



2 (table_name, record_id) → 各テーブル.id（論理的外部キー）
3

例:

1 LocalizationTranslation (id=17)
2 language_code = "ja"
3 table_name = "product_package_master"
4 record_id = 105
5 field_name = "name"
6 translated_text = "10レギュラーチケットパック"
7 ↓ 参照
8 LocalizationLanguage (language_code="ja")
9 ↓ 参照
10 ProductPackageMaster (id=105)
11 ↓ Unity Addressablesで対応
12 App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
13

データ投入順序: 最後（翻訳対象テーブルの後）

データ投入の正しい順序

1 1. LocalizationLanguage（言語定義）
2 2. GameTicketMaster（チケット定義）
3 3. ProductMaster（商品定義）※GameTicketMasterを参照
4 4. ProductPackageMaster（パッケージ定義）
5 5. ProductComponent（パッケージ構成）
6 6. ProductPrice（価格期間）
7 7. ProductPriceEntry（具体的価格）
8 8. ProductPriceChannel（販売可否）
9 9. LocalizationTranslation（翻訳データ）
10

重要:

2 → 3の順序は必須: ProductMasterはGameTicketMaster.idを参照するため

1 → 9の順序は必須: LocalizationTranslationはLocalizationLanguage.language_codeを参照するため
4の前後: ProductPackageMasterとストアプロダクトの作成順序は問わない（Unity Addressablesで管理されるた
め）

重要な依存関係マップ

商品パッケージ（id=105）を中心とした関係図

1 ProductPackageMaster (id=105)
2 ↕ Unity Addressablesで管理
3 App Store: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
4 Google Play: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2
5 │

6 ├── ProductComponent (id=1005)
7 │   └── ProductMaster (id=1)
8 │       └── GameTicketMaster (id=1) ← reference_master_idで参照
9 │

10 ├── ProductPriceEntry (id=3009)
11 │   ├── ProductPrice (id=2001)
12 │   └── ProductPriceChannel (id=4009)
13 │

14 └── LocalizationTranslation (id=17, 18, 19, 20)
15 └── LocalizationLanguage (ja, en)
16

1190



ストアプロダクトとの対応関係

バックエンド ⇔ Unity ⇔ ストアの連携

1 ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

2 │ バックエンド (PostgreSQL)                                 │
3 ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤

4 │ ProductPackageMaster (id=105)                           │
5 │   is_active = TRUE                                      │
6 └────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────────┘

7 │ API経由で取得
8 ↓
9 ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

10 │ Unity Addressables                                      │
11 ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤

12 │ Mapping:                                                │
13 │   package_id: 105                                       │
14 │   apple_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2"      │
15 │   google_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2"     │
16 └────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────────┘

17 │ 購入リクエスト
18 ↓
19 ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

20 │ App Store Connect / Google Play Console                │
21 ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤

22 │ Product ID: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2                 │
23 │ Price: $1.29 / ¥160                                     │
24 │ Type: Consumable                                        │
25 └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

26

購入フロー:

1. ユーザーがゲーム内で商品一覧を表示 → バックエンドAPIからProductPackageMaster情報を取得
2. Unity AddressablesがProductPackageMaster.idから対応するストアプロダクトIDを取得
3. ユーザーが購入ボタンをタップ → Unity IAPがストアプロダクトIDで購入処理

4. ストアが決済処理 → レシートを発行
5. Unity → バックエンドにレシートとProductPackageMaster.idを送信

6. バックエンドがストアでレシート検証
7. 検証成功 → ProductPackageMaster.idからProductComponentを取得して商品付与

データ削除時の影響範囲

❌ 削除してはいけないレコード

親レコードを削除すると、子レコードが孤立します:

LocalizationLanguage  を削除 → LocalizationTranslationが無効化

GameTicketMaster  を削除 → ProductMasterが参照エラー（reference_master_idが無効になる）

ProductMaster  を削除 → ProductComponentが参照エラー

ProductPackageMaster  を削除 → Component, PriceEntry, Translationが孤立 + ストアプロダクトとの対

応が崩れる

ProductPrice  を削除 → ProductPriceEntryが孤立

ProductPriceEntry  を削除 → ProductPriceChannelが孤立

特に注意:

GameTicketMasterはProductMasterから動的に参照されているため、削除すると商品マスターが無効になります

1191



ProductPackageMasterはストアプロダクトと1:1対応しているため、削除するとレシート検証時にエラーが発生し

ます

論理的外部キー（データベース制約なし）のため、削除しても即座にエラーにはなりませんが、アプリケーション
実行時にエラーが発生します

✅ 代わりに行うべき操作

削除の代わりに非アクティブ化:

GameTicketMaster.is_active = FALSE

ProductPackageMaster.is_active = FALSE  + ストア側で非公開に設定

ProductPriceChannel.is_sellable = FALSE

価格変更時の依存関係の変化

価格変更前（旧版 id=101）

1 [バックエンド]
2 ProductPackageMaster (id=101, is_active=FALSE)
3 ├── ProductComponent (id=1001)
4 │   └── ProductMaster (id=1) × 10
5 │       └── GameTicketMaster (id=1)
6 ├── ProductPriceEntry (id=3001: USD 99¢)
7 │   └── ProductPriceChannel (id=4001, is_sellable=FALSE)
8 └── LocalizationTranslation (id=1, 2, 3, 4)
9

10 [Unity Addressables]
11 package_id: 101
12 apple_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1"
13 google_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1"
14

15 [App Store/Google Play]
16 Product ID: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v1（非公開）
17 Price: $0.99
18

価格変更後（新版 id=105）

1 [バックエンド]
2 ProductPackageMaster (id=105, is_active=TRUE)
3 ├── ProductComponent (id=1005)
4 │   └── ProductMaster (id=1) × 10  ← 同じ商品を参照
5 │       └── GameTicketMaster (id=1) ← 同じチケットを参照
6 ├── ProductPriceEntry (id=3009: USD 129¢)
7 │   └── ProductPriceChannel (id=4009, is_sellable=TRUE)
8 └── LocalizationTranslation (id=17, 18, 19, 20)  ← 新規作成
9

10 [Unity Addressables]
11 package_id: 105
12 apple_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2"
13 google_product_id: "com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2"
14

15 [App Store/Google Play]
16 Product ID: com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2（公開）
17 Price: $1.29
18

ポイント:

GameTicketMasterは共有（最上位のマスターデータ）

ProductMasterは共有（同じチケットを参照）
ProductPackageMasterは別ID（価格が違うため + ストアプロダクトも別）

1192



Componentは新規作成（別packageに紐づくため）
PriceEntryは新規作成（別packageに紐づくため）

Translationは新規作成（別packageに紐づくため）
Unity Addressablesで新しいマッピングを作成

ストアで新しいプロダクトIDを作成

価格変更時の作業チェックリスト（ストア連携含む）

バックエンド側

[ ] 新しいProductPackageMaster作成（is_active=TRUE）
[ ] 旧ProductPackageMaster非アクティブ化（is_active=FALSE）

[ ] ProductComponent作成（新版用）
[ ] ProductPriceEntry作成（新価格）

[ ] ProductPriceChannel作成（新版: is_sellable=TRUE）
[ ] ProductPriceChannel更新（旧版: is_sellable=FALSE）
[ ] LocalizationTranslation追加（新版用、ja/en両方）

Unity側

[ ] Addressablesに新しいマッピング追加（package_id=105と新ストアプロダクトID）
[ ] 旧マッピングを削除または非アクティブ化
[ ] ビルドしてテスト

App Store Connect側

[ ] 新しいプロダクトID作成（com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2）
[ ] 価格設定（$1.29）
[ ] 旧プロダクトIDを非公開に設定

[ ] Sandbox環境でテスト

FAQ

Q: ProductMasterは価格変更時に新規作成が必要？

A: 不要。ProductMasterは商品の定義のみで、価格情報は含まれない。

Q: 旧版のProductComponentは削除すべき？

A: 削除しない。購入履歴が旧版を参照している可能性があるため。

Q: GameTicketMasterを削除したらどうなる？

A: ProductMasterのreference_master_idが無効になり、商品情報の取得時にエラーが発生します。削除せず、
is_active=FALSEで非アクティブ化してください。

Q: Unity Addressablesでマッピング情報はどのように管理される？

A: 通常、AddressablesのScriptableObjectやJSON設定ファイルに、ProductPackageMaster.idとストアプロダクトID
のマッピングテーブルを保持します。アプリ更新時にこの設定も更新することで、新しい商品や価格変更に対応しま

1194



す。

Q: AppleとGoogleで異なるプロダクトIDを使う必要がある？

A: 必須ではありませんが、各ストアの命名規則に従う必要があります。通常は同じID（例:

com.golfin.ticket.10pack.v2）を使用することで管理を簡素化できます。ただし、Appleは逆ドメイン形式を推奨するた
め、実際の運用では各ストアのガイドラインに従ってください。

Q: LocalizationTranslationのrecord_idは何を指す？

A: table_nameで指定したテーブルの主キーを指します。

table_name="product_package_master", record_id=105  → 

product_package_master.id=105

Q: 1つのProductPackageMasterに複数のProductMasterを含められる？

A: はい。ProductComponentで複数のレコードを作成することで実現できます。

1 例: スターターパック
2 - ProductComponent (package=201, product=1: チケット × 10)
3 - ProductComponent (package=201, product=101: クラブ × 1)
4 - ProductComponent (package=201, product=201: ボール × 5)
5

Q: 価格を変更せずに、商品内容だけを変更したい場合は？

A: 新しいProductPackageMasterを作成し、異なるProductComponentを設定します。価格が同じでも、
package_master_idを分けることで商品構成を独立管理できます。ただし、ストア側でも新しいプロダクトIDを作成

し、Unity Addressablesで新しいマッピングを設定する必要があります。

Q: 同じ商品を複数の販売チャネル（GAME, MKT）で販売する場合は？

A: 同じProductPriceEntryに対して、複数のProductPriceChannelレコードを作成します。

1 ProductPriceEntry (id=3009: 10チケット新版 USD 129¢)
2 ├── ProductPriceChannel (id=4009: channel=GAME, is_sellable=TRUE)
3 └── ProductPriceChannel (id=4010: channel=MKT, is_sellable=TRUE)
4

Q: 翻訳データが不足している場合、APIはどう動作する？

A: APIは該当言語の翻訳が見つからない場合、デフォルト値（英語またはマスターテーブルの値）を返すか、エラーを
返します。実装によって動作が異なるため、全商品に対して必須言語（ja, en）の翻訳を必ず用意してください。

Q: reference_tableが将来的に増えた場合、どう管理する？

A: ProductMasterのreference_tableフィールドで動的に参照先を切り替えられます。

1 例: クラブ商品の場合
2 ProductMaster (id=101)

1195



3 category = "CLUB"
4 reference_table = "club_master"
5 reference_master_id = 5
6 ↓ 参照
7 ClubMaster (id=5: Driver Club)
8

この設計により、新しいカテゴリの追加時にテーブル構造を変更する必要がありません。

Q: レシート検証時にProductPackageMaster.idはどう使われる？

A: レシート検証の流れ：

1. Unity → バックエンドに購入レシートとProductPackageMaster.idを送信
2. バックエンドがApp Store/Google Playでレシート検証

3. レシートが有効であることを確認
4. ProductPackageMaster.idを元にProductComponentから付与する商品を取得

5. ユーザーに商品付与

Unity AddressablesがProductPackageMaster.idとストアプロダクトIDを紐付けるため、バックエンドは直接ストア

プロダクトIDを管理する必要がありません。

1196



Price Change Procedure

Why Use a Different package_master_id?

In this design, price changes = creating a new product package.

Main Reasons:

1. Handling App Store Price Change Time Lag

When you change prices in App Store Connect, actual reflection takes time

During this period, users can still purchase at the old price

By using separate IDs on the backend, you can control sales reliably regardless of store reflection status

2. Preventing Unintended Price Sales

Old version: is_active=FALSE  → Absolutely cannot be sold

New version: is_active=TRUE  → Only this version is sold for sure

Clear control via price_validation API

3. Data Structure Constraints

In the current design, sales period management is tied to product_package_master_id

ProductPriceEntry  consists of product_package_master_id  + price + effective period

Managing multiple price periods with the same ID makes determining "which price is valid" complex

Using separate IDs allows price_validation API to simply check "is_active or not"

Price Change Procedure

Example: Raising the price of 10 Ticket Pack from $0.99 to $1.29

Step 1: Create New ProductPackageMaster

1 id=105, product_code=PKG_TICKET_10_V2, is_active=TRUE
2

Step 2: Deactivate Old Version

1 id=101, product_code=PKG_TICKET_10_V1, is_active=FALSE
2

Step 3: Create ProductComponent

1 For new version (id=105), link 10 units of product master (id=1)
2

Step 4: Create ProductPriceEntry

1 For new version (id=105), set prices: USD: 129 cents, JPY: 160 yen
2

Step 5: Update ProductPriceChannel

1 Old version price channel: is_sellable=FALSE
2 New version price channel: is_sellable=TRUE
3

Step 6: Add LocalizationTranslation

1197



1 For new version (id=105), add Japanese and English names and
descriptions

2

Price Change Checklist

[ ] Create new ProductPackageMaster (is_active=TRUE)

[ ] Deactivate old ProductPackageMaster (is_active=FALSE)

[ ] Create ProductComponent (for new version)

[ ] Create ProductPriceEntry (new prices)

[ ] Create ProductPriceChannel (new version: is_sellable=TRUE)

[ ] Update ProductPriceChannel (old version: is_sellable=FALSE)

[ ] Add LocalizationTranslation (for new version, both ja/en)

[ ] Update Unity product ID settings

なぜ別のpackage_master_idを使うのか？

この設計では、価格変更 = 新しい商品パッケージの作成として扱います。

主な理由:

1. App Storeの価格変更タイムラグ対応

App Store Connectで価格を変更しても、実際の反映に時間がかかることがある
その間、ユーザーは旧価格で購入できてしまう

バックエンドで別IDを使うことで、ストアの反映状況に関係なく確実に販売を制御できる
2. 意図しない価格での販売を防止

旧版: is_active=FALSE  → 絶対に販売されない

新版: is_active=TRUE  → 確実にこれだけが販売される

price_validation APIで明確に制御可能
3. データ構造の制約

現在の設計では、販売期間の管理が product_package_master_id  に紐づいている

ProductPriceEntry  は product_package_master_id  + 価格 + 有効期間で構成される

同じIDで複数の価格期間を管理すると、「どちらの価格が有効か」の判断が複雑になる
別IDにすることで、price_validation APIがシンプルに「is_activeかどうか」だけをチェックできる

価格変更の手順

例: 10チケットパックを$0.99から$1.29に値上げする場合

ステップ1: 新しいProductPackageMasterを作成

1 id=105, product_code=PKG_TICKET_10_V2, is_active=TRUE
2

ステップ2: 旧版を非アクティブ化

1 id=101, product_code=PKG_TICKET_10_V1, is_active=FALSE

1198



2

ステップ3: ProductComponentを作成

1 新版(id=105)に対して、商品マスター(id=1)を10個紐付け
2

ステップ4: ProductPriceEntryを作成

1 新版(id=105)に対して、USD: 129セント、JPY: 160円の価格を設定
2

ステップ5: ProductPriceChannelを更新

1 旧版の価格チャネル: is_sellable=FALSE
2 新版の価格チャネル: is_sellable=TRUE
3

ステップ6: LocalizationTranslationを追加

1 新版(id=105)に対して、日本語・英語の名前と説明を追加
2

価格変更のチェックリスト

[ ] 新しいProductPackageMaster作成（is_active=TRUE）
[ ] 旧ProductPackageMaster非アクティブ化（is_active=FALSE）

[ ] ProductComponent作成（新版用）
[ ] ProductPriceEntry作成（新価格）
[ ] ProductPriceChannel作成（新版: is_sellable=TRUE）

[ ] ProductPriceChannel更新（旧版: is_sellable=FALSE）
[ ] LocalizationTranslation追加（新版用、ja/en両方）
[ ] Unity側のプロダクトID設定更新

Design Implementation Guidelines: Do's & Don'ts (From A Developer's
Perspective)
This document outlines common design patterns that are easy to mock up but can be

challenging to implement in code. It’s meant to help designers avoid pitfalls and create

developer-friendly designs without sacrificing creativity.

✅ Do's: Design with Implementation in Mind

Design Practice Why It Helps

Design with real content and edge cases (long Prevents layout breaks and unexpected

names, error states, etc.) overflow

Consider mobile-first or responsive behavior Avoids major refactoring later

from the start

Include clear specifications for breakpoints Reduces guesswork

Provide fallback states (loading, empty, error) Improves UX and simplifies logic

Prioritize SVG use instead of images Better performance for browsers (faster load

times)

Collaborate early and proactively with Saves time by avoiding having to redesign or

developers to validate feasibility reimplement problematic elements later

🚫 Don'ts: Easy in Design, Hard in Code

Design Element Why It's Tricky

Overlapping elements with dynamic content Fragile and prone to layout shifts

Custom scrollbars or scroll-based animations. Browser inconsistencies and performance

Overly complex animations with a lot of issues

elements

Complex gradients, shadows, or blend modes May not render consistently across platforms

or browsers. Can cause performance issues

(slower page loading time)

1200



Sticky headers with dynamic height/content Can cause layout jumps and performance hits

Mega menus or nested dropdowns with Requires intricate event handling and

animations accessibility logic

Hover effects as primary interaction Doesn’t translate to mobile UX

🧠 Tips for Designers

Think in terms of states: loading, empty, error, success.

Ask: “How would this behave on a phone?”

Collaborate early with developers to validate feasibility

This “Do’s and Don’ts” list is not the “law” by any means. In other words, there will always be

exceptions to all of these things and situations where having them (or not having them) will

make sense. The idea though is to have these things in mind while designing, and, the most

important part being to collaborate early and proactively with developers. 

There will very likely be things both sides will need to compromise on, but active communication

will save a lot of time for both sides. Developers can give feedback on what may/may not work

or be ideal, offer alternative solutions, etc. and designers can ask why, push back, offer their

own alternative solutions, etc
